  
Isingeniso 
"Nondaba! Ngeke umoya wami uphumule kungekho i'manuscript' yakho lapha etafuleni lami." 
  La mazwi yiwona azala Ie ncwadi. A yeshiwo umlobi odumile uProfesa c.L.S. Nyembezi ewaqondise kimi ngocingo ngisebenza eYunivesithi yakwaZulu ngo-1981. Njengothisha wami engangimhlonipha kakhulu ngamtshela ukuthi uzoyithola maduzane. Umqondo walolu hlobo Iwencwadi ngase nginawo njengomuntu owayesebenza emtapweni wolwazi futhi nowayebona ukuthi ulimi Iwakithi alunalo lolu hlobo. Ngakhuthazwa imibono yabantu abanjengoProf. Absolom Vilakazi, Prof. K. Mngoma, Prof. Otty Nxumalo, abanurnzane N.F. Mbhele, RT. Wela, A. Hlengwa noDr. M.v. Gumede engangithi uma ngikhuluma ngalo msebenzi bakhiphe neyabo imibono.

Injongo Yale Ncwadi 
Ukulobela abafundi besiZulu inewadi yamagalelo abantu bakithi emikhakheni eyahlukene empilweni yase-Afrika. Futhi ngiyiqondise kubantu bakithi abafunda ezikoleni zabadala ukuba bangalibali ukufunda izinewadi zezingane ezinezinganekwane. Le newadi ihlose futhi ukubekela umphakathi wakithi izimpilo zabaholi: ukuzalwa, ukukhula, ukufunda, ubunzima, ukubekezela nokuzinikela kwabo ekufinyeleleni emaqophelweni ehlukene, kanye nokukhuthaza abalobi, ikakhulukazi abomlando wakithi, ukuba bacubungule izimpilo namagalelo aboMdabu ekwakheni iSouth Africa entsha kwezomlando. Okokugcina ukubekela intsha yonke yase-Afrika imisebenzi yabantu bakithi ekade ifihliwe ezinewadini ezilotshwe abezizwe ngathi, ikakhulu lezo ebezisetshenziswa ezikoleni. 

   
Okuqukefhwe Yile Ncwadi 
Incwadi yokuqala iqukethe izikhathi: 1700-1800-1900 okwazalwa ngazo abaholi okulotshwe ngabo. Abaningi abaholi okulotshwe ngabo abaseNingizimu Afrika ngoba ibhuku belingesinda kakhulu uma befakwa ngokufanayo abamanye amazwe aseAfrika. Le ncwadi ayibehlukanisanga abaholi ngemikhakha yenkolo, umbusazwe, imfundo, ezomphakathi njalo njalo. Lokhu kwenziwe ngoba abaningi abaholi bagxila emikhakheni eminingi umuntu emunye njengoDr ].L. Dube nabanye. Yikho nje ngibone ukuthi ngibehlukanise ngezikhathi zokuzalwa kwabo. Lapha kubhalwe ngabaholi abangasekho emhlabeni. lbhuku elilandelayo liyosibekela abaholi abasaphila eNingizimu Afrika. 


   
Inhlalo Vase-Afrika Bengakafiki Abelungu 
Ukuze kuzwakale kahle imisebenzi ebalulekile yezingwazi zakithi e-Afrika kufanele kulotshwe lapha ukuthi kwakuphilwa kanjani bengakafiki abelungu. Kuzoshiwo futhi ukuthi bona babenjani kwelakubo nokuthi yini eyabaletha e-Afrika. Noma zingebalwe zonke izingwazi zangasenhla noMzansi Afrika lezi ezimbalwa okulotshwe ngazo zizokhombisa ukuthuthuka kwamazwe ase-Afrika. 
  Izwe laseYurophu lalifana nelase-Afrika ngokuthi nakhona kwakunezizwana ezincane (tribes) ezaziphila impilo eyahlukene. Lezi zizwana zazikhonza izithombe futhi zivarnise ukulwa zodwa ngoba impilo yazo yabe ingahlelekile njengoba siyibona namhlanje. Ezinye ezibalwayo emlandweni yilezi: Angles, Saxons, Huns, Ostrogoths, Visigoths, Franks. 
  Ukuze kudaleke izwe laseNgilandi kwadingeka ukuba kuhlangane arna-Angles namaSaxons kwakhulunywa isiNgisi sokuqala okwathiwa iAnglo-Saxon. Zaya ngokuhlangana lezi zizwana zayeka ukuzula zazinza ezindaweni ezahlukene. Kanjena-ke kwadaleka amazwe aseYurophu njengoFrance. Izizwana lezi zaqala ukuba nabaholi, namakhosi nernithetho. Namhlanje sesizwa ngoJalimane  kanti kwaba ukuhlangana kwalezi zizwana. 
  Izizwe zala mazwe zagcina sezithintene nezwe lase-Afrika kwaqopheka umlando ongasoze wakhohlakala. Nakwelakithi eAfrika zazikhona izizwana ezincane ezagcina sezihlangene kwadaleka irnibuso yakoNigeria, Zaire, Xhosa, Zulu, Swazi njalo njalo. Ngesikhathi uShaka ehlasela izizwe zoMzansi Afrika nangasenhla wayeqonde ukuba kube khona urnbuso owodwa wabamnyama njengoba namhlanje sizwa ngernibuso yakoUnited States, Britain, Russia nerninye. Abalobi abaningi abamhlophe nabanye bomdabu baye bathi uShaka wayehlasela ngoba ethanda ukuchitha igazi. Igazi alichithekanga yini kubunjwa i-U.S.A. neminye irnibuso ngoba phela yayingekho

Amazwi Om/obi 
Azikabi ningi ngokwanele izincwadi ezilotshwe ngesiZulu uma uziqhathanisa nesiNgisi nesiBhunu. Imvamisa yizincwadi ezilotshelwe abafundi ezikoleni. Vma lukhona uhIobo Iwezincwadi ezinika umIando ngezingwazi zakithi eMzansi Afrika nakuyo yonke i-Afrika mhIawumbe zingeke zifike esihlanwini. Kodwa uthi uma ubheka ohlangothini Iwakwezinye izizwe ufice ukuthi lolu hlobo cisho yilona oluningi kakhulu. 
  Ubuneane balolu hlobo Iwezincwadi lube nemiphumela engathuthukisi. Eziningi izingwazi ziyakhohlakala ngoba azikho emabhukwini alotshwe abamhlophe ngoba bengabazi noma bengabathandi. Ngakho-ke lezi zingwazi azikacwaningwa ngokwanele ukuze kuphumele obala imisebenzi yazoo Lokhu kuba sengathi thina asizange sayibeka induku ebandla ngokuba nezingwazi kwezempi, kwezombusazwe, kwezemfundo, kwezempilo, kwezenkolo, kwezomnotho, kwezabalobi, kwezababusi, njalo njalo. Abafundi ezikoleni zakithi bangakutshela kangeono ngoJan van Riebeeek kunoSobukwe, noLuthuli noAnton Lembede. Yingoba ekufundeni kwabo abahlangani nalezi zingwazi ngokujulile njengo van Riebeeek. ' 
  Izincwadi ngempilo yomuntu ziyayithinta impilo yomunye umuntu kwesinye isikhathi iguquke. Iqhawe liyakwenza ukuthi omunye athi 'mina ngifuna ukuba njengobani' esho iqhawe lelo. Ngingajabula uma Ie ncwadi nezinye ezizoyilandela ziyophumelela ekwandiseni ulwazi kumphakathi wakithi ngezingwazi zakithl.

bayothola" enye yezincwadi engafundwa usalJlabe ikhefu. Abalobi ahanhlobonhlobo bayocosha benabe ekulobeni imidIalo nokunye. Abacwaningi bemfundo ephakeme' bayocwaninga kabanzi bavumbulule okuningi okungaphumelelanga ukukhishwa kuleli bhuku nokulungisa amaphutha akhona kwezinye izincwadi. 




14. 

  Ngizwakalisa ukubonga okukhulu kuProf. Sibusiso Nyembezi owake wangifundisa esenguthisha. Ngangingazange ngacabanga ukuthi ngingake ngilobe incwadi. Vcingo lwakhe lwafika kimi wathi, "Nondaba, ngeke ngithokoze uma ngingenakho okulotshwe uwe phezu kwetafula lami." Ngokumhlonipha nangendlela akhuluma ngayo ngalala ngiphenduka. Emveni kokuba sengikhethile ukuthi ngizobhala lolu hlobo lwencwadi ngahlala phezu kosiba ngaloba. Ngibonga isineke sakhe sokulungisa amaphutha emfundamakhwela. 

  Angibonge futhi uO.E.H. Nxumalo owayelokhu evuselela umoya wami uma esebona ukuthi ushona phansi. Vme njalo Mkhatshwa nomoya wentuthuko. Ngeke ngikhohlwe abanye abakhuthazi njengoProf. Absolom Vilakazi, Prof. Khabi Mngoma noProf. Elkin Sithole ephesheya kwezilwandle. 

  Ngabe ngiyaphosisa uma ngishiya ekubongeni isigungu seNqolobane Yamagugu akwaZulu esasixoxa ngalolu hlobo lwencwadi ukuthi ingabe iyikho yini ukubeka itshe esivivaneni. Kini nonke ngithi: "unwele olude!" 

  Ngibonga ubaba umfundisi uD.D. Zondi ngokungikhuthaza abuye angicobelele nokunye ayekucosha kwabaziyo. Ngibonge futhi ibandla lakithi eDivali ngokuba nesineke ekulaleleni izinkulumo ebengizenza ngezinye zalezi zingwazi. 

  "Izingwazi Zase-Afrika" yibhuku elizama ukulandela izingwazi eMzansi Afrika, enhla ne-Afrika naphesheya. Siyazi ukuthi kunabantu bakithi abathunjwa bayiswa emazweni aphesheya. Abaningi babo bafike baqopha umlando. Ngoba umsuka wabo ulapha ngibone ukuthi ngeke sibashiye ngaphandle. 


  
umuzi awunikezwa uShaka uMkabayi wawuseMahlabathini. 
  Okunye okwenza ukuba uShaka akhombise ukurnethemba uMkabayi yilokhu: VShaka wathatha indodana yenkosi yesizwe sabeSuthu amaPhuthini (Puting) wayinikeza uMkabayi ukuba ayikhulise. Lesi sizwe singezinye ezizweni ezanqotshwa uShaka wasesingenisa embusweni wakwaZulu. Yakhula indodana yale nkosi nabantu bakayise ababehlala esigoclini saseNquthu. Kuhambe kwahamba abakwaPhuthini bahlangana namaZulu baganiselana. K wagcina sekukhona izibongo zesiZulu ezixubile, abanye kuyisizukulwane senkosana yenkosi eyakhuliswa uMkabayi. 
  Akukho okwakwenziwa inkosi ebusayo okungazange kwabikwa kwinkosazana uMkabayi. Naye wayenikezwa ithuba lokuba akhiphe owakhe umbono. Kwakuthi lapho impi iphurna ihamba iyohlasela, amabutho aqale edlule eMahlabathini nasebaQuiusini ukuyothatha izibusiso zethongo. Yayinele ifike impi uMkabayi agqokise okwesilisa bese efaka urnqubule ekhanda. Wayephatha urnkhonto nehawu ahambe phakathi kornkhurnbi owawuvarnise ukuba rnkhulu. Kwakuthula kuthi cwaka ngenkathi ehamba phakathi kornkhurnbi, negwala lizizwe selithola arnandla nokuzinikela.

Arnabutho kaMkabayi ayedurne ngobuqhawe nokungesabi; izinto ezazikhonzwe inkosi uShaka. Wonke amadodana kaSenzangakhona ayernhlonipha edane eya kuye ukuyothola izeluleko. UMkabayi wayethi urna ebona inkosi uShaka ebona ubuqotho nernisebenzi yakhe, abone ukuvuka kombuso wokhokho asebadlula.

  Empini eyaba khona phakathi kwabakwaZulu nabakwaButhelezi (ngaphansi kuka Phungashe) uZulu wehiulwa wathunjwa uSenzangakhona waze wakhululwa sekukhokhwe

izinkomo ezingamashumi ayisithupha. Lesi sigameko salandelwa esokuthi uSenzangakhona wabesethola umakoti kwaButhelezi kwavela ubuhlobo noPhungashe. 

  UMkabi wayenendodakazi uNdikidi eyabuye yaziwa ngelikaNozinhlanga. Ngenkathi kufika abelungu enkosini uShaka wayekhona uMkabi noma sekuxoxwa nenkosi. Phela uShaka wayernkhonzile uMkabi. 

  UMkabi wafa ngendlela engajwayelekile. Sekushiwo ukuthi uMkabi waphila isikhathi eside. Waze wafa sekubusa inkosi uCetshwayo. Enyangeni kaJuly zizine impi yamaNgisi yahlasela kwaZulu. Kuthiwa izinduna zabalekisa abesifazane nezingane bayocashiswa ukuze bangalimali uma seyibambana ernzini wenkosi. UMkabi wenqaba ukuyocasha esho nokushb ukuthi usephile isikhathi eside ezibona izimpi. Wathi kungcono afe ngoba inkosi uCetshwayo ihlaselwa nje ayenze lutho. Kuthiwa indlovukazi yathatha ummese yazinquma uqhoqhoqho yafa khona lapho. Yayidume ngokuphatha kahle yonke imizi yamakhosi kusukela kuJama. Yayibazisa abantu benkosi kanti nabo babeyazisa njengonina wesizwe. 

  Ukuze kubonakale kahle isikhundla sendlovukazi uMkabi kuzonikezwa ambalwa amakhosikazi enkosi uSenzangakhona. Nanka-ke: 

Indlovukazi enkulu yokuqala uMkabi unina womntwana uNozinhlanga. Waze wakhothama eyindlovukazi. 

Eyesibili uFudukazi owafa engenabantwana. Eyesithathu uNandi owazala inkosi uShaka kanye nendodakazi uNomcuba. Esehlukene noSenzangakhona wathola indodana uNgwadi kwenye indoda. 

Eyesine uLangazana owafa eneminyaka elinganiselwa ku-118. Wathola indodana uMagwaza owafa empini ka-1838 kuliwa namaBhunu. 

Eyesihlanu uMzondwase unina kaMhlangana. Eyesithupha uMpikase unina wenkosi uDingane. Eyesikhombisa uMagulana, owathola intombazane. Eyesishiyagalombili uBhibhi Ntuli unina kaSigujana.

Nandi 1764 - 1827 
"Umendo awuthunyelwa gundane kanti futhi ikusasa alaziwa." 
Empilweni yakhe uNandi wabelwa ubumnandi bokukhuJa njengezingane zesikhathi sakhe; wabelwa ubuntombi njengezintombi zesikhathi sakhe; wabelwa ukuqoma njengezintombi zesikhathi sakhe; wabelwa ukukhuJelwa kungavumeki ngokwesiko njengezinye izintombi zesikhathi sakhe; wabelwa umendo njengabanye ozakwabo; wabelwa ubunzima emendweni kwaze kwafika isikhathi sokuba ashiye umuzi wakhe ahambe edinga efuna indawo yokuhlala. Wabuzwa ubunzima obuthwalwa abaningi besifazane ngisho nanamuhla. Ekugcineni wabelwa umvuzo wokubekezela. ekufuneni inhlalakahle yakhe nengane yakhe uShaka. Ngokufushane singathi impilo yakhe yaba impilo abedluJa kuyo abaningi besifazane. 
  Akesizwe ngalo Nandi owayekhonzwe kangaka inkosi uShaka. Wayeyindodakazi yenkosi uBhebhe yaseLangeni. KuJinganiselwa ukuthi wazalwa ngo-1764 elllZini wasoBongeni kwaZuJu esigoclini saseMelmoth ngokwanamuhla. 
Unina kwakunguMfunda indodakazi yenkosi uQwabe. 
WakhuJa njengawo wonke amantombazane waze wangena ebuntombini. Ezingxoxweni zabo beyizintombi kwaphatheka igama lomNtwana uSenzangakhona. UNandi wafikelwa ukuyibona Ie nsizwa eyayibatshazwa ngobuhle. 
  Nembala Iwaze lwafika usuku olungaliyo babonana kwase kokheleka umlilo wothando olwaba nomphumela omkhuJu emlandweni wakwaZuJu. Emva kwesikhathi kwezwakala ukuthi uNandi akaphilile usekhuJelwe. Wagcina esendele kuSenzangakhona uNandi waba inkosikazi yesithathu 
10 
kuSenzangakhona. UNandi wezwana kakhuJu noMkabi, enye yamakhosikazi kaSenzangakhona. Nendodana kaNandi, uShaka, wakhuJa emthanda uMkabi. UNandi wahlala noMkabi emzini eSiklebheni iminyaka embalwa waze welamanisa ngendodakazi uNomcuba. 
  Kuthiwa uNandi wayenolaka eshesha ukuzwela uma kwenziwa amancoko. Abanye babona ukuthi lokhu kudalwa yinhlalo yakhe eyayingemnandi. Kwakude kuhletshwa ngaye kubuye kugigiyelwe ngaye ngoba wenda esekhuJelwe. Nengane yakhe uShaka yaba nesidina ngisho nakwezinye izingane. Wayeshayeka masishane uShaka abuye abizwe ngamaganyana angasile agudliselwa ekuzalweni kwakhe. 
  Le nhIalo yenza ukuthi uNandi abe nenhliziyo elukhuni, kwathi nendodana yakhe yafunda ukuzivikela kowabo. USenzangakhona waba nothando olunciphayo kuNandi ngenxa yalolu laka. Kwaze kwaba indaba ezekwayo lena. 
  NgobuJukhuni benhlalo yakhe nomntanakhe, uNandi wathatha imithwalo yakhe wahamba wayohlala nezihlobo eLangeni. Nalapha futhi inhlalo yabanzima, ikakhuJukazi ekaShaka. lzingane zezihlobo zamphatha kabi. Unina wahlala umoya wakhe uJokhu ungeneme engazi ukuthi uzokwenzenjani. 
  Ngo-1802 kwavela indlala enkulu eyaziwa ngelokuthi u"Madlantule" eyabanga ukuthi athuthe uNandi nabantabakhe bayofuna indawo engcono. 
  Baqonda esizweni saseMbendweni emlonyeni womfula iMatikuJu. Ngesikhathi ekhonze lapha uNandi wagana uGendeyana wathola indodana uNgwadi. Isizwe saseMbendweni sasiphansi kwenkosi uPhakathwayo. 
  UNandi akahlalanga isikhathi eside lapha ngoba ebona ukuthi indodana yakhe uShaka yayingenaso isikhundla esicacile kuJe ndawo. 
  Ngo-1803 wathutha uNandi wahamba wayohlala nodadewabo kayise esizweni sakwaMthethwa, esasiphansi kwenkosi uDingiswayo. Umoya kaNandi waqala ukukhuJuJeka lapho ebona indodana yakhe idlala ngokukhuJuJeka. UShaka wakhombisa ubuqhawe wazenzela ugazi ngisho nasenkosini uDingiswayo. 
II 


 

  Inkosi uSenzangakhona yavakashela inkosi uDingiswayo ikhuthazwa udadewabo uMkabayi. Wafike wathatheka kakhulu ukusina kukaShaka nobuqhawe bakhe ngokuxoxelwa inkosi uDingiswayo. Akuphelanga sikhathi esingakanani ebuyele ekhaya uSenzangakhona washona ngo-1816. UShaka wathatha ubukhosi bakwaZulu emveni kokuba kade kubambe inkosazana uMkabayi. UMkabayi wamamukela ngokuthokoza uShaka ebukhosini bakwaZulu. Naye uNandi wemukelwa kahle njengonina wenkosi. 

  UNandi wahlala kwaBulawayo ernzini omkhulu wenkosi uShaka. Emva kwesikhashana wamakhela owakhe umuzi eMkhindini eyayiphakathi kwemifudlana iMateku neMbuzane. Wahlala kulo muzi isikhathi eside waze wahlatshwa isifo okuthiwa esohudo esamthatha ngo-October 1827. 
Ukufa kukaNandi kwayiphatha kabi kakhulu inkosi uShaka. 

Nakhu phela yayihlala njalo ikhumbula ukuthi unina wayikhusela ezikhathini ezinzima zokukhula kwayo akazange ayilahle. Kuthiwa abantu ababeso!wa ukuthi balila ngaliso linye babebulawa. UNandi wangcwatshwa endlini afela kuyo. Unmyango wezemigwaqo wenza itshe lesikhumbuzo sendawo lapho afela khona uNandi. Akesiphothule umiando kaNandi ngezibongo zakhe: 

USomnqeni. 
UMathanga ialwahlangani, Ahlangana ngokubon' umyeni. 
U Gedegede lwasenhla nenkundla. Uphoko phalala kuMaqhwaialzi, Angibonang' uphoko ukuphalala. UMboni wamabhuzenge uSontanti. USontanti onjengowakwaGwazana. Udl' ubisi lwenkom' enezimpondo, Ukwesab' abayisengayo. 

Intombi ialMbengi weNguga ialSoyengwase ialMaqamede. UXebe woMhlathuze. 

Mjazi ontongande zingamadoda. Uyishaye yenyus' isabiza.

kuwo unina kwakuthiwa kuseTshiya. UJobe wayeyithanda kakhulu indodana yakhe uTana kangangoba waze wavurna ukuba ikhulele ekhabonina. UTana waze wabuyela oYengweni esethombile. UJobe wayenesifiso sokuba uTana kube uyena nkosi urna yena engasekho. 


Uzungu IokubuIaIa uJobe: Kwathi ngoba esegugile uJobe uDingiswayo noTana basunguIa uzungu lokuba uyise abulawe. Induna uNodunga kaMakhanya kaNjonjonjo wakwaMthethwa wayizwa Ie nhlebo wahamba wayobikela uJobe. 
  Esezwile ngalolu zungu uJobe wahlala izinsuku eziningi engakhulurnisi muntu edidwe akuzwile. Wagcina ngokuba anike leyo naleyo ndodana yakhe inkabi. Wabe esetshela induna ukuthi itshele amadodana akhe ukuthi yileyo naleyo ndodana ihlabe eyayo inkabi ngoba uJobe wayezofika kodwa wafika ngelilandelayo ephelezelwa amabutho amaningi. Wayesewatshelile amabutho ukuthi ayobulala wonke amadodana akhe angarnshiyi uDingiswayo. 
  Nebala uJobe watsaka amathe kuphuzwa amabutho ase engenela amadodana kaJobe ngernikhonto. UDingiswayo wahlatshwa ngornkhonto ethangeni kodwa wabaleka nawo weqa uthango lwesibaya. Wabaleka nornkhonto ethangeni waze wangenisa kuDlaba kaMavovo emaCubeni. Lapha-ke barnkhipha urnkhonto wahlala laze lanqurna inxeba. UTana yena wabulawa. 
  Wasuka lapha waya phansi koNdi kuMthirnkhulu kaBhungane kaNsele emaI-llutshini. Wangenisa ernzlru kaNgqwashu khona emaI-llutshini. UNgqwashu wabesehamba eyombika enkosini uMthirnkhulu. Inkosi yathi akelashwe bese elethwa kuyo khona izozibonela ukuthi uzalwa uJobe ngempela. Walethwa-ke uDingiswayo eseluleme. Inkosi yathi kuye kuhle alande amazinyane amabili ebhubesi. La mazinyane ayehlezi nonina. 
Phela lokhu kwakuyindlela yokubona ukuthi'igazi lenkosi 
lizohlonipheka yini ezilwaneni. Nebala wabuya nawo arnazinyane engazange athola ngisho urnyocu. Inkosi nabantu bayo bakholwa ukuthi ngempela uDingiswayo uzalwa ebukhosini bakwaJobe. Amazinyane abuyiselwa kunina. Inkosi u-

! 
  
Mthimkhulu yahlaba inkabi emhlophe ihlabela uDingiswayo. 
  Kwaphela izinsuku ezintathu kwenzekile lokhu uDingiswayo wavalelisa ngoba esaba ukuthi impi kayise iyamlandela. Wahamba uDingiswayo waze wagcina engenise enkosini uBhungane inkosi yamaHIubi. Esahleli lapha wezwa ngokufa kukayise: Wazimisela ukubuyela ekhaya ayothatha ubukhosi 
	bakheayekadeebufuna. 	. 
  Ngalesi sikhathi base beqalile abelungu ukubonakala behamba begibele amahhashi futhi bephethe izibhamu. Babedlula khona ngasezweni lakhe uBhungane. Kuhle kwaziwe nokuthi kwakuqabukela lokhu kuzwakale ngoba sekukhona abathi babone umIungu nakhu phela babeba babili noma mhIawumbe abemunye. Sengathi kukubo la belungu lapho uDingiswayo athola khona injomane nesibhamu afika nakho ekhaya. Imilandu ekhona ayisho ukuthi wakufunda nini ukugibela injomane nokudubula ngesibhamu. 
Indlela ebange ekhaya: Wahamba waya ekhaya. Eseseduzane nasekhaya wathola iqiniso lokuthi akasekho uyise nokuthi washiya ebeke uMawewe. Engakafi uJobe wathi akakholwa ukuthi uDingiswayo wafa. UMawewe uzalwa umakoti wakubo kaDingiswayo. UDingiswayo wafika wema entabeni ngenhla komuzi wakubo wamemeza wathi: 
"Ngqwaba, ngqwaba, yemuka nayo! Uyiyenga ngani na?" 
Abantu bethuka ukuthi ngabe ubani 10 muntu omemeza ebusuku entabeni. Wehla entabeni wayongenisa kwamkhwenyawabo uMbangambi kaDlozi kaLushozi wasemaTshobeni. Naye uMbangambi kwaba yima ecacelwa ukuthi ubani lona okade ememeza entabeni. UDingiswayo wavivisa amabutho, uMawewe owayesezwile ngokufika kwakhe wabaleka waya ekhabonina kwaNxumalo. 
  Inkosi yakwaNxumalo yala ukumbuyisela emuva uMawewe njengesicelo sikaDingiswayo. UDingiswayo wathumela izwi enkosini yakwaNxumalo eyitshela ukuthi uzoyihlasela uma 
16 


, .! 
ingambuyisi uMawewe. Ayibange isalinda inkosi yakwaNxumalo yashesha yathumela uMawewe emuva eluYengweni. UDingiswayo wabesekhipha izwi lokuthi uMawewe kabulawe watshela ababemlethile ukuthi uyobuya abenezwi nenkosi yakwaNxumalo. 
Inguquko ekubuyeni kukaDingiswayo: Esebulewe uMawewe uDingiswayo wathola ithuba lokufeza izifiso nezinjongo zakhe ngesizwe sakwaMthethwa. Ziningi izinto athi ekubuyeni kwakhe waziguqula wabuye wafaka izinhlelo ezintsha empilweni yabantu. Kuhle sikhumbule ukuthi okokuqala nje ukufika kwakhe egibele injomane futhi ephethe isikhali esingaziwa kwenza ukuthi abantu bamthande, bamhloniphe, bamesabe. Lezi zinto zaziyingqalabutho kubantu bakule ngxenye yomhlaba. Wahlela abesilisa wabehlukanisa ngamabutho ngobudala bawo. Yilelo nalelo butho lanikezwa igama. Amabutho ayehlala evivinywa ukuze ahIale ecijile. Ibutho laliba nomholi bese kuba khona izinduna zempi yenkosi uDingiswayo. Izinduna zempi zaziyiphaka sezixoxile nenkosi. 
UDingiswayo akagcinanga ngokuguqula uhlelo Iwezimpi. 
Ngonyaka wakhe wokuqala eousa waqala ukuhweba nabamhlophe eDalagubhe (Delagoa Bay). Wathumela izinkabi eziyikhulu ukuba ziyothenga ubuhlalu kanye nezingubo zokulala. Wabuye wathumela namaningi amazinyo ezindlovu. Abahwebi abamhIophe babemthumela izipho njengezitsha zokudlela, imicamelo, amadlelo kagwayi nokunye. Kulezi zipho uDingiswayo 
. wayekhetha ezinye athi abantu bakhe abazakhe ngokwabo. 
Lowo owayephumelela ukwakha okucishe kufane nesipho leso wayeklonyeliswa. Kubikwa ukuthi umkIomelo omkhulu wathoIwa indoda eyakhanda isihlalo ngokuqopha ukhuni. Kubikwa ukuthi kwagcina sekunefektri encane enamadoda ayikhulu eyasungulwa uDingiswayo. 
  Ukuthitthukisa izinga lokulwa nendlela ayehlasela ngayo kwadala ukuhlakazeka kwezizwana ezazakhelene naye uDingiswayo. Akesibone ukuthi uDingiswayo wawabutha kanjani amabutho akhe. Nanka-ke amabutho:

iZiehwe induna kunguTayiza. 
iNyakeni induna kunguDube kaYengeni. iNhlangano induna kunguNgomane kaMqomboyo waseMadletsheni. 
iNingizimll induna kunguMayanda ka Veyana wakwaMkhwanazi. 
iMini induna kunguNomadidi kaGugushi wasebaThenjini. 
iSilazana induna kunguNohaya kaNgaba (Ngabha) kaNsindana wakwaMwandla. 
iNyakatho induna yalo ayaziwanga.

Ibutho leZichwe ladla izinkomo zalo ladla nezinkomo zamanye amabutho ladla nezenkosi imbala. Inkosi yathukuthela kakhulu labulawa leli butho kanye nenduna yalo uTayiza. UDingiswayo wabesebutha elinye ibutho walibiza ngalo igama leZichwe induna yalo kwaba uBllza. Lasuswa endaweni yalo layiswa eMangweni. Lingakahambi ibutho uDingiswayo waba nembizo enkulu lapho atshela khona abantu ukuthi igama lakhe elisha esikhundleni sikaGodongwana uDingiswayo, bangabe besambiza ngelikaGodongwana. 
UkuhlaseIa kukaDingiswayo: Kwathi ukuba abone ukuthi impi yakhe seyiqinile waqala ukuhlasela izizwe, waqala ngazo eziseduze naye. Abanye abalobi bathi wayezisukela izizwe azihlasele futhi wayehlasela ngesihluku. Uma sicwaninga sithola ukuthi: indlela okwakunqotshwa ngayo ngalezo khathi indlela yempi, impi ayinaso isihe. Zonke izizwe ezazizinikela ngaphandle kokulwa azizange zaphathwa kabi zazamukelwa phansi kombuso wenkosi uDingiswayo. 
  Lokhu kuyakhombisa ukuthi injongo yenkosi uDingiswayo kwakung ukuhlanganisa izizwana ezincane ukuze zakhe isizwe esikhulu esinamandla. 
  Futhi nokuhlasela kwakhe kwakusukela ephuzwini elithiIe ngoba enkolweni yesiko lakubo kwakuthiwa ungamsukeli

kodwa akazange ambulale wadla izinkomo nesigodlo ngoba ethi ukubulala inkosi kudliwe nesifazane kuphofisa umhlabathi. Okwesibili wahlasela uTokozwayo kaMandayiya owafa kuleyo 
mpi. 
Okwesithathu wahlasela uPhakathwayo kaKhondlo ka- 
Mncinci kaLufutha kaSimamane wakwaQwabe. Wehlulwa uPhakathwayo waze waya kuDingiswayo eyoxolisa. Baxolelana, nakhu phela babendiselene. Okwesine ukuhlasela wakuqondisa kuMatiwane kaMasumpa kaSihayo waseMangwaneni. 
  Okwesihlanu wahlasela uMacingwane kaLuboko waseNgonyameni eNkandla emaChunwini. Sekuthi okwesithupha usehlasela uZwide kaLanga wakwaNxumalo (kaNdwandwe). Wathola ubunzima obukhulu ekulweni kwakhe noZwide ngoba umbuso kaZwide wawumkhulu futhi amabutho akhe 
enomfutho. 
UZwide wayakhe ngaphesheya kweMfolozi eganwe 
udadewabo kaDingiswayo uGijimi. Kuthiwa bekuthi njalo uma ehluliwe uZwide esethunjiwe abuye adedelwe ngoba uDingiswayo ehlonipha ubuhlobo. 

Ukukhonza kukaZulu kwaMthethwa: Inkosi uSenzangakhona yaqala ukuthuma abantu kwaMthethwa ukuba bathengise ikhathazo. Induna uMudli wabuya nezinkomo kuDingiswayo. Wathunywa futhi uMudli enkosini uDingiswayo ukuba ayokhongela inkosi uSenzangakhona. Wavuma uDingiswayo ngoba embona empofu uSenzangakhona. Lokhu kwenza ukuba bangahlaselani . 
19 





Ukukhonza kukaShaka kuDingiswayo: UShaka wafika kwaMthelhwa ehamba nonina uNandi nodadewabo uNomcuba. Bafikela oHeni ernzini kaDingiswayo. Wabavuma uDingiswayo bahlalshiswa. Inkosi yamnikela kuNgomane owathunywa ukuba akhele uShaka umuzi. Lo muzi kwathiwa kukwaGqogqa. UShaka waiUkwa izinkomo. Ufika lapha nje uNandi sewake wagana uGendeyana wakwaQwabe azala kuye uNgwadi. 
  Beza kwaMlhethwa nje yingoba induna uMudli wathi ababaleke ngoba uSenzangakhona uthukuthelele indaba kaGendeyana. UShaka wahlala lapha waze wabekwa induna yaseSinameni esigabeni esinye sasoYengweni. Waba nezibongo zakhe zobuqhawe nakhu phela wayeba khona kuzo zonke izimpi ezaziphakwa uDingiswayo. UDingiswayo uwanqoba wonke nje amakhosi ukhona uShaka uyazibonela. 
USenzangakhona uvakashela uDingiswayo: Wayejwayele uSenzangakhona ukuvakashela kwaMthethwa. MhIa efika okokugcina wayehamba nenkosikazi yakhe uBhibhi ozalwa uSompisi kaKuguqa wakwaNtuli. Engakabuyeli ekhaya uSenzangakhona wenzelwa umgidi lapho kwasina khona amabutho. USenzangakhona wakhangwa kakhulu insizwa eyasina kahle kakhulu. Wathi uma exoxa ngayo kuDingiswayo wathola ukuthi uShaka indodana yakhe. Wabizwa uShaka baqala ukubonana ubuso nobuso sekuphele iminyaka eminingi behlukana. 
UShaka ulhalha ubukhosi kwaZulu: USenzangakhona wasuka kwaMthelhwa wabuyela ekhaya. Kwaphela izinsuku ezimbalwa yafa inkosi uSenzangakhona. Wanele wabikelwa uDingiswayo wathumela uNgomane noSiwangu kaMbikwana wakwaMlhethwa namabulho. Baphelezela uShaka bafika bambeka ebukhosini bakwaZulu. Izikhulu zikaSenzangakhona zabulawa - oMudli, noZivalele, Malangala, noMbumana noSigujana. 
Imizi yenkosi uDingiswayo: Nansi imizi eyayisemqoka kubusa uDingiswayo: oYengweni, eMnini, eZiyondleya, oHeni, eManineni, eNhlambeni, eZichweni, eNyakeni, eNingizimu, 
20 
eNlambanana, eBalungwini. 
eNhlangano, 
eNyakalho, 
eSifazaneni, 

Ukufa kukaDingiswayo: Sekushiwo ukuthi ezimpini ezaba khona phakalhi kukaZwide noDingiswayo kwakuvamile ukuba uZwide anqotshwe athunjwe futhi. Ngenxa yobuhlobo wayededelwa abuyele ezweni lakhe. Kwenzeka kwezinye zalezi zimpi wanqoba uZwide kwathunjwa uDingiswayo. Akazange akhululwe uDingiswayo. Wayiswa ernzini kaZwide eNyakalho nenlaba uSigwekwe eduzane noNongoma. Lapha-ke wabulawa uDingiswayo, cishe ngo-1818. 
Isikhundla sikaDingiswayo sathathwa umfowabo uMondisa. 
Umuzi kaDingiswayo wehlukana kabili abanye bevuma uMondisa abanye bengamvumi ngoba belhi kukhona amadodana kaDingiswayo ayesekhulile efanele ukuthatha isikhundla sikayise. UMondisa wabesebulala zonke izikhulu zikaDingiswayo. UNgomane wasuka namabutho akhe bayobikela uShaka. UShaka wabesemamukela uNgomane nabaholi abangamvumanga uMondisa. Emva kwalokhu uShaka wabulala uMondisa walithatha lonke elakwaMthethwa. Lokhu kwaba ukuphela kombuso wakwaMthethwa okuyiwona owaba isisekelo esiqolho sokuvuka kombuso kaZulu owaduma umhIaba wonke waze wanya~azisa owamaNgisi ngempi yaseSandlwana.

Mzilikazi (Khumalo) kaMashobanci 1770 - 1868 

Inkom' ekhal' eMlhonjaneni, 

Izizwe zonke ziyizwil' ukulila, Izwiwe nguDunjwa wasoYengweni, Yezwiwa uMangcengeza kaKhali, 
Yaye yezwiwa amaNlungwa akwaSokhumalo. 

Ngesikhathi inkosi uShaka ihIasela izizwe izama ukwakha umbuso owodwa wabansundu e-Afrika, akekho owayazi ukuthi ukuhlakazeka kwabantu beya kwamanye amazwe kwakuyodala izizwe ezintsha. Indaba kaMzilikazi iyinkomba yalokhu ngoba uma sikhuluma ngesizwe samaNdebele esiseZimbabwe sikhuluma ngesizwe umsungu1i waso okunguMzilikazi wakwaKhumalo. 
  UMzilikazi kwakuyindodana kaMashobana inkosi yesizwe sakwaKhumalo. Unina kaMzilikazi kwakunguNompethu indodakazi yenkosi yakwaZulu. Yena uMzilikazi kulinganiswa ukuthi wazalwa ngo-l770. Kuthiwa kwathi esemncane wasuswa ekhaya kubo wayiswa emzini wenkosi uZwide lapho akhulela khona. Wakhula kanye nontanga emzini kamkhulu uZwide. Ekukhuleni kwakhe inkosi uZwide yayithe shi ilwa izimpi ezinzima nenkosi yesizwe sakwaMthethwa uDingiswayo kaJobe. Empini enkulu eyalwiwa kwafa inkosi uDingiswayo kwafa noyise kaMzilikazi. 

UMzilikazi uyinkosi: Kwathi ukuba afe uMashobana uZwide wabeka uMzilikazi ebukhosini besizwe sakwaKhumalo. Esefile uDingiswayo umbango phakathi kwezizwe zabaNguni wangena kwelinye izinga. UShaka wayesebusa ,kwaZulu esewuqalile umkhankaso wakhe wokuhlasela izizwe ukuze akhe umbuso 
24 

owodwa onamandla. 
  Isikhashana efile uDingiswayo kwaqubuka izimpi phakathi kukaShaka noZwide. Ngokungamethembi kahle uyisemkhulu uZwide, uMzilikazi wabaleka waya ngasenkosini uShaka. Inkosi uShaka yabe isimenza umholi wamabutho yamkhombisa ukumethemba okukhulu. Ukumethemba inkosi yakukhombisa 
ngokuba imthume uMzilikazi ukuba ayohlasela isizwe sabe Suthu esasiseduze nelakwaZulu. Wahamba uMzilikazi wasihlasela Ie sizwe wasehlula wathumba izinkomo. 
  Wabesengenwa isilingo uMzilikazi. Lesi silingo sagcina sesichithe eminingi imiphefumulo saze sagcina ngokuba kudaleke isizwe samaNdebele ezweni okuthiwa iZimbabwe namuhla. 
  Izinkomo lezi okwathiwa abozithumba abuye nazo wabona ukuthi kungcono azigcine. Ngesikhathi kulindelwe ukuthi izinkomo zifike enkosini uShaka lutho, uMzilikazi wazigcina noma sekufike izwi livela khona komkhulu. Izithunywa zenkosi uShaka zaphathwa ngokwedelela sengathi abafokazana. Izimpaphe ezifakwa enhloko zanqunywa zase ziphindiselwa emuva. Wayazi kahle kamhlophe uMzilikazi ukuthi lesi senzo sizoyithukuthelisa kakhulu inkosi uShaka nakanjani imjezise. Ukuze azihlenge olakeni Iwenkosi uShaka uMzilikazi wazakhela inqaba phezu kwentaba iNtubeni. 
  Nebala inkosi uShaka ayichithanga sikhathi yathumela amabutho kuMzilikazi. Lokhu kuhlasela kokuqala akuphumelelanga ngoba amabutho ehluleka ukungena enqabeni. Yathi inkosi uShaka isadla amathambo ekhanda ifuna isu lokufundisa uMzilikazi isifundo angasoze asikhohlwe kwabese kufika imbuka lakwaKhumalo. Kusobala ukuthi lambuluka ngoba 'Iesaba ukuthi impi yenkosi uShaka ingase ifike ibabhuqe bengazi ukuthi uMzilikazi uzabalazelani nezinkomo zenkosi.

abakhetha ukuba basale. Wabathatha wabangenisa phansi kombuso kaZulu. 

UMzilikazi ubaleka uya enhla nezwe: Wabaleka njalo uMzilikazi wayonqamula ezigodini zaseFilidi wedlula ePiet Retief waze wafika e-Ermelo ngobusika buka 1821. Ubunzima bobusika benza ukuba uMzilikazi nabalandeli baphumule bakhe amadlangala. WabesehIasela izizwana ezincane azifica lapho. WazihIakaza wathumba izinkomo zazo kwathi ezingabalekanga wazingenisa eqenjini labalandeli bakhe. Ngale ndlela kwanda imfuyo, kwanda amabutho, kwanda abalandeli. Kwaba ukuqala kokuba kudaleke isizwe esiyingxubevange yezizwana ezincane. 
  Ngokwazi ukuthi inkosi uShaka izomlandela wesuka lapha waqhubeka nokubheka eNyakatho nezwe wedlula eMpumalanga neNtilasifali kwathi ngo-1822 wathi ukuzinza eduze nomfula i-Olifants maduze nendawo okuthiwa manje iGroblersdal. Lapha wakha umuzi wakhe omkhulu owaziwa ngokuthi kuseKuphumeni ekhumbula ukuphuma kwakhe kwaZulu. Yayikhona eminye imizi emincane ayeyakhile. Nalapha futhi wahIasela izizwe azifica. Zahlakazeka, wathumba imfuyo nabantu. Lezi zizwe wayezehIula kalula ngoba izinga laze ekulweni izimpi lalisephansi. Isomiso samphoqelela uMzilikazi ukuba ashiye eKuphumeni aqhubeke nokubaleka. 
  Kuhle kushiwo lapha ukuthi ziningi kabi izinkinga nobunzima ababehIangana nakho kulolu hambo. Yayingekho imigwaqo; izwe linamahIathi nezikhotha konke kwesabeka; kulukhuni ukuhamba nokuthwala abalimele ezimpini kuliwa nezinye izizwe; izingane nabesifazane kwakufanele bagadwe; izinhIoli kwakufuneka zikhaliphe kakhulu ingabikhona elala emsebenzini. 
  Esesukile eKuphumeni wahamba kwathi lapho kuhlangana khona imifula i-Olifants neSteelpoort watholana phezulu nesizwe samaPedi. Nokho wasinqoba. Wabe esehIala khona ezweni labaPedi waze wasuka ngo-1823 walandela umkhondo oya ernfuleni iVaal. Wabesakha phakathi neHeidelberg nePotchefstroom. Wafika lapha ngo-1823 waze wahamba ngo1827.

Umbango wezinkomo: Ukwanda kwemihIambi eminingi yezinkomo yadala ukuba uMzilikazi abenezivakashi ezingamenyiwe. Amaqembu esizwe samaK?~ana ayelo~u e~.asel~ izindawo lapho kubekwe khona lzinkomo zlkaMzilikazl. Ayefike ahIasele abaleke masinyane nezinkomo ezimbalwa. 
  Ngo-1828 inkosi uMoletsane wesizwe sabaTaung wakhuthaza uJan Bloem umholi wamaKorana ukuba ahole impi kuxoshwe uMzilikazi aphume aphele eNtilasifali. UMoletsane wayenenjongo yokuba axoshwe uMzilikazi kanti uBloem yena wayejahe izinkomo. Ngenkathi ehIasel,,:a uMzilikazi impi yakhe enkulu yayingekho iyohIasela isizwe sakwaNgwaketse enhIa nenyakatho. Kwathi uma ebona uMzilikazi ukuthi zimbi izinto watshela bonke abalandeli bakhe ukuba bashiye izinkomo bacashe ehIathini. 
  UBloem owayehola eyabahIaseli wachazeka ukuthola izinkomo engalwanga. Bayishushumbisa imihIambi bebuyela nayo emuva. Angithi kuhanjwa izinsuku eziningi kubuye kumiwe kuhlatshwe kuyo Ie mihlambi. Kwathi emva kwezinsuku ezintathu ebusuku atheleka amabutho kaMzilikazi-isalele impi kaBloem. KwahIabana ngisho nezifiki empini .. Kwathathwa izibhamu eziningi zabuyiswa izinkomo.

Ekuxoxeni kwakhe uSchoen wayememezela ukuthi ufuna-, ukuvakashela izwe eliseduze nelikaMzilikazi. Wacabanga' uMzilikazi efuna isu lokurnheha uSchoen eze kwelakhe izwe. 

  Kwathi urna uSchoen ebuyela eNtilasifaii ngobusika buka 1829 ephelezelwa u William McLuckie bahlangana nezinhloli zikaMzilikazi. Izinhloli zabancenga ukuba bavakashele uMzilikazi owayakhe urnuzi wakhe eduzane nendawo ebizwa ngokuthi iPiloli namuhla. UMzilikazi wacela uSchoen ukuba arnkhombise ukuthi isibhamu sisebenza kanjani. 

  Ukuhambela kukaSchoen kwamcacela uMzilikazi ukuthi kudingekile ukubazi kabanzi abelungu nernikhuba yabo. Ngakho-ke wazirnisela ukuba kube khona ubudlelwano phakathi kwakhe nabo. Wabe esecela uSchoen ukuba ameme abanye abelungu ukuba bavakashele ezweni lakhe. Wathurnela izinduna zakhe ezimbili ukuba zihambe noSchoen owayeyobonana nornfundisi uRobert Moffat eKuruman. Bahamba bafike bahlala isonto eKuruman. 

  Sebeliqedile isonto' sebezobuyela emuva bancenga uMoffat ukuba abakhaphe ingxenye yohambo. Wabakhapha baze basondela ernzini ornkhulu eNkungweni endaweni yaseMagalisberg. Besahamba endleleni bahlangana noJames Archbell neqembu lakhe bevela ePlatberg. USchoen wabatshela ukuthi uMzilikazi uyabathakasela abamhlophe abavakashele izwe lakhe. iphurnelele.

UArchbell wayengazi ukuthi lesi senzo sokungena nezikhali ezweni lenkosi yisenzo sokuhlosa impi. Kwathi urna beyongena ngasemasangweni omuzi ornkhulu kaMzilikazi kwadingeka ukuba balinde kuvele izwi kuMzilikazi elishoyo ukuthi bayavurneleka noma chao Izwi elavela kornkhulu lathi uBarends akamukeleki.

UMoffat warnukelwa ngelikhulu isasasa urna efika ekupheleni kuka 1829. Lokhu kuhIangana kwaba ukuqala kobuhlobo nokuzwana kweminyaka erniningi eyalandelayo. . UMzilikazi uqhubeka nokuhlasela: Kwaphela izinsuku ezimbalwa ehambile uMoHat uMzilikazi wahlasela kathathu izizwe ezazakhe entshonalanga nezwe lakhe. lsizwe esalimala kakhulu esarnaNgwaketse. Ngo-1831 uMzilikazi wathurnela impi yakhe ukuyohlasela ngaphesheya komfu1a iVaal. Lapha impi yatholana phezulu namabutho enkosi yesizwe sabaTlokwa, uSigonyela. Yehlulwa ekaSigonyela. UMzilikazi wabesehlasela inkosi enkulu yabeSuthu, uMshweshwe. UMshweshwe wavele wazicashela enqabeni yakhe iThaba Bosigo akaze athintwa lutho. 
Ngesikhathi ephaka impi ukuba iyohlasela isizwe sarnaShona eZirnbabwe, urnbuso kaMzilikazi wahlaselwa izizwe ezintathu: amaHiligwa, amaKoranas nabeTswana. Babeholwa uBarend Barends. UMzilikazi wakubalekela ukuba impi itholane phezulu ngezifuba ngoba wabona ukuthi abahlaseli laba bahlome ngezikhali ezinzima. 
EkaMzilikazi yacasha ehlathini abahlaseli bazithathela izinkomo. Sekuthi eduzane nentaba iMoordkop yafika eka-

Mzilikazi ebusuku yahlasela behlulwa. UBarends yena akazange aqhubeke nernpi ayeyihola wasala endaweni iMakwassie sekwala amadolo nakhu phela nokuguga kwasekubhokile. Nokwehlulwa kwernpi ayeyihola watshelwa izinduna zernpi. 
  Ernveni kokuba ehlulekile ukuhlasela inqaba yaseThaba Bosigo, . uMzilikazi wahlasela abeTswana eduze nendawo iMagaliesburg. Irnizarno kaMzilikazi ukuba ehlule isizwe sabeTswana yaphazanyiswa ukufika kule ndawo kwabafundisi barnaFrentshi abango Jean Lows Prosper Lernue, Jean Pirre Pellisier noSarnuel Roland. La rnadoda asungula irnishani endaweni yaseMosega. Ukungathokozi kukaMzilikazi kwenza athurnele izinduna zakhe ukuba zibize abefundisi ukuba beze ernzini wakhe ornkhulu. 
  UPelisier waya ernzini kaMzilikazi ngo-April ka-1832 waphathwa kahle kakhulu. Kwaphela isikhathi eSUushane ernva kwakho konke lokhu abefundisi ababevela ezweni laseTransvaal baqoqa konke okwabo bahamba. Bahanjiswa ukubona ukuthi ingxabano phakathi kukaMzilikazi nesizwe sabaHurutse kungeke kusize urnsebenzi wabefundisi. 
UZulu uhlasela uMzilikazi: UMzilikazi wahamba ekhaya kwaZulu ngendlela engajwayelekile. Naye uMzilikazi wayazi ukuthi isenzo sakhe siyogcina ngokwenza ulaka lukaZulu ukuba lurnlandele. Nebala lokho ayekulindele kwenzeka ngo-1832. 
  UMzilikazi wayengazelele ukuthi kungathi ekupheleni kuka1832 uZulu ahlasele ngoba phela uMzilikazi esenecala lokubaleka nezinkorno zikaZulu. Naye uMzilikazi wayehlalele ovalweni kodwa lokhu kuhlasela kwarnfica engazelele. UZulu uhlasela nje ekaMzilikazi impi ayikho uyiphake wayiqondisa enhla nezwe. 
  Ubunzima benza ukuthi uMzilikazi abalekele uZulu. Wafika esigodini saseMarico wahlasela izizwe azifica khona. Ukuvikela urnbuso wakhe uMzilikazi wakha imizi yamabutho erningceleni. Wakha urnuzi iMosega wawenza ikomkhulu wenganyelwa induna yernpi uMkhaliphi. Eseyakhile irnizi eyishurni nanhlanu yamabutho uMzilikazi wazakhela isithabathaba sornuzi wakhe owaziwa ngokuthi iseGabeni. Ngo-1834 uMzilikazi wayese- 
30 
zinzile ezweni elisha. 
  Ngo-1835 enyangeni kaMay uMoffat waphelezela udokotela uAndrew Smith owayeharnba ngezesayensi. Banqamula ezweni likaMzilikazi. Kuthe esebuyela ernuva eKoloni uSmith wacelwa uMzilikazi ukuba ahambe nezinduna zakhe ziye eCape Town. Nebala zahamba izinduna. Zingakabuyi induna enkulu yasayina isivurnelwano egarneni lenkosi uMzilikazi. lsivurnelwano sathi uMzilikazi uyoseka uHulurneni waseKoloni urna 10 Hulurneni ehlaselwa. Isivurnelwano sasayinwa ngenyanga kaMarch ngo1836. 
  Ngawo 10 nyaka uMzilikazi wacelwa abefundisi baseMerlka ukuba avume basebenze urnsebenzi wevangeli ezweni lakhe. Nebala ngo-1836 uDaniel Lindley, Alexander Erwin Wilson noHenry Veneble bafikela eMosega baqala umsebenzi wobufundisi. 
  Umsebenzi wabo awuchurnanga ngenxa yezirnpi kant! futhi noMzilikazi wayengeneme ngendlela abelungu ababanda ngayo befika ubuthaphuthaphu bethi bazozingela amazinyo ezindlovu. Ngo-August ka-1836 abalandeli bakaMzilikazi bahlasela inkarnbi yabazingeli babelungu phansi kornholi uStephanus Petros Erasmus. Kwafa abaningi abelungu kulesi siwombe. Arnabutho kaMzilikazi edlula lapha ayohlasela iqernbu elaliholwa uUebenberg. Babulawa cishe bonke abaleli qembu. 
  Emva kwalokhu uMzilikazi waphaka enkulu irnpi ukuba iyohlasela abafuduki ababeholwa uHendrik Potgieter. EkaMzilikazi yayiholwa uMkhaliphi. Yatholana ngasernfuleni iVaal. . AmaBhunu ayevele eselindele ukuhlaselwa. Ernpini enzima eyaziwa ngokuthi eyaseVegkop yehlulwa ekaMzilikazi ngo-October ka-1836. ArnaBhunu abe esephaka eyawo yokuba kujeziswe uMzilikazi. Yawuhlasela urnuzi ornkhulu iMosega ngoJanuary ka1837.

wabaleka nabaningi abalandeli weqa umfula iLimpopo. 

Ngaphesheya komfula iLimpopo: Ekufikeni kwabo ngaphesheya kwalo mfula abalandeli bakaMzilikazi behlukana kabili. lqembu elalilandela uMzilikazi laqonda eNyakatho nentshonalanga. Elesibili elalilandela uMkhaliphi laze lafika lapho kukhona iZimbabwe lase lakha umuzi omkhulu uGibixhegu. Ithemba lokuthi la maqembu ayobuye ahIangane laphela. Indodana kaMzilikazi uNkulumane wabe esebekwa waphatha abantu bakayise. UMzilikazi akazange ahIale kwaGibixhegu noma amaqembu esebuye ahlangana. Wazakhela owakhe umuzi eduze nalapho kukhona iBulawayo. Lo muzi wanikwa igama lokuthi uMahlokohloko. 
  Ngesikhathi ewela umfula iVaal uMzilikazi wayenabalandeli abanhlobo mbili. Kwakukhona amaZulu ayesuke nawo kwaZulu bese kubakhona abalandeli ayebathola ezizweni ayezinqoba njengabeSuthu nezinye. 
  Wathi ukuba azinze ezweni lamaNdebele kwabonakala ukuthi izifiki lezi zibanempilo esezingeni elingaphezu kwabanikazi bendawo, amaKaranga namaShona. Nalapha futhi uMzilikazi wakha imizi eyayigadwe amabutho. UMzilikazi akazange ahIale isikhathi eside ernzini owodwa ngoba umbuso wakhe wawumkhulu. Wayenezinhloli ezikhaliphile futhi izimpimpi zakhe zibaba hal Zigcwele yonke indawo. 
  Kwaba khona ukuxhumana phakathi kukaMzilikazi nomholi wamaBhunu uPotgieter. Ukuxhumana kwagcina ngokuba kusayinwe isivumelwano ngo-January ka-1853 kuphele amasonto amathathu eshonile uPotgieter. NgoMay ka-1853 uMzilikazi wasayina esinye isivumelwano nomholi uA.W. Pretorius. 
  UMoffat wakwazi ukuba atholele abefunclisi imvume yokusebenza ezweni likaMzilikazi kodwa wehluleka ukuba athole umhlaba okuzothiwa ungowabefunclisi. 
  Urnzingeli uHenry Hartley owayethandwa uMzilikazi wafika neJalimane uKarl Manch owayefuna umcebo ombiwayo. Ngo1867 uKarl wahamba ecwaninga ezimayini ezindala wathola izimboni zegolide. 
Lezi zimboni zenza ukuba indawo yesizwe samaShona 

32 

namaNdebele ibe indawo ebalulekile. Baningi abelungu abathutheleka bezomba igolide. UMzilikazi akazange akuthande ukufika kwabelungu abaningi ezweni lakhe. Noma engenzanga lutho ngalokhu wahlushwa ukuguga nempilo kwazise ukuthi iminyaka yase ihambile. 

UMzilikazi uyawushiya umhlaba: UMzilikazi waba nesikhathi eside sokuphila. Ukufa kwakhe ngo-1868 kwaba ukugcina kokubusa iminyaka engamashumi amane nanhlanu. Le minyaka yaba yinkomba yomlando waseMzansi Afrika. Baningi abantu nezizwe okwaguquka impilo yabo ngenxa kaMzilikazi. Le mpilo yabonakala kakhulu eNtilasifali naseRhodesia eyaziwa namhlanje ngokuthi iZimbabwe. 
  Wayenazo izimpawu zokubona kukaShaka. NjengoShaka uMzilikazi wayenendlela yokunqoba bese ethatha izizwe azinqobile zanclise umbuso wakhe. Imizi yakhe nokuyivikela kwakukhombisa indlela ayethanda ngayo ukuvikela abantu bakhe. Ukusayina izivumelwano nabelungu kwakukhombisa ukuthi wayenalo uthando lokuhlalisana kahle nabelungu. Ukungabathancli abelungu abaningi ezweni lakhe yingoba wayengathandi ukuba kuguquke impilo namasiko omdabu. Wafa uMzilikazi washiya umlando oyohlala usemqoka eMzansi Afrika.

I 
Ntsikana, (Gaba) 1783 - 1820' 
"Ulo Thixo omkhulu osezulwini" 

Wayeyindodana kaGaba induna yenkosi uNgqika. Unina kwakunguNonibe inkosikazi yesibili kaGaba. Kulinganiswa ukuthi uNtsikana wazalwa ngo-1783. 
  Kwathi ukuba kufe uyise basuka abakubo bayokwakha ngasemfuleni iMankazana kude buduze nomuzi kaNgqika. Yilapha lapho abona khona umfundisi uDr J.T. Van der Kemp owayehlala emzini kaNgqika ngo-1799-1800. Wayethanda ukumlalela eshumayela umfundisi. Zamthatha izintshumayelo, wafisa ukuba aguquke akholwe. UVan der Kemp wayaziwa ngelikaNyengana. 
  Kuthe esekhulile ngokwesiko lakubo waganwa. Waba namakhosikazi amabill uNontsonta, owabe enengane eyodwa, noNomanto, owathola izingane ezintathu. Ngalesi sikhathi wayesenyamalele uNyengana ngenxa yeziphithiphithi zokulwa. Wathi ukuba afe uyise wathatha ifa lakhe kwathi emva kweminyakana wathutha wayokwakha eGqora esigodini saseMankazana. Wayethi uma ehlell noma ehamba ezwe sengathi uzwa izwi likaNyengana. Kwase kukhona omunye umlungu owayeshumayela njengoNyengana. Yena kwakungumfundisi uJames Read owayaziwa ngellkaNgcongolo. Ngonyaka ka-1816 uNtsikana waguquka wemukela inkolo yobuKrestu engeniswa umfundisi uJoseph Williams weqembu labefundisi elalaziwa ngokuthi London Missionary Society. 
  Wathutha uNtsikana wayohlala eduzane nomuzi wenkosi uNgqika khona ezothola ulwazi olubanzi ngenkolo yobuKreslu. 
  Imibhalo yeBhayibheli yagxila kakhulu emqondweni kaNtsikana futhi izingxoxo ayeba nazo nomfundisi u Williams zaguqula umcabango wakhe. Ngokwamukela imfundiso yabe- 
34 
. , 
, 

45. 

fundisi ukuthi umunlu akabe nenkosikazi eyodwa wabe 
, esehlukana nenkosikazi yesibili uNomanto. Wayinika ingxenye yefa lakhe. Sekuthi ngo-1818 wase efa umfundisi uWilliams. Ukuqhuba umsebenzi wakhe uNtsikana wakha esakhe isikolo eMankazana lapho ayeshumayela khona ukuba abanlu bayeke izindlela zosiko bathathe ezobukholwa. 
  Kukhona ingxenye yomlando kaNtsikana othi ukuguquka kukaNtsikana kwaqala bengakafiki abefundisi. Lo mlando uqhuba uthi ngelinye ilanga uNtsikana wabona umbani ubulala inkabi ayeyithanda. Ngalo futhi lelo langa wazama ukuya emgidini komunye umuzi samvimbezela isiphepho kwaze kwaba kathathu. 
Nokho waqhubekela phambili wafika sekugidwa. Wahlala 

isikhashana wabe esephuma ethi nomndeni wakhe awuphume engachazanga lutho kuwo. Wahamba waya emfuleni lapho ageza khona ubuso ekhuluma, "Kufanele abanlu bathandaze 
bangagidi." . . 
UNtsikana waba nemibono waprofetha. Uyena owabona ,mp' 

kaShaka iza izogwinya umbuso wakwaXhosa. Uyena owaprofetha impi yaseMalinde ngo-1818 phakathi kwamaNgqika namaNdlambe nokuthi abakwaNgqika bayokwehlulwa. Uyena owasho ukuthi kuningi ukonakala okuyoba khona: izingane ziyobhema, izizwe ziyovukelana zixabane kuze kugcine ngokuchitheka kwegazi; umame uyoxabana nendodakazi kanye nomakoti; indodana iyovukela uyise, umngane avukele umngani. Kodwa kuyothi ekugcineni kufike ukuthula. 
  Njengomeluleki wenkosi uNgqika, wathi uNgqika angangeni ezalulekweni zikamprofethi uNxele owayeqhatha impi. UNgqika akamlalelanga uNtsikana yize ayetsheliwe ukuthi uma engena empini uyokwehlulwa. Nebala yatholana ngo-1818 yehlulwa ngoJune ekaNgqika njengokusho kukaNtsikana. Ngo1819 uNtsikana nenkosi baphoqeleka ukuba bathuthe bayokwakha eThwathwa eduze neLushington. Lokhu kwadalwa ukufika kwabelungu ababezokwakha base bexosha abanlu ezindaweni zabo. UNtsikana nabanlu abaningi basuka bashiya amasimu bengavunanga. 
Wafika kule ndawo wagula kakhulu uNtsikana. Zonke

  Bathi beqambe befika abelungu ngo-1824 uShaka wayesakhe umbuso onamandla nowesatshwa yilo lonke izwe. Wawusuka ogwini IwaseMpumalanga kusukela oPhongolo unyuke uye ngaphesheya koThukela. Lo mbuso wasewaziwa ngaphesheya kwechibi iLake Victoria ubuqhawe bawo bufaniswa nowamaSparta kwelaseYurophu. Abaningi abalobi bayavuma ukuthi uShaka waqopha umlando kwezepolitiki yabansundu ngoba wakhuthaza izindlela ezintsha kwezepolitiki nokubuswa kwabantu. 
  Wayeyinkosi kwezombusazwe. Ngokufaka izinduna zakhe ezikhaliphile kanye namakhosi angaphansi kwakhe wenza ukuba izinjongo zakhe zazeke futhi zingabulawa yizenzo zemishoshaphansi. 
  Abalobi nezingcweti kwezombusazwe zimfanisa nabakhulu baseEurope oJulius Caesar noNapoleon Bonaparte kwezempi. Kuthi uma sebeloba ngekhono lakhe lokulandelanisa izinto (organizing ability) afaniswe noAlexander the Great bese kuthi uma kukhulunywa ngaye ngobuqotho ekuphatheni abantu (discipline) afaniswe noLycurgus (owakha umthetho oqinile wesizwe samaSpartans kanti futhi waduma ngokwakha uhulumeni wamaSpartans wabaqotho ezweni lamaGriki).

Laba lobi babethi uma beloba ngokuhlasela kukaShaka ebumba isizwe esisodwa esimnyama, bamfanise noAttila owaduma ngombuso oqinile ongenasihe.

UShaka wayemkhonze kakhulu unina ekhumbula 

ukuhlupheka kwabo bobabili behamba befuna indawo yokuhlala. Ukhula nje uShaka ukubona konke ukuhlupheka kukanina nemizamo kanina yokurnkhulisa. Noma esebusa akazange amkhohlwe unina ngoba azi ukuthi ukuba unina akamsingathanga wamkhulisa ubukhosi ngabe akabutholanga. Ngakho-ke bonke labo ababeqhuba ubutha obudala a.basinda~ga olakeni lwenhliziyo ebuhlungu kaShaka lapho eseshiywe uruna. Nokho wakhombisa ukulalela ngoba kwathi lapho emkhuza uGala iqhawe lakhe walalela lwehla ulaka. 
  Ubudlelwane bakhe nabelungu baba yinto enkulu eyokhunjulwa njalo. Abelungu bokuqala eFarewell noFyrm bamukelwa uye mathupha. Base beluzwile udumo lukaShaka. Wazilalela izinkulumo zabo lapho bexoxa ngelakubo, amakhosi abo nokuthuthuka kwabo. UShaka wabuka izibhamu, izevatho nokunye ababekuphethe, nokuthi babethuthukile ekwenzeni okuningi. Wavuma uShaka ukuba banikwe indawo eThekwini ngo-1824. Wayeqonde ukuba kube khona ubudlelwano phakathi kwabo noZulu ukuze noZulu akwazi ukucobele1a ulwazi abase benalo.

kweminingi imizi ngoNandi ngakho  

phakathi kombuso wakwaZulu nowarnaNgisi wathurnela inxusa lakhe uSotobe nabanye ukuba baye enkosini yamaNgisi bayokwakha ubuhlobo nobudlelwane. 

  USotobe neqembu lakhe basuka ngo-May ka-1828 'belibangise eNgiiandi ukuyobonana noKing George IV. Urnkhombindlela owayehamba nabo kwakungu J.5. King. Le njongo yokwakha ubuhlobo yabhuntsha ibhuntshiswa izikhulu zaseNgiiandi ePort Elizabeth. Zabaphatha kabi oSotobe zabahlalisa izinyanga ezintathu zibabuza irnibuzo engapheli. Waze wathukuthela uSotobe baqoqa okungokwabo babuyela ekhaya. Akakhombisanga ukuthukuthela uShaka ngokungaphurneleli kwale rnizamo kodwa kwahlala emqondweni wakhe insolo eyaphurna emazwini akhe okugcina rnhlazana efa. Akushiwo lapha ukuthi waze wafa uShaka engazange walwa nabelungu. 

  Sesishilo ukuthi befika abelungu ngo-1824 urnbuso wakwaZulu wase urnkhulu sewaziwa ngisho naphesheya kwezilwandle. Emva kokufa kukaNandi uShaka wathurnela enkulu impi iyohlasela uSoshangane (eRhodesia). Kule mpi kwakukhona abafowabo uDingane noMhiangana. Ngalesi sikhathi kwase kukhona ukukhononda ngombuso kaShaka phakathi kwabanye baseNdlunkulu. UDingane noMhiangana 
. bavurnelana endleleni ukuthi bazobuya abulaweuShaka. 
Nebala babuya bafica inkosi isesibayeni nezinye izinduna. 
Bayibulala bobathathu noMbopha kaSithayi. Wabuza ukuthi bambulalelani kodwa akekho owaphendula. UShaka wakhulurna amazwi uZulu angawakhohlwa nanamuhla wathi:. "Nibulala rnina-nje ngeke nilibuse ziyeza izinkonjane zezulu yizona eziyokulibusa." 
   Yize uShaka abusa irninyaka eyishurni kuphela udurno lwakhe lwanda urnhlaba wonke ngisho naphesheya kwezilwandle. Amanye arnakhosi ayekhulurna ngarnandla akhe. Ukubusa nobuqotho bakhe abukhanganga amanye amakhosi kuphela. Abalobi bezinkondlo bezinhlanga ezahlukene baloba ngoShaka. Abalob! bezornlando baloba ngoShaka; abalobi bezindaba zabantu abaziwayo ernhlabeni abarnshiyi uShaka; abalobi bernidlalo yaseSteji (drama) bayaloba ngoShaka; abadwebi abarnshiyi uShaka; abalobi barnaphephandaba bayaloba 
44 
, 
J 
55. 
. ngoShaka; abaqarnbi bamaculo bayalutusa udurno lukaShaka. . Izikhulurni eziqavile emphakathini ziyakhulurna ngoShaka. 
Bakhona abalobi ikakhulukazi abarnhlophe abangazange babone ubuhle kuShaka kepha babona ububi bodwa. 

  Iqiniso ukuthi irnisebenzi nempilo yakhe uShaka yenza izinhlobonhlobo zabalobi bathande ukuloba ngaye. Abanye babuza urnbuzo othi: Uma uShaka kwabe kungurnbulali omkhulu, wayengawuqamba kanjani urnbuso wezizwe ezahlukene phansi kwesandla sikaZulu? 

  Ake silobe ukuthi yimaphi arnabutho ayenawo uShaka asakhurnbuleka kwawesilisa nawesifazane. Nanka awesilisa: arnaWombe, isiKiebe, uKhokhothi, uMbelebele, iziMpohlo, . iziNyosi, uFasimba, amaPhela, isiPhezi, uDlangezwa, uMbonarnbi, uNteke, uMgurnanqa, iziKhwembu, amaKhwenkwe, uNomdayana, iNdabankulu, uGibabanye, uFojisa, iMfolozi. Sotobe KaMpangalala 

"Undaba zingaphesheya kolwandle" 

USotobe kaMpangalala wakwaGazu kwaSibiya wayengowendlu yasebukhosini bakwaSibiya. Noma kungatholakali kahle ukuthi wazalwa nini ngempela uNdlunkulu uMkabi uthi wathi egcagca uSotobe wayesengumfanyana kungaziwa ukuthi uyena wokuqala eMzansi Afrika oyohamba olwandle engumkhulumeli wombuso kaZulu elibangise enkosini yamaNgisi uJoji. Asizwa lutho futhi ngokukhula kwakhe kodwa kwakungehlukile kakhulu kwabanye abafana. Akekho owayazi ukuthi esekhulile uyoba yinduna nomholi wempi phansi kwengcweti enjengenkosi uShaka. 
  USotobe waziwa kakhulu ngokuba umholi weqembu likaHulumem kaShaka elathunyelwa phesheya ukuyokwakha ubudlelwano noHulumeni wamaNgisi. Yinto eyabingakaze yenzeke eMzansi Afrika ukuba uHulumeni wokudabuka awele izilwandle ayothi akuhlaliswane ngokuthula lokhu abathi namhlanje phecelezi "peaceful co-existence". 
  Kuthiwa uSotobe wayemkhulu futhi esukile lapha emhlabathini noma edla imbuzi yayingelutho kuye wena owabona uManyosi kaDlekezele. 
  Kwathi noma engasekho uShaka uSotobe wahlala ernzini kaDingane eMgungundlovu eyala inkosi uDingane. Ngale nkathi wayesaziwa ngokuthi uyise wenkosi ngezeluleko zakhe. lndodana yakhe yokuqala kubo bonke abafazi bakhe kwaba nguNobiya. Asisho lapha ukuthi ngenxa yomqondo wakhe ojulile akukho okwakuxoxwa ngezinto ezisemqoka engekho uSotobe yize wayengesona isikhulumi. 
  Siz0t.hi fahla fahla ngesimo sezinto kwaZulu ngale nkathi nangeslmo samazwe ayesondelene noZulu. Abamhlophe base

  Ngale nkathi kwakusafike abelungu bokuqala bafika nenduku eyisimanga oyikhomba esitheni bese udonsa insinjana encane isitha silale phansi sife ungakafiki eduze. Bakhuluma-ke bekhuluma nangengomuso lombuso kaZulu. Kwavunyelwana lapha ukuthi kudingeka kwenziwe izinto ezimbili ezisemqoka. 
  Okokuqala ukuba kuvikelwe imincele yombuso ukuze izitha zingangeni kalula. Okwesibili kwaba ukwandisa nokuqinisa impi (isenzo esagcina sesenza ukuba uShaka bamgxeke abanye ngokuthi kwakuvivwa kakhulu abesilisa bengasakwazi ukuhlala emakhaya.)

Ukuba khona kwamaNgisi namaBhunu eduzane kombuso wakwaZulu akwenzanga inhlalo kaZulu inethezeke. AmaBhunu abona izwe lakwaZulu akholwa ukuthi ukulambela kwawo izwe angase asuthe uma ethola elakwaZulu. 
  AmaNgisi wona ayehalela ukulithatha elakwaZulu alifake phansi kombuso wawo khona kuzoqina umbuso wamaNgisi eMzansi Afrika. Ngo-1842 uHulumeni wamaNgisi wenza iNatali ukuba ibe phansi kombuso wawo. 
  Khona la ngaphakathi kwaZulu kwakukhona nomoya woqhekeko nakhu phela abanye basakhala esikaDingane. Noma kungabanga kuhle ukuba amaNgisi ebesethi indawo esukela oThukela kuya eMfolozi eMnyarna eyawo ngalolu hlelo wasala esethula uMpande. NamaNgisi awazange asheshe ukususa abantu kule ndawo. 
  Selokhu iNatali yathathwa arnaNgisi ukungezwani namaBhunu kwaqhubeka. Inkosi uMpande yena wazenzela ubudlelwano obuhle kuwo womabili la maqembu. Wayengaqonde chuku. ngokuthi amaJingqi babentshontsha izinkomo emapulazini abamhlophe eduzane nemifula iKoonap neBaviaans. Kwaba' nesikhalo sokuthi umuzi kaMaqoma useduze kakhulu nabelungu. Sekuthi-ke ngo-1822 sekwakhiwa inqaba iFort Beaufort ukuze kugadwe abantu ababede behlasela abamhlophe, ' noMaqoma asuswe endaweni ayenikwe yona, Phezu kwalokhu, uTyhali, umfowabo omncane kaMaqoma, waliphaka iqembu .' lakhe wahlasela indawo lapho kususwe khona uMaqoma (neutral area) wase akha neqembu lakhe ngaphesheya komfula iMancazana. 
	Uthuthuva 	phakathi 	kwabansundu 	nabamhlophe 
Iwahebhetheka kwathi ngo-1823 abalimi abamhlophe balalekelwa kakhulu eziwombeni zokulwa. Abamhlophe baqoqana bakha elikhulu iviyo elahlasela labhubhisa imizi kaMaqoma ngoDecember zinhlanu. Kwathunjwa izinkomo eziyizinkulungwane eziyisikhombisa zikaMaqoma zayiswa eFort Beaufort. 
  Emveni kokuba abalimi sebekhokhelwe ihIawulo labo uMaqoma wabuyiselwa izinkomo ezingu 5200. Ngesikhathi inkosi uShaka enyakazisa izwe kakhulu eminyakeni ka-1827 no1828 uMaqoma wasuka wayocasha endaweni yaseWaterkloof eduze nomfula iKat. Ukwenza lokhu ngoba ebona ukuthi abakwaNgqika base beqala ukukhathala kwezempi. Wathi uqala unyaka ka-1829 zingu-21 kuJanuary wayithela impi yakhe uMaqoma phezu kwabaThembu bengazelele. Wathumba izinkomo eziyizinkulungwane ezintathu wabuye wabuyisela eyodwa inkulungwane. Umnurnzane uSir Lowry Cole owayengungqongqoshe waseKoloni kusukela ku-1772 kuya ku-1842 wanquma ukuthi kufanele ajeziswe uMaqoma axoshelwe ngaphesheya komngcele. Kwaba isicelo esilukhuni lesi ngoba ukuthathwa kwezwe likaMaqoma phesheya komfula iKat nokuthunjwa kwezinkomo zakhe kwakhombisa ukuthi indlela yokuthula ivaliwe. Okokhela umlilo kwaba urnthetho obandlululayo kaHulurneni wamaNgisi wokuthi njalo amacala ayelahla abansundu kujeziswe bona hhayi abamhlophe. Yathungeleka kanjalo impi eyasuka ngo-1834 yaphela ngo-1835 eyaziwa ngokuthi Sixth Frontier War. 
  Zazingu-12 kuOecember ngo-1834 lapho impi yakwaXhosa yatheleka eKoloni ibulala konke ehlangana nakho kusuka. eSomerset East kuya phansi e-Algoa Bay. Le mpi kakhukhulelangoqo yathi urna ifika ezintabeni zaseWinterberg yazithela kwekaPiet Relief, yabuyela emuva yathi ingena eGrahamstown yathola ukuthi uCharies Somerset useyilindele. Kwathunyelwa usizo oluphuthurnayo kulo lonke izwe ngisho naphesheya. Lwafika usizo bayidudula eyakwaXhosa kwaba ukwehlulwa kwayo. 
  Kwaphela izinyanga eziyisithupha iphelile Ie mpi wafa uHintsa ngo-1835. UHulurneni wamaNgisi wamemezela ukuthi lonke izwe likaHintsa kusuka eCiskei kuze kufike eKeiskamma sekungelamaNgisi. Khona manjalo isizwe samaMfengu esasikule ndawo sasuselwa eduzane neFort Peddie. 
  UHulurneni wamaNgisi wamemezela futhi ukuthi wonke amaXhosa asengaphansi kombuso wamaNgisi. Umholi wezempi uLiet. Col. H.G. Smith akazange amethembe uMaqoma, esho nokuthi "uyisigcwelegcwele esinenkani nonya" (remorseless and relentless savage). 
  Ngomhlaka-17 enyangeni kaSeptember ngo-1835 kwavunyeIwana ngoxolo kwase kuqoqwa amakhosi akhonjiswa imingcele yezindawo zawo. USmith yena njengoMongameli weKoloni wabusa iCiskei kwase kuthi uMaqoma noTyhali noMhlala benziwa izimantshi. Ngalesi sikhathi ungqongqoshe weKoloni kwaku uSir Benjamin O'Urban owaqamba i"Province of Queen Adelaide". wathurnela isinqurno kuO'Urban. Lesi sinqurno sasithi akasheshe abuyisele indawo i"Province of Queen Adelaide" kubanikazi amaXhosa. Isinqurno sakhishwa zingu-26 kuOecember 1835 saze safika kuO'Urban zingu-21 enyangeni kaMarch ngo-1836.

urnbuso kaStockenstrom waba nempatho enobunlu kuMaqoma namanye amakhosi. UStockenstrom walandelwa uLieut-Col. John Hare. yokuphila kwaphesheya. Naye uMaqoma wadela konke ukuze ahIenge isizwe sakhe kulo mkhankaso owabe unamandla amakhulu. UMaqoma wangena kuyo ngokungabaza, sekuthi enyangeni kaSeptember kwaba uyena inkosi yokuqala eyacela uxolo. Akazange akunake Iokhu uSir Harry Smith, waqhubeka nempi kwaze kwathi zingu-17 kuOecember ka-1847 kwaba yima ememezela ukuvuma uxolo.   Ekuhoxiseni kwakhe uMaqoma empini wanikezwa indlu' encane eLovedale lapho ahlala khona namakhosikazi akhe. Ngo1848, isiphelile irnpi, wasuswa eLovedale nomuzi wakhe' wabuyiselwa lapho ekade akhe khona eduze nornfula iTyhume. 
  Arnakhosi ahIala engathokozanga ngokuthenwa kwamandla awo. Unyaka ka-1850 waletha ukornisa okukhulu okwenza ukuthi nokuthukuthela kwamakhosi ngempatho yarnaNgisi kuqhubeke.

NoMaqorna wabona ukuthi ngabe akwenziwa lutho urna belokhu bekhononda wase engena shiqe empini enkulu eyaqala ngo-1850 yaze yaphela ngo-l853. Le mpi yaziwa ngokuthi i"Eight Frontier War". Yahlasela ekaMaqoma yanqoba iBiinkwater, yadlula yanqoba iWaterkloof, yedlulela eKroome, zonke kuyizindawo eziseduzane nezintaba iWinterberg. Yadlula lapho ihamba i1wa ngokukhulu ukuzirnisela yaqonda eCradock naseSomerset East. Okwakunguyena owayephaka impi kwakunguMaqorna uqobo, uSandile wayekhuthaza ngesikhundla sakhe. Kwaphela izinyanga eziyisithupha ibambene phezulu ilwa kakhulukazi ezinqabeni ezazisentabeni. Ekugcineni amakhosi amaRarabe acela uxolo. Kwaphinda futhi kwaba uye uMaqoma owacela uxolo kuSir George Cathcart owayesebusa iKoloni ngalesi sikhathi. 
  Okokuqala akwenza uCathcart ukudingisa abakwaNgqika abasuse eWinterberg naseMatola abase ngaphesheya kornfula iKabousie. Urnholi waseKoloni uSir George Grey wenza olunye uhIelo nokubusa abakwaXhosa. Yileyo naleyo nkosi yaba nemantshi endaweni yayo ukuze konke okwenziwa yinkosi ikudlulise kuqala emantshini. 
  Kwaba lukhuni ukuba amakhosi abhunge ahlangane ngoba izirnantshi kwakufanele zazi konke okwenziwayo zithurnele irnibiko kuSir George Grey. Wayeyinkosi yesizwe samaHlubi esasakhe endaweni noMtshezi (Estcourt) yaziwa ngokuthi iWeenen eNatali. Kulinga-niselwa ukuthi uLangalibalele wazalwa ngo-1818 ezalelwa esigodini saseUtrecht eNatali. Yena-ke wabayindodana yesithathu kwayisihlanu kaMthimkhulu, indlalifa kaBhungane Hlubi. Unina yayeyindodakazi kaMashoba inkosi yaMangwe. Abazali bakhe bametha igama elithi Langalibalele ngoba wazalwa ngesikhathi esinzima lomisile kunendlala. 

  AmaHlubi ayehlala esigodini esiseduze neUtrecht ekuqaleni kuka 1800. Sekuthi ngo-1818, unyaka azalwa ngawo uLangalibalele, amaHlubi asede ehlaselwa amaNgwane nezizwana ezincane zabeSuthu. Nawo amaHlubi aselokhu ehamba efuna izindawo ezingcono ezingenalo uthuthuva. Ngale nkathi amaHlubi ayengenawo amandla okulwa nalezi zizwe.

, Yafika ekaLangalibalele engasekho esebalekele kwelabeSuthu wakhonza enkosini uMolapo. Injongo kwabe kungtlkuvala izikhala zokubaleka (passes) ezintabeni zoKhahiamba. UTheophilus Shepstone owayengunobhala wakwaNdabazabantu walandelwa ngumfowabo uJohn W. Shepstone. ULangalibalele wenza ukuba uZibuse wabamhlophe eNatali uthi ukuma isikhashana ngenxa yenguquko eyafika noSir Gamet Wolseley 0.wayezongamela iNatali. Umthetho wokudingiswa kukaLangalibalele eRobben Island awuvunywanga uHulumeni phesheya ngoba kunezinsolo zokuthi awuhambanga ngendlela efanele kanti futhi nalokhu kudingiswa kwakungadingekile. Ukuphathwa kabi kukaLangalibalele kwaqeda ubuhlobo obabusaphembeka phakathi kukaCetshwayo noShepstone. Izicelo zikaCetshwayo ukuba uLangalibalele abuyiswe phansi kwakhe zathalala waze wahanjiswa uLangalibalele. 
  ULangalibalele yena wasuswa esiqhingini wabo.shelwa eKoloni ngo-1875. Futhi kwabe sekuvunywa ukuthi e~ye yamakhosikazi akhe nabanye abantu bayohlala naye. Kwathi-ke ngo-1877 wadedelwa wabuyela eNatali wahlala eduze kwendawo yakhe endala. 
  Wayengasaphilile kahle uLangalibalele kwagcina ngokuba.afe ngo-1889. Ithuna lakhe laba umhlanganisi-maHlubi ngoba nJalo ngonyaka ebehlangana khona ~ukhonza nokukl:!ule~a ~thuneni lenkosi eyamela isizwe sayo nglsho nasekuboshweru. ISlthombe sakhe esathathwa nguS.B. Barnard ngenkathi uLangalibalele eseCape Town sikhona eCory Library eGrahamstown eKoloni. Iphepha iSlar ka-9. 3. 1967linaso futhi isithombe sakhe.

kaMpande abuthwa ebuthweni uThulwana. 

  Waqala ukulwa impi yokuqala uCetshwayo mhIa uMpande ehlasela arnaSwazi. Wakhula uCetshwayo ehlala ernzini waseKubazeni enabantu abaningi abafika ukurnkhornbisa ukuthi bayafisa athathe isikhundla sikayise. Ngokunjalo kwakukhona abeqernbu likaMbuyazi. Iqernbu likaCetshwayo lase laziwa ngokuthi uSuthu kanti elikaMbuyazi kuyiziGqoza. UMbuyazi wazarna ukuhlasela uCetshwayo ngoDecernber ka-1856 yatholana ernpini yaseNdondakusuka wafa uMbuyazi narnaningi arnabutho. UCetshwayo wayehola uphiko oluphakathi eeeleni kungurnfowabo (rnzala) uHharnu olunye uphiko kungurnlungu uChristian Groening. 
  Kusukela ngalesi sikhathi uCetshwayo waba nesandla ernbusweni, lwanda udurno lwakhe. Wadurna ngobuqhawe, ngobuhlakani nangobuholi obuqotho. Ukungaphili kahle. kwenkosi uMpande kwenza ukuba uCetshwayo enze urnsebenzi wenkosi isaphila. Kwakhiwa ubudlelwano noHulurneni warnaNgisi ukuze asize ernbangweni kaZulu narnaBhunu. Urnphurnela walokhu kwaba ukufika kukaNobhala wakwaNdabazabantu waseNatali uTheophilus Shepstone (uSorntsewu) kwaZulu. 
  Wafika ngo-1861 wabika ukuthi uHulurneni wakhe uyokwarnukela uCetshwayo njengenkosi yakwaZulu ernva kukaMpande. Wafa uMpande ngo-October 1872. . 
  Ziningi-ke izinkinga abhekana nazo uCetshwayo ekuthatheni kwakhe ubukhosi. Ukungezwani phakathi kwakhe uZulu kwakungakapheli ngoba babesekhona ababekhala esikaMbuyazi; arnaBhunu eNtilasifali ayelokhu ezarna ukuthola ingxenye yezwe lakwaZulu; uHulurneni waseNatali naye wayekhornbisa ukuhalela ukuthatha elakwaZulu libe phansi kornbuso warnaNgisi. 
  Inkosi yacela uSorntsewu ukuba axazulule inkinga phakathi kwayo noZulu. Waphuthurna uSorntsewu wayogcoba uCetshwayo ukuba abeyinkosi yakwaZulu ngo-Septernber 1, 1873. Lokhu ukwenzanje ngoba ebona ithuba lokuba arnaNgisi angene kwaZulu. Isikhathi u-1873 kuya ku-1879 eNatali sasiguquguqulwa isirno sikaHulurneni warnaNgisi phesheya. 
74 

. Wangena ebuholini barnaNgisi ngo-1874 uDisraeli waqlrusa ukuthi uHulurneni wakhe uzirnisele ukwandisa urnbuso wakhe , 'ngaphandle kwaseNgilandi. Phezu kwalokhu ornunye wabaholi barnaNgisi wayesernbikela uHulurneni ukuthi kungakuhle arnazwe aseNingizimu Afrika ahlanganiswe phansi kornbuso warnaNgisi. 
. Lokhu kusho ukuthi anqotshwe bese ebuswa norna azihlanganise noHulurneni warnaNgisi (confederation). Inkosi uCetshwayo wayezirnisele ukusebenza ngokuthula narnaNgisi kodwa engazirnisele ukufakwa phansi kornbuso warnaNgisi. Kuze kube yilesi sikhathi urnbuso wakwaZulu wawusazimele yize wawuhaqwe iziharnbi ezimhlophe nazo kwathatha isikhathi ukuba zihlasele uZulu. Irnpilo yakwaZulu nezornnotho kwakubanelisile abantu futhi bedayiselana nabahwebi. ArnaNgisi ayengenerne ngokuba khona kukaHulurneni warnaBhuni eNtilasifali. Uhulurneni warnaNgisi wakhetha uSorntsewu ukuba abhekane nenkinga yaseNtilasifali. Akabuzanga uSorntsewu ngo-April 12, 1877 uSorntsewu warnernezela ukuthi iNtilasifali isiphansi kornbuso warnaNgisi yena uSorntsewu uzongarnela iNtilasifali. Sekuthi ngoba uSorntsewu efuna usizo IwarnaBhunu ukuthola elakwaZulu useya kwaZulu eyokhulurna ngokubangwa kornngcele phakathi kukaZulu narnaBhunu. 
USorntsewu wancenga izithunywa zenkosi ukuba zivurnele arnaBhunu ukuba ingxenye yakwaZulu ebangwayo anikwe yona. 
Izithunywa zenkosi sezibubonile ubuxoki bukaSorntseu othi urna epharnbi kwenkosi abe urnngani ayithernbise usizo kodwa kuthi urna ingekho ayidayise. Zarntshela ernehlweni konke lokhu wacasuka uSorntsewu washiya umhlangano. 
Asisho lapha ukuthi ngale nkathi uSir Bartle Frere wasethunyelwe ukuba uNgqongqoshe ornele iNgilandi kulo lonke laseMzansi Afrika. Wayethunyelwe ukuba angenise wonke uMzansi Afrika phansi kornbuso warnaNgisi.' Kwarnkhayela uFrere ukuthi urnbuso wakwaZulu akekho ongawuthinta. Wayesethola icebo lokubhixa inkosi noZulu ezincwadini ayezilobela uHulurneni waphesheya. Lo rnbhixo wawuthi

Eziningi izincwadi ayezibhala zazigxeka uCetshwayo zimthwesa amacala amabi kuthiwa wuye osukela amaBhunu. NgoJanuary 1878 uSomtsewu waloba ende incwadi esho ukuthi ukudedelwa kukaCetshwayo nombuso wakwaZulu kuyingozi enkulu kumlungu nombuso wamaNgisi eNingizimu Afrika. Washo nokusho ukuthi uma amabutho kaCetshwayo engaguqulwa abe izisebenzi izwe lakwaZulu lingathuthuka. 
  Kwamkhanyela noCetshwayo ukuthi uSomtsewu akathembekile, wayesezama ukukhuluma nezinye izikhulu ngoba engalufuni uthuthuva. Ngokuqhubeka kwezohwebo zangena izibhamu kwaZulu zidayiswa kakhulu umlungu uJantoni Oohn Dunn) owayengunobhala nomeluleki wenkosi, futhi eseze wenziwa enye yamakhosi akwaZulu. Ngale nkathi uCetshwayo wayesakhe omunye umuzi awubiza ngokuthi Mayizekanye.

IKhornishani yethula umbiko wayo ngoJune 1878. Kwathi ngoba iKhornishani isekela uCetshwayo uFrere akaze awushicilela umbiko ukuze wazeke kabanzi. Esikhundleni salokho waqhubeka naye nokubhixa uCetshwayo ezincwadini ayezilobela phesheya esho nokusho ukuthi sesifikile isikhathi sokuba kube khona okwenziwayo.

  Wangena eyunivesithi yaseGlasgow ngo-1851 kwathi ngo1852 waqala izifundo zobufundisi eTheological Hall ye-United Presbyterian Church e-Edinburgh. Waphothula izifundo zakhe ngo-1856, kwathi ayefunda nabo bamupha ibhuku elilotshwe amagama abo bonke, bekhombisa ubunye ayebumele uTiyo. 
Waba ngowokuqala ukugcotshwa phesheya abe ngumfundisi.

Kulinganiselwa ukuthi uMokone wazalwa ngoJune 1851 eBokgaga eNtilasifali. Uyise wafa empini yamaSwazi ngo-1863. Wakhula engazange alithole ilhuba lokuya esikoleni.   Ngo-1873 wabe eseqashwa ngokugcwele ekolishi iLovedale. wagcina esebe ngumgcini mabhuku  nomphathi wezimali ezikhokhwayo  . 

  Ngokunakekela izinto kanye nokwethembeka wafundiswa ukuphatha izingcingo zikathelefoni kathi kuzothi ngesikhathi '. sezinxushunxushu asize ngokuthurnela izingcingo ezindaweni .. eziningi. Uyena owaphatha isiteshi sezingcingo les( kwaze kwaba ngu-1874. 

  OkaBokwe waqala izingoma ngo-1875 akaze akhathala, walokhu eqhubekile kwezomculo. Wayenesineke uBokwe futhi enomqondo ojulile. MhIawurnbe lesi sineke wasitholiswa. ukukhula kanzima. Wasebenza esemncane ehola u-25c ngenyanga. Izincwadi ezalotshwa ayebasebenzela zatusa ukukhuthala kwakhe emsebenzini, ukuzinikela emsebenzini, ukuzwana kwakhe nabantu asebenza nabo. Ngokwethemba uDr. Stewart wamenza isekela lakhe eLovedale. Kwathi noma . abahwebi abaziwayo befuna ukurnqasha ngemali engaphezu kweyaseLovedale, ngekhono lakhe ekugcineni amabhuku, wala uBokwe wakhetha ukusiza iLovedale. Yakhula nakuye imali wagcina esehola u-R200 ngenyanga. 

  Sesishilo sathi kwezomculo wayedla ubhedu futhi ezifundisela yena ukucula. Ukwenza konke lokhu nje kuningi akwenzayo lapha eLovedale. Uyena owengamele ikhwaya lasekolishi, engamele izingcingo, asize ekufundiseni, asize emidlalweni yekolishi. Waba yingxenye yeLovedale. Wawu-'_ ngeke usasho ukuthi yilowaya John Knox owayengene eLovedale Primary School eneminyaka eyishumi. 

  Ngonyaka ka-1892 uBokwe wavakashela phesheya eScotiand lapho akhanga khona abaningi ngokuhlabelela izingoma ezaziqanjwe wuye. Abathatheka kakhulu kwaba abefundisi abakhuthazeka ukuba bazosiza ukuthuthukisa amathalente omdabu aseAfrika. Wabuya uBokwe esethole oluningi ulwazi kwezomculo kanye nakwezenkolo. Phela uya phesheya nje ubesengurnvangeli owaziwayo webandla lePresbyterum. Waqhubeka nokusebenza eLovedale nokushurnayela emphaka- 
96 
103. 
thini. 

  Kwathi ngo-1897 wavalelisa eLovedale emva kokuphatha izingcingo zakhona nokwengamela iposi irninyaka engu-24. Waba ngomunye kwabambalwa phakathi kwabamhlophe nabansundu abatuswa urnongameli jikelele wamaposi eNingizimu Afrika. Watuswa kakhulu ngokuzinikela, nokwethembeka, nokukhuthala emsebenzini wakhe.

Wahamba irninyaka emibili kusuka ku-1900 kuya ku-1901. Wabuya ekhaya wasebenza njengomvangeli waze wagcotshwa ngo-1906. "Imvo" yangena shi kwezombusazwe ngenxa yesimo

sokuphathwa kwabansundu. Ngemisebenzi kaJabavu, inkosi uSigeawu owayethweswe kala lokuvukela umbuso (High Treason) wagwetshelwa eRobben Island iminyaka eyishumi, lachithwa kala inkantolo enkulu (Supreme Court) eCape Town. 
  Phakathi kweminyaka 1878 no-1880 abansundu bezwa ubunZima obukhulu, kwaphuma umthetho owaziwa ngokuthi Disarmament Act owaphoqela abantu ukuba izikhali zabo zaziwe uhulumeni noma bephuewe; wonke umuntu wesilisa kwathiwa makaphathe ipasi aboshwe uma engaliphethe; ukudayisa kOlshwala besilungu kwaqhubeka ngendlela emangalisayo; kulesi sikhathi kwaphumelela umthetho othi umuntu angephucwa ubuzwe bakhe uma uhulumeni wamaNgisi ekholwa ukuthi lokhu kufanele. UJabavu walwa nale mithetho waze waphumelela ukuba umthetho wokuphuea abamnyama ubuzwe babo uguqulwe. Uyohlala ekhunjulwa futhi uJabavu ngoba wamisa umthetho owawususa abaTembu ezweni labo elaziwa kobelungu ngokuthi iGlen Grey. UJabavu wakhononda kakhulu ephepheni lakhe ngesihluku salo mthetho waze waguqulwa. Futhi nguye uJabavu owasiza ekukhululweni 0 kwamakhosi ayevalelwe eRobben Island ngoba kuthiwa azama 00 ukuvukela umbuso wamaNgisi. La makhosi kwakungoTini Maqoma, Gungubele Matanzima, Edmund Sandile, Gumna kanye nabanye ababili. UJabavu kanye noRose Innes babeka kala ezandleni zikaNdunankulu owabona ukuthi la makhosi awanaeala wawakhipha ngo-1888. 
  Ngonyaka ka-1896 kwaqubuka isifo esabulala ezmmgi izinkomo esaziwa ngokuthi uLandapense (Rinderpest). Lesi sifo ? senza ukuthi izikhulu zikahulumeni zenze umthetho owathi' izinkomo ezinalesi sifo kufanele zidutshulwe. Kwatholakala ukuthi izindawo ezibalwayo ezabansundu. UJabavu wakhwela 0 wadilika kulo mthetho waze wahoxiswa. ~ 
  Uyena futhi uJabayu owazabalazela ingxenye kaMzilikazi ezimpini zeminyaka ka-1893 no-1896 kanye nempi kaBhambatha ngo-1906 necala elathweswa inkosi uDinuzulu. Waloba kabanzi ekhombisa umqondo wabamhlophe owawuqonde ukulimaza abansundu. Kwezobandlululo uJabavu wakhipha amangwevu asakhunjulwa nanamhlanje. Wayeluzonda ubandlululo engaze- 

106 

nzisi. Waze wasungula inhlangano eyaziwa ngokuthi "Imbumba Yezizwe" eyakhula yaba ingxenye yenhlangano yomhlaba i'Universal Race Congress' eyahlangana eLondon ngo-I911. UJabavu wathunyelwa ukumela abansundu kule nhIangano. 
  Kukho konke okuhle akwenza uJabavu ezamela isizwe esinsundu, wenza iphutha elaguqula isimo sempilo yakhe. Wavikela, welekelela uSavers emthethweni we "Natives Land Act" ka-1913. Lo mthetho wawuqonde ukuba abansundu bancishwe umhlaba ezweni lomdabu. Yiwo 10 mthetho owanikeza abamhlophe ingxenye enkulu yezwe, kwasekuthi abansundu babelwa ingxenye eneane. Iphepha 'Imvo' laduma ngokuthi lilekelela uHulumeni kwaduma nokuthi naye umhleli walo unjalo. Kusukela ngalesi sikhathi igama likaJabavu lafanekiswa nelabagqilazi. 
  Ngaphandle kokulahlekelwa igama emphakathini wehlelwa izigigaba ezingezinhle kulesi sikhathi uJabavu: Ngo-1900 kwashona inkosikazi yakhe eyabe imsize kakhulu kukho konke ayekwenza. Yamshiya namadodana amane. Kwathi sekuphele izinyanga eziyisithupha ishonile inkosikazi yakhe waganwa uGertrude Joninga waseKnappes Hope Mission eduze naseKing Williamstown. 
  Ngesikhathi sempi yamabhunu namaNgisi, iphepha 'Imvo' lavalwa ngomthetho wezimpi owathi uJabavu wayelwa nezempi kusuka phansi engafuni kuliwe. Kwaphinda futhi ngoAugust 1901 kuya kuOctober 1902, yavalwa futhi 'Imvo'. Lokhu kwandisa ezinkulu izindleko. Phezu kwalezi zinkinga zephepha, 

* omabhalane baqhamuka nokukhulu ukungathembeki nobu. tsotsi. Umsebenzi wakhe wagulisa umphefumulo wakhe ikakhulu ngoba wayesengene ezikweletini ezinkulu ezama ukuthi iphepha lingawi. v:'azalwa ngo-1861 . en?aweni yaseMphahlele esigodini sasePletersburg eNtilaslfall. Wayeyindodana kaKgorutte Josiah Makgatho inkosi yesizwe saMakgatho. Waqala ukufunda eduzane nasekhaya waqhubeka waze wafunda imfurido ephak~me ekholiji laseKilnerton ePitoli. Leli kholiji lasungulwa abaholi besonto l~seWeseli ukuthuthukisa izinga lernfundo ng.okuqeqes~a othisha eNtilasifali. Wakhombisa ukukhalipha eZl~dweru zakhe kwathi lapho eqeda izifundo zakhe eKiln~.~ton wa~ola urnfundaze wokuya phesheya. Wafunda ekhohj1 lase-Ealmg eliseMiddiesex eNgilandi. Wafunda lapha kusukela ngo-1882 kuya ku-1885. Waqinisa kakhulu kwezenkolo nezokufundisa. 
  Wabuya phesheya wa~disa eKilnerton kusukela ngo-1887 kuy~ ku-1906. Ngesikhathi efundisa lapha waqamba inhlangano yothi~ha ,;yaziwa. ngokuthi "!'ransvaal African Teachers' Assoclatwn o~athi e~va kwernmyaka yaba inhlangano esemqoka phakathi kweZ1nhlangano eMzansi Afrika. Wasebenza kakhulu ezama ukuba kuthuthuke izinga lernfundo kwa: bansund~. Wa~ angayeka ukufundisa wangenela umsebenzi wokudaytsa lZ1ndawo ngoba efisa ukuba kube yilowo muntu abenawo urnhlaba azozibiza ngawo. 
  UMakgatho walubona usizi Iwabantu bakubo bengenawo amalungelo athize ngenxa yobandlululo. Wakholwa ukuthi kudingeke kakhulu ukuba abantu bahlangane bahlele kahle izindlela zokulwela amalungelo abo nobuntu babo. Ngo-1906 wasungula Inhlangano eyabizwa ngokuthi i"Transvaal Native Political Union". UMakgatho waba urnongameli wale nhlangano 
118 

kusukela ngo-1906 kuya ku-1908. Waphurnelela ukuba Ie nhlangano yakhe ibe nobunye ne"Transvaal Native Congress" waba urnongameli wayo kusuka ngo-1912 kuya ku-1930. Emva kwesikhathi Ie nhlangano yabizwa ngokuthi "African National 
Congress" . 
UMakgatho ebona izinjongo, irnibono nernisebenzi ye ANC 

kufuneka yaziwe kabanzi nokuthi indlela yokwenza loku ukuba kulotshwe njalo ephepheni, wazinikela ukuba abambisane no Alfred Mangena ekushicileleni iphepha elaziwa ngokuthi "Native Advocate" Emva kwesikhathi wasiza ekusunguleni iphepha "Abantu-Batho" Wawenza 10 msebenzi kusukela ku- 
1912 kuya ku-1914. 
Ngonyaka ka-1917 wakhethwa waba urnongameli ka-ANC 

esikhundleni sikaJ.L. Dube omqondo wakhe wawungasathandeki kubalandeli mayelana nokuthi u-ANC kufanele enzenjani ngomthetho wornhlaba wabantu. 
  UMakgatho wahlala irninyaka engu-7 ehola i-ANC efaka urnoya wokukhuthala. Wayengumshumayeli waseWeseli into eyasiza futhi ukuba athinte abaningi. NjengoClements Kadalic. UMakgatho wayekholwa ukusebenzisa izinkantolo ukulwela amalungelo abansundu. Ngesikhathi sayo i-ANC yaphumelela emacaleni amaningi ngisho nelokuvikela intela ye-Pol Tax. 
  Wabuye walwa futhi nomthetho owawusungulwa ukuthi abesifazane mabaphathe amapasi. Umbhikisho aba nawo waba owezitimela. Abakaloliwe abazinakanga izicelo zokuba izitimela zandiswe ukuze bahambe kahle bangarninyani. Sekuthi ngelinye ilanga abanye abantu bazinikela bangena ezinqoleni zabelungu. Leli cala lathalala. Ngo-1919 waphurnelela ukuba izikhulu zasePitoli zivurne ukuba amaNdiya abenalo ilungelo lokuvula izitolo edolobheni. Ekuqaleni kuka-1930 kuye phakathi ka-1940 wayekhona kuKhongolose. Waqala waba urngcini zirnali phansi kukamongameli uSeme, emuva kwalokho wasiza uKhongolose 
waseGoli. 
UMakgatho wabuye waba ilungu lengqungquthela eyabizwa 
uHulurneni yaziwa ngokuthi "Government Native Conference". Waloba inewadi enesihloko esithi "Seven Days in Hospital". 
Abanye baye baphosise bathi igama likaMakgatho uSamuel.

akhulume njengesazi nesijundiswa".

Nazaretha. Umfundisi owalandela umfundisi uIsaiah, wavuma ukuthi amaNazaretha angajova agcabe futhi. Wavuma emva kwezicelo eziningi zikaHulumeni ukuba axegise umthetho webandla mayelana nokugcaba nokujova. 

  AmaNazaretha anernikhosi yokukhonza. Kukhona emibili emikhulu eyenziwa njalo ngonyaka. Kukhona umkhosi omkhulu owenziwa ngenyanga kaJanuary. Amakholwa aya entabeni iNhlangakazi ahlale khona amasonto amabili kwenziwa izinkonzo zokukhuleka, nokwelapha nokuzinikela. Lapha u- Shembe wayelandela isahluko 27 encwadini kaEksodusi. 

  Ngawo 10 mkhosi kuyahlatshelelwa kusinwe. Kungakahanjwa wonke umuntu ukha impepho bese ibekwa izinqwaba ezimbili eyabesilisa neyabesifazane. Lezi nqwaba zizoshiswa bese bonke abantu bedlula kuzo besina ngesizotha belandelana. Lona-ke umkhosi wokuqala owamiswa uShembe. Uvarnise ukuthatha izinsuku ezingu-15. 

  Umkhosi wesibili omkhulu ungenyanga kaJuly Ekuphakameni. Kuthiwa lona umkhosi wamadokodo (festival of tabernacles) ngokulandela Isahluko 30 encwadini kaLevi. La mkhosi uthatha amasonto amathathu. Elokuqala elokugubha umkhosi wasebafa. Amanye amasonto awokukhonza, nokwelapha nokusina. Kukhona imikhosi emincane emibili. Oka-April kuthiwa iPhasika. Wenzelwa Ekuphakameni. Uthatha izinsuku eziyisikhombisa. Bese kuba khona umkhosi kaSeptember owaziwa ngokuthi umkhosi wezintombi. Kuhlangana izmtombi ezivela ezimishini ezahlukene zebandla. Zifika zizozwa uShembe eshumayela bese zisina. Nawo 10 mkhosi wenzelwa Ekuphakameni. Uthatha isonto elilodwa. 

  UShembe wasebenzisa umkhosi wokweshwama ebandleni lakhe. Wamisa ukuthi akekho umNazaretha oyokudla emasimini ukudla engakakubusisi uShembe. Wayengasho ukuthi ukumisa lokhu ngoba ezenza iNkosi. 

  UShembe wayengumqambi wamaculo. 'Izihlabelelo ZamaNazaretha' ezashicilelwa ngo-1940 zinamaculo angu-222. Okusheshe kuthathe umfundi wamaculo ukuthi ambaIwa akhuluma ngoJesu Krestu. Amaculo akhe athinta umcabango nenhliziyo futhi akhulume ngesimo esiseduzane nempilo
