uHIange kwaba nohlelo lwezifundo zamantombazane. Okwakhathaza kakhulu uDube ekubuyeni kwakhe kokuqala ukuthi uHulurneni kwakungathi akayikhuthalele imfundo yabamnyama . Izinga eliphakeme lernfundo kwakuyibanga lesine (Std .. 4). Kwesakhe isikole wazama ukuthuthukisa izinga ukuze Iigcme ebangeni eliphurnela eyunivesithi. Lokhu kukhombisa ukuthi uDube kwakumkhanyela kahle ukuthi inkululeko nenqubekela phambili yabansundu iyosekelwa izinga labo lemfundo~ ikakhulukazi ukufundela imisebenzi. Nokho kwaba lukhum kwiziphathimandla ukuba ziyizwe into eyayishiwo uDube ukuthi imfundo ephakeme ayihambisane nokuthuthuk~ kwernfundo kwezemisebenzi. Namhlanje kukhalwa ngokuthi abampisholo abayifundele imisebenzi ngenxa'y0~usweleka ~ezikole ezibafundisa imisebenzi. Nokho sezlqalile ukwakhiwa izikole zama"Technikon" zokufundela imisebenzi. 
UDube akaneliswanga umsebenzi wesikble sasOhlange. 

Wazama ukulwela amalungelo abantu bakubo ngeminye imizamo. Waba ngomunye kwababekhona emhlanganweni omkhulu eBloemfontein ngo-1909. Abaholi babehlangene lapha bevela eMzansi Afrika befuna ikhambi lokuvimba urnthe- 

135 
 
thosisekelo (South Africa Bill). Babefuna ukuba kususwe kuwo ingxenye eyayigunyaza ubandlululo. Le mbizo eyaziwa ngo- . kuthi i"South African Native Convention" yayibizwe uye uDube nomnumzane uWalter Rubusana. Ngawo u1909. uDube wahamba neqembu elalikhethiwe ukuba liye eNgiiandi litshele uHulumeni wamaNgisi ukuba angenzi ubandlululo lube umthetho. Kwabe bazishaya ngendlebe etsheni. 

  Ukwe~a nje lokhu. uDube usesungule iphepha 'nanga laseNatah ngo-1903. Leli kwaba iphepha lokuqala labomdabu eNatall. UDube waba wnhIeli walo kwaze kwaba u-1915. Wabona ukuthi indlela yokuthuthukisa ulwazi, nemfundo ukuba kube khona iphepha labomdabu. 

  Walisebenzisa kabanzi 'nanga' ezama ukutshala umoya wobumbano. Namhlanje 'nanga' lifundwa abantu abaningi emazweni amaningi. Ngo-1906 uDube waloba ngempi kaBhambatha esho imibono yakhe ngalolu thuthuva. Lokhu kwamxabanisa noHuiumeni waze waboshwa kuthiwa uhambisana nomzabalazo kaBhambatha. 

  UDube waba ngomunye wamadoda asungula uKhongolose ngo-1912. Yena-ke wakhethwa waba uMongameli-jikelele wokuqala wale nhIangano. Wasebenzisa 'nanga' ukutshala umsebenzi kaKhongolose nokukhuthaza ubulunga kuKhongolose. Ngo-1914 wahola iqembu lamadoda ayekhethwe ukuba aye eNgiiandi ayochazela uHulumeni ngokuhlupheka komuntu onsundu ikakhulukazi ngenxa yomthetho wezwe ka" 1913. Lo mthetho wanciphisa wnhIaba owabelwa abamnyama waze wanciphisa nelungelo labo lokuthenga umhlaba. UDube wahamba noSolomon Plaalje, Walter Rubusana, Msane noMapikela. UHulumeni wamaNgisi walushaya indiva uhambo lwabo babuya belambatha. 

  Ngokuqala kwempi yokuqala yomhlaba ngo-August ka-1914 uDube waya ePitoli eyobonisana nabaphathi ngosizi lwabamnyama. Wazama kaningi uDube ethumela amanxusa kuHulumeni ezama ukuthi kuboniswane ngezombusazwe. Kwaba sengathi uzishaya ngendlebe etsheni. Ngonyaka wokuqala ehola uKhongolose wabiza umhlangano eShowe lapho akhuluma kabanzi ngobumbano nangobandlululo. Wathi kubantu: "Niyazi

yini izinto ezibhungwayo ngani manje? UJenene .uHertzog owengamele izindaba zabantu ufuna ukuba ehlukaruse abamnyama nabamhlophe, thina siyiswe lapho singazi khona. Ufuna kube . khona umthetho ozokwenza lokhu. Indaba enkulu lena edinga ukuthi kube khona enkulu imbizo yabantu lapho izwi lomnyama liyozwakala mayelana nalo mthetho.   Ngokukhonza kakhulu ukuthuthuka kwesizwe esinsund~ neAfrika yonke uDube waba nyamanambana kuHulumeru, ebukwa njengomuntu ophehla umoya wobuphekula. Waboshwa wethweswa amacala ngokunye ayekwenzela isizwe sakubo. Kwathi ukuba kubonakale ukuthi wayengaqondile ubudlova baqala ukusondela kuye abamhlophe sebefuna usizo mayelana

137 
 
khona kulesi sikhundla waze wafa ngo-1946. Wayekholwa kakhulu ukuthi ngokudaleka kobumbano siyofika isikhathi lapho amandla eyobuyela kwabansundu njengalokhu bekunjalo ngaphambi kokuhlulwa kwabo ezimpini. Lokhu' kukholwa kwamenza ukuba azimbandakanise nezinhlangano, namakhosi, nabaholi bamasonto, kanye nabamhlophe ababekhombisa izifiso zokusiza abansundu. 
Emva kwesikhathi kwadaleka inxushunxushu kuKhongolose. 

Ezinye izisusa zokungezwani zasukela ekubeni uDube wayelandela ezinkambweni zomholi ayemkhonzile uBooker T. Washington. Phela uWashington wayekhonze ukuthula nokuguqula isimo sempilo yomunlu omnyama ngokusebenza nokuxoxa neziphathimandla. Abanye kuKhongolose babona ukuthi lezi zindlela ziyathathela. Ngale nkathi uKhongolose waseNatali wayengahoshelani kahle umoya namanye amagatsha ayegxeka umongameli uDube. UDube wagcina ngokuba asishiye phansi isikhundla waqhubeka nokuba umongameli kaKhongolose eNatali. Wabuye wasishiya futhi lesi sikhundla emva kokugula sathathwa umfundisi u-Abner Mtirnkulu. UDube waziqhubekela nomsebenzi wokuthuthukisa uHlange nokuyala iNdlunkulu yakwaZulu eyayingaphansi kwenkosi uSolomoni kaDinuzulu. 
  Izinga aliqopha lokuthuthukisa imfundo yabansundu lenza ukuba uDube abe owokuqala onsundu ukuklonyeliswa ngeziqu zobudokotela ilion. Doctor of Philosophy ngo-1936 eklonyeliswa iNyunivesithi yaseMzansi Afrika (UNISA). Yaba miningi imicimbi eyenziwa ukuhalalisela uDube ngokuhlabana kwakhe. 
  Nasemabandleni esonto uDube waba usizo. Ngo-1920 yena nomfundisi uZ.R. Mahabane bamela ezamabandla enhlanganweni yomhlaba eHet Zonte ezweni laseBelgium phesheya. Bona-ke babemele iSouth African General Missionary Conference eyayiyinhlangano yabaholi kwezenkolo. 
  Iningi labefundisi ngalezi zikhathi lalingamalungu kaKhongolose ngokukholwa ukuthi umphakathi wonke uyadinga ukuthuthukiswa ngezindlela eziningi. UDube yena waba isibonelo esikhulu ngoba akagcinanga ngokuba ngurnfundisi wevangeli. Wayengumphathi wekholishi uHlange; engumhleli wephepha 'nanga laseNatali'; engumlobi futhi engumholi 
138 

kwezombusazwe. Nakuzo izinhlangano ezazixoxa nohulumeni ngokuphathwa kwabansundu, wayekhona. Wayeyilungu lenhlangano yabamhlophe eyayizama ukwakha ubudlelwano phakathi kwezizwe (Institute of Race Relations).

Mqhayi, Samuel Edward Krune 1875':' 1945 
"Bha/a-ke phe/a ndodana ye-Afrika, ungalokhu uthemeleza; Isikhathi siyabaleka." 
Kubalobi abansundu igama likaMqhayi ngeke lasala lingabalwa. Wazalwa ngoDecember 1 ka-1875 endaweni yaseGqamashe esigodini saseTyume eKoloni. Uyise uZiwani wayengumshumayeli, unina uQashani indodakazi kaBedle indodakazi kaCiko yena wayengumuntu osebenza ekhaya njengamanye amakhosikazi. Unina wafa esemncane impela ngakho wafunda ukuzenzela izinto eziningi. Kwakunguyena yedwa umfana ernzini kaZiwani. Wafunda ukukhuthala, ukuhlonipha, ukunakekela, ukwethembeka nokuzicabangela. 
  Uyise waphumelela ukuyisa indodana yakhe esikoleni eEvergreen. Kuthe esenerninyaka eyisishiyagalolunye abakubo bathutha baya eKentane, esigodini saseTranskei. Bathutha ngoba indlala yayibhokile isifuna ukuqeda izibaya zabanurnzane. 
140 
Wafika lapha waqhubeka nezifundo zakhe zesiXhosa kanye namasiko. Inhlalo yakhe eKentane yamnika ulwazi olubanzi ngenhlalo yabantu bakubo abansundu. Waze waloba ~g~le nhlalo esekhulile wathi: "Ngiyambonga ubaba ngokungJ)'lsa eKentane, ngoba lokhu kwanginikeza ulwazi olubanzi ngempilo yobuzwe babantu bakithi." 
  Ukuthanda isizwe sakubo asifisele okuhle kwasuka ngesikhathi efunda lapha eKentane. Esenerninyaka engu-16 ubudala, udadewabo uJane wamyisa ekholishi laseLovedale ngo-1891. Wasebenza ngokukhulu ukuzirnisela esikoleni yize wayekhathazwa ukungabibikho kahle kwemali. Akavumelanga ukuba isimo semali sikhubaze izinjongo zakhe ngemfundo. Ngezikhathi zokuphumula kungafundwa nangamaholide, wa~ yebamba amatoho ukuze athole imali yesikole. Uloba ngaso lesl sikhathi esinzima yena okaMqhayi esekhulile: "... ukuze ngithole imali ngangisebenzela isikole ngihola indibilis~ (isen~) ngehora, ngisebenza amahora amathathu uma seslphumile isikole. NgeMigqibelo ngangihola usheleni nozukwa (15 cents)." 
Ngamaholide wayengayi ekhaya esebenza e-East London. 
Phezu kwakho konke lokhu kuhlupheka uMqhayi akakhombisanga ukukhathazeka emoyeni. Wayefunda noma iyiphi incwadi ayeyithola. Kuye imfundo yayisemqoka ukudlula ukusweleka kwemali. Lapha watholana nezingqungqulu zabefundisi, zawothishela kanye nabaholi kwezombusazwe. Wathi uma efunda futhi ezwa ngokungezwani phakathi kwabaholi abamnyama nabarnhlophe kwezinye izinto, wabona indlela esamlindele uMqhayi. Abaholi afunda ngabo wabuye wathintana nabo abanye yilaba: Charles Sinxo, abefundisi 0 W.B. Rubusana, P.J. Mzimba, E. Makhiwane, LW. Wauchope noJohn Knox Bokwe. Wayeyinkomo edla yodwa uMqhayi. Lokhu kwabonwa masishane umfundisi uShepherd owaxoxa nabanye waze waloba ukuthi uMqhayi wayenowakhe umqondo enza lokho abona ukuthi kufanele. Wayengathatheki irnibono yabanye ngakukholwayo yena.- 
  Naye uMqhayi uyasho ukuthi 10 mqondo wokuzimela wabakhathaza odadewabo besho nokusho ukuthi lena yinto ayifunda kubafana ayelusa nabo. Sesishilo ukuthi wayekhuthele. Okunye

ngaye ukuthi wayenehlo enakekela eshesha ukubona izinto. 

  Ngo-1897 uMqhayi waphumelela ukuthola isitifiketi sokufundisa. Wafundisa eWest Bank e-East London. Akafundisanga isikhathi eside uMqhayi washiya phansi ngoba engatholi ukuthokoza ekufundiseni. Irnibono yakhe ngokufundiswa kwezornlando waseNingizimu Afrika yashayisana nendlela eyayimiswe ababusi. Kwadingeka ukuba akhethe phakathi kwezinto ezimbili: ukulandela indlela eyayikhonjwa unembeza noma alandele indlela yababusi noma ayeke phansi ukufundisa. Wakhetha ukuyeka ukufundisa. 

  Walobela iphepha 'Izwi Labanlu' kodwa lahlupha ngokuvalwa ngenxa yokungezwani kwabahleli .nokusweleka kwezimali. Wabe eseqashwa iphepha labelungu e-East London. Emva kwesikhashana washiya lapha wabuyela ekufundiseni. Wasiza uJohn Tengo Jabavu ekuhleleni iphepha 'lmvo Zabantsundu'. Waqhubeka nalo msebenzi waze wafa uJabavu ngo-1921. 

  Ngo-1922 wamenywa ukuba ayofundisa eLovedale kodwa akazange aye khona ngoba engavumelani nabefundisi abaphethe isikole mayelana nezindlela okufanele kufundiswe ngazo urnlando wakwaXhosa. Lona kwakungumqondo wakhe ayezimisele ukuwulandela. Lo mqondo wajuliswa kakhulu ukubona ubumpofu babanlu bakubo okwephula umoya wakhe kakhulu. Waze waloba ngethemba aba nalo ngalesi simo wathi: 

"Mhlawumbe ngelinye ilanga uHulumeni uyoba nomusa asisize thina abampoju njengoba esiza izimpojana ezimhlophe." 

  Leli themba lahambisana nenkuthazo ayeyinikeza abanlu ukuba bangabheki kwezinye izizwe uma befuna ukukhululeka. U-Mqhayi wayengomunye wabaholi njengoW.B. Rubusana noJ.L. Dube abazama ukuba abanlu bahlangane i-Afrika yonke. U10ba kanje ngengozi yokuhlakazeka kwabansundu: 
"Ngokwahlukana kwethu sizenza sibe umsobo wabasizondayo."

esikoleni nga-1890. Akekho owayazi ukuthi uphuma nje uyogcina engurnlobi odumile nomholi kwezombusazwe. 
  Waphuma esikoleni wafundisa iminyaka emithathu. Phela kulezo zikhathi umuntu ofunde njengaye 'kwakuthiwa isifundiswa. Useshiya ukufundisa nga-1893 eseya eKhimbili (Kimberley) lapho athola umsebenzi eposini. Kwakuthi uma engenzi lutho afunde isiBhunu, isiFrench, isiJalimane, isiSuthu, 
isiXhosa nesiZulu. 	? 
  Uyasuka lapho usethola umsebenzi enkantolo eba ngumhumushi nakhu phela unguzilimizonke. Ngesikhathi esebenza enkantolo waba muhle kakhulu umsebenzi wakhe ngangoba imantshi yakhona eMafeteng yamusa enkantolo enkulu wasebenza phansi kukaLord Edward Cecil. 
  Nakhu-ke sekuqubuka impi phakathi kwamaNgisi namaBhunu (Anglo-Boer War) nga-1899. USolomon wangena ngasemaNgisini wazinikela ukuba bamnike namuphi umsebenzi ongasiza amaNgisi. Emva kwesikhashana waba urnlobi ngezimpi kakhulu ngokuhlaselwa kwendawo iMafikeng. 
  Umlando wale mpi owaziwa ngokuthi iAnglo Boer War Diary eyalotshwa nguSolomon eloba ngokuhlaselwa kweMafikeng isanda kushicilelwa kule minyakana edlule. Yaphela impi uolomon wayohlala eKhimbili eseqala iphepha i"Koranta ea Becoana" (The Tswana Gazette). Leli phepha lalikhishwa ngezi1imi ezimbili isiTswana nesiNgisi, yena uSolomon waba ngumhleli walo kusuka ngo-1901 kuya ku-1908. 
  NgoJanuary enyakeni ka-1912 kwaba nomhlangano omkhulu we-"African Native National Congress" lapho kwakusungulwa khona Ie nhlangano. USolomon wakhethwa waba ngowokuqala uNobhala-jikelele wale nhlangano. Futhi waba ngomunye \ wabaloba umthethosisekelo wale nhlangano. UDr J.L. Dube wakhethwa ukuba uSihlala-jikelele wale nhlangano. Kungawo futhi 10 nyaka lapho asiza ekusungulweni kwelinye iphepha i"Tsala ea Batho" (The Friend of the People) elaba inoni kakhulu emphakathini ngoba lalikhuluma ngempilo yabansundu nezinkinga zayo. Ngenxa yomsebenzi omkhulu kaKhongolose uSolomon washesha walivala leli phepha. 
Usungulwa nje uKhongolose welama inhlangano ekade 

146 

iqalwe nguye uSolomon i"Diamond Field Men's. Own Brotherhood". Lena kwakuyinhlangano yokuqala yabansundu kwezombusazwe eMzansi Afrika. UKhongolose usungulwa ngoba kudingeka inhlangano ezosingatha uwonkewonke. 
  UHulumeni wamaNgisi wakhipha umthetho ngomhlaba wakuleli. Lo mthetho owaziwa ngokuthi i-1913 Native Land Act wehlukanisa izwe leli wamisa ukuthi abamnyama bazohlala endaweni encane kunabamhlophe. Abokudabuka kuleli baphatheka kabi ngangokuthi uKhongolose wakhetha amadoda ayomkhulumela kuHulumeni wamaNgisi phesheya ngobubi balo mthetho. Ngo-1914 uSolomon wahamba namadoda oDr J.L. Dube, Dr W.B. Rubusana, T.M. Mapikela noS. Msana, bahamba baqonda khona eLondon. 
  Babenethemba lokuthi inkulumo yabo iyophumelela ekuguquleni 10 mthetho. UHulumeni wamaNgisi walushaya indiva udaba Iwabo babuya bedumele. USolomon yena wasala phesheya isikhashana ehambe ekhuluma emihlanganweni echazela umphakathi wamaNgisi isenzo esibi esenziwa uHulumeni wabo ngomthetho wezwe ka-1913. Kwakuthi uma esephelelwa imali alobe izindaba ngezwe lakubo emaphepheni beseehola. 
  Sekuphele isikhashana wabuya ekhaya yize ithuba lokuba abhunguke lalikhona. Waloba ibhuku elashicilelwa ngo-1915 elalixoxa ngenhlalo yabansundu kuleli ngaphambi kokufika kwabamhlophe, ngesikhathi sebefikile, kuze kube isikhathi sempi. Isihloko sebhuku sithi "Native Life in South Africa before and since the European War and the Boer Rebellion" 1916. 
  Kuhle kushiwo lapha ukuthi ngesikhathi eseLondon wathalana noqweqwe uProf. Daniel Jones owayefundisa ezezilimi (linguistics) eyunivesithi yaseLondon. Wathola usizo olukhulu mayelana nezokuloba. Sebegcina ngokuloba incwadi ebizwa ngokuthi "Sechuana Phonetic Reader" eyashicilelwa ngo-1916. 
  Ngokukhuthazeka sekuthi ngaye u-1916 uSolomon usekhipha incwadi eyaba nedumela i"Sechuana Proverbs, with Literal Translations and their European equivalents." Leli bhuku liyiqoqo lezaga nezisho zabeTswana ezibuye zahunyushwa ngesiNgisi. 
Unyaka ka-1919 waba nedumela ngoba izizwe zomhlaba 
147 

, 

zahlangana edolobheni iVersailles eFrance ziyoxoxa udaba lokuthul~ emva kwe~pi yomhlaba yokuqala 1914-18. Lo mhlangano wazlwa ngokuthi Versmlles Peace Conference. Waphinda futhi uKhongolose wajuba amalunga athile ukuba 'aye khona eVersailles ayothula inkinga yokuhlupheka kwabansundu kuleli. USolomon wayengomunye wala madoda. Bafika eVersailles abaze bemukelwa emhlanganweni, kwadingeka ukuba babuyele ekhaya. 
  Waphinda w.asala futhi umfokaPlaatje ngoba eqonde ukuya emhlanganweru omkhulu wabansundu i"Pan-African Congress". Lo mhlangano wawubizwe isaziwa esikhulu kwabansundu eMelika uDr W.E.B. Du Bois. Lena kwakuyingqungquthela yokuqala eyahlanganisa abamnyama umhlaba wonke bezoxoxa ngesimo, nempatho yabo emazweni ngamazwe. Emva kwalo mhlangano uPlaatje wahambela amazwe aseFrance, Canada nase-United States ehambe echaza ngempatho enzima yabansundu kuleli ezandleni zamaNgisi. 
  Esekwenzile lokhu wabuya kwelakubo wazinikela ekusizeni izinhlangano ezazizama ukusiza abansundu ikakhulukazi eKhimbili. Okwakhathaza umoya wakhe kakhulu umthetho iLand Act ngoba yena wasibona lesi senzo sokuncisha abansundu umhlaba kuyisenzo sikaHulumeni sokuvikela abalimi abamhlophe bangehlulwa abalirni abansundu abase banda. Waloba ephepheni Umteteli Wabantu likaNovember 29, 1924 wathi: 

"Ekuqaleni kwerninyaka eyishurni eyedlule kwatholakala ukuthi kunabansundu abangaseneliswa ukulima indawana khona bezothola amasaka ambalwa ommbila ozodliwa kuphela ekhaya. Kodwa kukhona laba asebedayisa izinkomo ezingasho lutho bathenga ezohlobo. Ekuvuneni ngo-1911 abalirni abamhlophe baba nokwethuka ngoba abalirni abansundu bavuna izinkulungwane ezintathu zamasaka kakolweni nenye inkulungwane namakhulu ayisithupha e-muid kanti abamhlophe bona' bavuna phakathi kwamakhulu amathathu namane kuphela ama-muid." 
  Lo mthetho wezwe wenza ukuthi abansundu bangakwazi ukuthenga nokuqasha umhlaba ngaphandle kwezindawo abakhethelwe zona uHulumeni. Abaningi abalirni baxosha abantu emapulazini, lokhu kwadala ukuba laba bantu baqashwe 
148 

ngamaholo aphansi ezimayini. Abanye abayanga ezimayrm kodwa baya emadolobheni ngoba bengasenamhlaba. Lokhu kwadala ukugcwala emadolobheni, kwaba irnijondolo nobuphofu. Ngokucabanga kukaSolomon konke lokhu kwaqala mhlazana abansundu behlangana nabaFuduki ngo-1830. Encwadini yakhe u"Mhudi" uxoxa ngomlando wakuleli awuchaze njengoba ungachazwa umuntu onsundu. 
  Wanikwa indawo abantu baseKhimbili ukumbonga ngomsebenzi ayewenzela umphakathi. Le ndawo wayinikwa ngo-1928. Ngonyaka ka-1930 wazidela amathambo uSolomon enyangeni kaDecember wahlasela uHulumeni elwa ngendaba yamapasi. Lena kwaba yimpi yakhe yokugcina. 
  Asisho lapha ukuthi incwadi yakhe u"Mhudi" (1920) kwaba incwadi yokuqala ezincwadini ezisamlando kwezabansundu. Engakafi wahumusha ngesiTswana incwadi kaWilliam Shakespeare (umlobi odurnile eBrithani) i"Comedy of Errors" yena wayinika isihloko esithi "Diphoshophosho" ngo-1930. Waphinda futhi wahumusha u"Julius Ceasar" wakhe futhi uShakespeare wamnika isihloko esithi "Dintshontsho tsa Bo-Juliuse Kesara". Lena-ke yashicilelwa engasekho emhlabeni ngo-1937. Uye futhi owahumusha izincwadi zikaShakespeare u-Othello noMuch-ado-about nothing. Futhi waba umlobi walezi zincwadi: Boer War Diary; Native Life in South Africa; Sechuana Proverbs; Sechuana 
Reader.

Sithole, Chakijana kaGezindakci 1880 - 1907 

"Wonke umuntu olapha uzolala ekamu kubonwe amapasi enu bese nedlula-ke ekuseni niye emsebenzini. Sesikhathele ukufuna uChakijana noMangathi kuse bemkhomba lapha nalapha." 

UChakijana owadida amakhanda abelungu ngempi kaBhambatha wayezalwa uGezindaka kaNomaqongqotho kaJobe wakwaSithole. UGezindaka wayakhe eQhudeni lapho kwazalelwa khona uChakijana babuye bayokwakha eNhlazatshe. Wabuthwa uChakijana ebuthweni uDakwa kwathi ngempi yamaNgisi namaBhunu wathunjwa amaBhunu. Inkosi yamaBhunu uPiet Scotts yayimthanda kakhulu ihamba naye njalo, yaze yamenza induna yayo. 
  Babevamile ukuhamba behlola impi yamaNgisi lapho icashe khona. Kwakwenzeka ngesinye isikhathi uChakijana athunywe yedwa ukuyohlola izinqola ezingase ziphangwe emaNgisini. Wayebuye ahlole futhi ukuthi impi yona ikuphi nokuthi amahhashi wona akuphi. Konke lokhu kwafundisa uChakijana izinto ayeyozisebenzisa esekhulile. Wafunda ulimi IwamaBhunu nokuthi alwa kanjani. Wafunda ngenkolo yawo nenhlalo nobuzwe bawo. Wafunda ukuba yinhloli nokuthi impi ayiphaka kanjani. 

Uyaqala ukuba yinhloli egcwele: Wake wathunywa ukuba ake ayohlola izinqola zamaNgisi ezaziphuma eDandi 'l'iya eFilidi zithwele ukudla kwamasotsha. UChakijana waqonda kumaNgisi wayobuza ukuthi izinqola zime nje ngempela ziyaphi. Akekho kubelungu owacabanga ukuthi ngabe uyinhloli ngoba phela babebaningi abantu ababehola izinqola. Ngisho namasosha awazange amsole azibonela umuntu oxoxayo. Wasibona sonke 

154 

isimo nokuthi izinqola zithweleni. Ekubuyeni kwakhe emuva watshe1a amaBhunu ukuthi izinqola zithweleni nokuthi kulula kanjani ukuba ahlasele amaNgisi. Induna yamaBhunu yan~l~ yezwa lokho yathi uChakijana akahole iviyo lamasosha. Emprm yaseZinhlonga amaNgisi ahlaselwa engazelele ehlulwa kwaphangwa konke ayenakho. 

Ayambamba amaNgisi uChakijana: Kwathi ethunyiwe ngelinye ilanga ukuba ayokwenza ~~benzi wob~oli ~bomdabu abamaziyo batshela amaNgISI ukuthi uyinhlo~ kwab~ liyamshonela njalo. Wabanjwa nomunye uJantshi Mtshali begadwe izikawoti zabeSuthu. Ngelinye ilang.a babona. ~ban~ bemba umgodi omunye wabatshela ukuthi amaNgIsl athi azogqiba bona ngoba bayizinhloli z~aBhunu. UC::hakijana wabuza komunye unongqayi ukuthi bazofelaru ngoba abenqabile ukuphendula imibuzo engase ibe khona. Khona manjalo wayiswa kwabakhulu abathi aka~~xe konke ayekw~nza noPiet Scotts nokuthi impahla babeYJfihlaphi. UChakiJana wabatshela yonke into ngisho nokuthi imali nezinhlamvu kumbelwephi. Base besinda-ke ukungena emgodini. 
  Ngelanga elilandelayo wahola inkosi yamaNgisi wayisa lapho kufihlwe khona imali nombayimbayi. Kwathi uma bemba sebefika esisefweni semali wezwa onkabi bethi "Muhle Cakijane y~na losi sefo lona." Basikhipha isisefo bahamba naso. Ngomsebenzi wakhe uChakijana wanikwa uR80.70. Wabe esecela ukuba adedelwe aye ekhaya kodwa ala amaNgisi amethembisa umholo othe xaxa. Ngelinye ilanga amaNgisi enomhlangano uChakijana wathola ithuba lokuba eqe abalekele ekhaya. 

Ayambamba amaBhunu uChakijana: Ukuhlala nam~~si ~a~ mfundisa uChakijana izinto ezazikhonzwe amaNglSl; ulimi lwawo nobuzwe bawo. Wathi ezihlalele kupo ekhaya kwafika uPiet Scotts nedlanzana lamaBhunu. Wathathwa njalo wahamba namaBhunu. Wanikwa umsebenzi wokuhlola amasosha amaNgisi eMahlabathini. Ukuze angasoleki wakhumula izingubo wabhinca njengabantu bendawo wafuna umkhondo wase enza uphawu emthini omkhulu njengoba kwakuvunyelwene. Lo 
155 



 
muthi wawuseduze nesitolo lapho afike athenga khona umentshisi. 

  Wabuyela" emuva esehlole ukuma kwamasosha amaNgisi. wathi ngeke bawangobe ngoba maningi kakhulu amasosha.' UNdunankulu wamaBhunu akakunakanga bayiphaka naye uChakijana yahamba yagonda esitolo seNgisi eNkonjeni yaphanga impahla eningi. Ingxenye yamaBhunu eyayina: 
Chakijana yedlulela ekhaya oNdini lapho bafica izingola eziningi zamaNgisi zilibangise enkantolo eMahlabathini. 
Izingola lezi zazinabashayeli kuphela, amasosha esenkantolo. 

AmaBhunu athi "sibonwa yini!" aphanga eziningi izinkomo. Esazishushumbisa kwezwakala ukudubulana kula maBhunu asale ngasesitolo. Yatholana kwafa amaBhunu amaningi. Ngalesi khathi itholene phezulu okaJobe waghubeka nokubaleka nezinkomo zaze zafika enkambini yamaBhunu. 
  Emva kwalokhu uJenene uBotha waphaka impi enxambili, eyabelungu neyabomdabu. Eyabelungu yaholwa uScotts eyabomdabu yaholwa uChakijana. Le mpi yayiyohlasela amaNgisi eBethel lapho alimala khona uScotts waze welulama emva kwamasonto amathathu. Emva kwalesi wombe uBotha wayikhomba eThaleni. Lapha-ke aphela amaBhunu noScotts wafa eduze komngane wakhe uChakijana. Wafa amehlo ethe njo kuChakijana. 

UChakijana ubalekela enkosini uDinuzulu: Emva kwempi yaseThaleni uChakijana wabalekela oSuthu enkosini uDinuzulu. Esikhundleni sikaScotts kwangena uJoni Lebisathe. AmaBhunu aphuma umkhankaso efuna uChakijana. Kwathi uma ehluleka ukumthola athumela kuyise uGezindaka ukuthi uma engayikhiphi indodana yakhe uzoboshwa. UGezindaka wabeseya oSuthu wafike watshela uChakijana umbiko awutholile uvela emaBhunwini. UChakijana wabona ukuthi uyise usengozini wabe sesuka eyozinikela emaBhunwini. Wawafica ethukuthele kabi athi ulahlwa yicala lokubaleka empini ngakho uzodutshulwa. Wakhala wathi into eyamphatha kabi ukufa komholi uScotts. Wabe esexolelwa njalo.

UChakijana uhlangana noBhambatha: Emva kwezinsuku ezimbalwa uphelile umhlangano omkhulu waJheleka uBhambatha kaMancinza ehamba nendodana yakhe uNdabayakhe, kanye noMngoma noNkantolo. Baqala-ke ukubonana noChakijana. Inkosi uBhambatha wayesezwile ngemisebenzi kaChakijana. 

  OkaMancinza wabe esesho ukuthi njengoba bona besakhuluma yena useyiphakile eMgungundlovu ibambene. Washo nokuthi uthembele enkosini uSilwane owayenabantu abaningi esilungwini. Kuthi lapho bebonisana athi uBhambatha: 

  " Abelungu abekho nempela, bayingeosana kabi ngoba abaphesheya eNgiiandi abahlangene nalaba abanganeno. Irnpela ngimethembile uSilwane noNyoniyezwe kaMawele." "Kepha uthole kanjani ukuthi abelungu abahlangene?" "Ngizwe ngomabhalane eMgungundlovu." "Unazo izibhamu?" "Awu! zigcwele izindlu ezimbili ngiyazazi impela. Ukhona umuntu wami osebenza esitolo eMpanza siyozithola kakhulu lapho, ezinye siyoziphanga." 

  Ebuza uChakijana ukuthi kuyoqalwa ngaziphi izibhamu waphendula kanje uBhambatha: "Kuqalwa ngezisesitolo lapho kukhona. abelungu abane nabafazi abathathu kepha abalali khona bonke abelungu; munye kuphela olala khona. Bayobanjwa abelungu nabantu abasebenza kubo bangadutshulwa nempela ngoba impi ayikaqhathi." Wajabula impela uChakijana ngaleli eebo nokubona ukuthi uyethembeka. 

  Basuka oBhambatha, Chakijana, Ngqengqengqe, Mngoma noNkantolo bahamba namaviyo abantu beya esitolo eMpanza. Bangenisa ernzini wenduna kaBhambatha ebusuku lapho bahlatshiswa izintondolo ezintathu. Ekuseni uChakijana wakhonjiswa isitolo okuyiwa kuso. Waeela amadoda ambalwa awethembayo ukuba ake ayihlole indawo. UBhambatha usethuma induna uMgombane ukuba ibize umhlangano wabantu ophuthumayo kungatshelwa noyedwa umIungu ngalo mhIangano.

. noChakijana. 
Yaduma inkundla izindimbane zabantu zikhuleka "Bayede!"

  Endleleni wahlangana noThobela Khanyile noZishede wakwaZiqubu. Bahamba baze bangena edolobheni eMshwathi. Bangena ehhotela badla. Kusenjalo kwangena onongqayi ababili bathi: "Ake nithule umsindo! Dlanini nje niqede. Wonke umuntu olapha uzolala ekamu kuboshwe amapasi enu bese nedlula-ke ekuseni niye emsebenzini. Sesikhathele ukufuna uChakijana noMangathi kuse bemkhomba lapha nalapha." Baphuma onongqayi bashiya amaphoyisa ukuba agade abantu. Kwabe sekungena izintombi amaphoyisa alibala yizo athi lapho eziphelezela seziphuma bashaya baehitha oChakijana baqonda eMgungundlovu. 
Bafika ekuseni baya kuSobantu ummeli wenkosi uDinuzulu.

kaHertzog eyayiqonde ukuphuca abantu amalungelo amaningi nokuba nomhlaba. 
  Ngokuba usihlalo kaKhongolose eKoloni abuye abe isekela likasihlalo wenhlangano yokuvota kwabantu (Cape Native Voters Convention) phambi kuka-1936 kwadingeka ukuba atshele umphakathi ukuthi ubona yiphi indlela mayelana nokukhishwa kwabantu ekuvoteni njengawo wonke umuntu. Wathi uMahabane yena ubona ukuthi uma bevota bodwa abantu kulungile uma kuwukuthi abelungu bayakhathazeka uma bevota nabantu. 
  UMahabane waba ngomunye ababephambili ekubizeni ingqungquthela yama-Afrika (All African Convention) ngo-1935. Waba yilungu lesigungu lika-AAC elakhethwa ngo-1936 ukuba liyoxoxa noNdunankulu uHertzog ngaphambi kokuba umthetho wokukhipha abantu evotini kawonkewonke ungene ePhalamende. Kwathi noma ephikisana nernithetho eyabonakala ihIangabezana nezifiso zabo, inkulumo ayeseyibeke ngaphambili eyavumelana nokuhlukaniswa kwamavoti, yanyakazisa isikhundla sakhe nokuthembeka kwakhe. Futhi ngisho nomfutho weqembu awubanga nawo amandla amakhulu. 
  Kusukela ngo-1937 ngesikhathi uMahabane ehola u-ANC wayeyisekela likasihlalo we-AAC. Kusukela ngo-194O kuze kube u-1954 waba isekela eligcwele likamongameli ka-AAC okokuqala phansi kukaJabavu kwase kuba phansi kukaWycliffe Tsotsi. 
  Wazama kakhulu uMahabane ukudala ukuzwana nobudlelwane phakathi kwalezi zinhlangano zombili yize Ie mizamo ingaphumelelanga. Ngokuthanda ukuba kuhlangane izinhlanga ezimnyama-Abansundu, amaNdiya, namaKhaladi-uMahabane wasebenzelana noAbdul Abdurahman bezama ukubiza imihlangano ezobahlanganisa. 
  1? mihlangano yaba khona ngo-1927 nango 1934. Kwathi ukusungulwa kwemihlangano yezizwe ezingemhlophe (NonEuropean Unity Movement) ingene ku-AAC ngo-1943 uMahabane waba umongameli wayo wokuqala. Wasibamba lesi sikhundla kwaze kwaba u-1956 lapho aphoqwa ukuba asishiye ngoba wenqaba ukuba angasebenzi phansi komthetho wama-School Board emfundweni yabantu. Phela isiphakarniso sika-NEUM 
172 
sathi alikho ilungu lenhlangano yaso eliyosebenzelana futhi lisize kula makornidi namaBhodi ezikole. 
  Kwathi kuya ekupheleni kuka 1940 kuya phambili uMahabane wasegxile ekusebenzeni kakhulu ezintweni eziphathelene nesonto. Wasebenza kakhulu ekusizeni ukusungula inhlangano yabefundisi bamabandla ehlukene (Inter-denominational African Ministers' Federation). Yasungulwa ngokomthetho ngo-1945. Phakathi ebandleni laseWeseli walwa ukuba abantu nabo babesezikhundleni eziphezulu. Ngo-1956 engumongameli we-IDAMF wabiza imbizo eBloemfontein ukuba kuzobhungwa ngeziphakarniso zeKhornishani kaTomlinson. 
  Umgomo wombiko wale Khornishani eyayihlola isimo somuntu omnyama kuleli, wathi umbono weKhornishani ukuthi kube khona ozibuse babantu abamnyama kube khona ukuthuthuka ngokwehlukana. NgoDecember ka-1957 waba usihlalo womhlangano owalandela owokuqala. Wawuhlangene eyunivesithi yase Witwatersrand, usuhlanganise abansundu nabamhIophe. Kwaba khona iziphakarniso eziqinile mayelana neziphakarniso ze-Khornishani kaTomlinson. 
  Kwathi emva kwale nhIangano uMahabane wahambela eWest Afrika eyisithunywa emhlanganweni wamabandla omhlaba. Wathola ithuba lokuvakashela amazwe anjengoGhana neNigeria. Emhlanganweni wabaholi abamnyama owawungoDecember ka-1960 uMahabane wakhethwa ukuba sekornidini lokwakha umthethosisekelo nokulungiselela omunye urnhlangano owawuzoba seMgungundlovu ekuqaleni kuka 1961. UMahabane akaboshwanga yena phansi komthetho wokuvikela izwe (State of emergency) yize ozakwabo babanjwa bavalelwa. Kubonakala sengathi lokhu kwenziwa ukuthi wayesekhulile kakhulu uMahabane irninyaka isihambile. Wafa ngo-1970.

  Injongo eyayisemqoka kuMsimang kwakungukubona abansundu nabamhlophe kuleli zwe behleli besebenza ngokuzwana. Futhi akazange alibalekele iqiniso lokuthi uma kungenzeki lokhu kuyochitheka igazi.   NgokukaMsimang uma abamhlophe bengazama ukuba bathuthukise izinga lokuzwana bayeke ubugovu bokuba konke kube okwabo bakhohlwe abansundu, indaba yokuthi akubuse iningi (majority rule) yinto engeke yaba semqoka. Okufunwa aboMdabu ukuba babe yingxenye kuHulumeni wezwe. 
  UMsimang wagxeka kakhulu inqubo yokubusa ngezabelo (Homeland policy). Washo nokusho ukuthi lesi senzo esokuba kwembathiswe into embi ngengubo eyamkelekayo. Ukuqambeka kwe-ICU (Industrial and Commercial Workers' Union) 
Wonke umIando ophathelene neziNyunyana zezisebenzi (Trade Uninons) ezinsundu usuke ungaphelele neze uma ungalandi nge-ICU noCiements Kadalie. 1? nhlangano yaqopha omkhuIu umlando ngernisebenzi eyayenza ezikhathini ezinzima eyasungulwa kuzo. Ake sizwe ngokuqala kwayo bese sizwa ngernisebenzi yayo. 
  Kwathi ngelinye ilanga kunguMgqibelo ntambama ngo-1918 uKadalie ezihambela nabangani bakhe ababili, wasukelwa yiphoyisa lomlungu lamduduIela ngalena kwesitubhe (pavement). Uthe ethi hlolohlolo latheleka kuye lamshaya langena indlela selanelisiwe. Uma ethi uKadalie uzoyobika emahhovisi amakhuIu amaphoyisa, abamphelezele abangane bakhe, bala baphetha bengenwe yingebhe. Umlungu owayeseduzane owayibona yenzeka Ie nto waya kuKadalie wamnika iphepha elinekheli lakhe wathi uma efuna ukwenza icala uzirnisele yena ukuba ufakazi. 
  Watheleka uKadalie esiteshini samaphoyisa wayibika indaba ngokwenzeka kwayo. USayitsheni owayephethe isiteshi watshela uKadalie ukuthi yinto engajwayelekile ukuba umuntu onsundu acebe iphoyisa lomlungu eSouth Africa. Emva kwalokhu uKadalie wathola eminingi irnibuzo ngokuthi uhlalaphi ngempela, wavelaphi nokuthi wafundaphi. 
  Asichaze lapha ukuthi isingisi sakhe sasehluke kakhuIu kumaAfrika amaningi kanti yiso kuphela ezilimini zaseMzansi Afrika ayesikhuIuma. Wabonakala enomoya wobuphekuIa.

Wafika ngosuku oluIandelayo wazithela kweminingi irnibuz~ kodwa egcizelela ukuthi wavelaphi ngempela nokuthi wafundaphi. kabanzi lolu daba.

umIungu lona kuhle kusunguIwe inhlangano yezisebenzi (Trade Union) njengoba ikhona kwabamhlophe ukuze amalungelo ezisebenzi avikeleke. Emhlanganweni kaJanuary 19 ku-1919 umnurnzane Batty wakhuIuma ngokucaciIe ngomsebenzi ongenziwa iNyunyana yabansundu. Umhlangano w~v.uma ngazwi linye ukuba isunguIwe Ie nhlangano bese lblzwa ngokuthi "Industrial and Commercial Workers' Union".

yaba ngu-R1,40.

enkuIu indlala. 
Iyaqala Ukusebenza I-ICU 
Zisuka phansi i-ICU yahlangana nozakwabo wabelungu i"Cape Federation of Labour Unions" ukuba kutelekelwe ukuthi ukudla kungayiswa phesheya umphakathi walapha ube uIamba. Usuku lokuteleka lwarniselwa uDecember zingu-17 ku-1919. Ngalolu suku wacela emsebenzini ukuba ake aphuthe amahora ambalwa uKadalie. Wahamba wagqugquzela isitECleka sokuqala sabamnyama eMzansi Afrika. 1?si siteleka sasinezinjongo ezimbili: ukunqamuIa kokuhanjiswa kokudla phesheya nokuba izisebenzi ezinsundu zingaholi ngaphansi kuka-60c ngelanga.

  Ngokuthi i-ICU yayisencane nemali yayo ingesize, uzakwabo wabamhlophe wasiza ngoba athole izirnali zokupha i-ICU ukuze kuphurnelele isiteleka. Saqhubeka ngomfutho isiteleka kwathi kuphela isonto lokuqala uHulurneni wakuhoxisa .ukuwezwa kokudla. Kwaphela arnasonto amathathu siqhubeka kodwa sathi siphela iclCU yase ikhokhe R1 012,00.

UGeneral Smuts owayesengungqongqoshe wezenhlalakahle wavuma ukuba uChampion abuye eThekwini ngo-1933. Nebala wabuya wafika sekunebhodi eyengame1e wonke amalokishi abantu.   Izikhalo zabantu wayezibika njengoba zinjalo angakhethi gama elizozenza zibe ngeono. Lokhu kwamenzela izitha phakathi kwabelungu. "Kukaningi abeIungu beza kithi njengabangani kodwa emva kwesikhathi kutholakale ukuthi bazobulala umzabalazo wethu. Bagadeni laba bahlobo!" 
Eqala ukuhola i-LCU. yaseNatali wakhombisa ukuthi abamhlophe abakazimiseli ukuhlonipha umuntu. Ngakho-ke izimali zika-LCU. wazisebenzisa ukuthenga amapulazi ngoba ethi umhlabathi yiwona oyoletha inkululeko: 
"Abelungu kufanele basinike amaholo alingene ukuthi siphile. 
Uma bengafuni kuhle ukuba baqashe abel~ngu bakubo ... " 
Wayevamisile ukuba akusho lokhu uma ekhuluma ngamaholo abantu. Wayekholwa ukuthi abantu bayophumelela uma beqikelela kwezomnotho. Wayehlala ebakhuthaza abantu ukuba bafune izindlela zokuthenga umhlabathi, bavule izitolo,

"Angazi ukuthi lingiphatheleni, kungaba ukuboshwa mhlawumbe ukushaywa, ukudingiswa, noma ukufa. 

Ukuphela ngithandaza uNkulunkulu ukuthi angisize angiphe amandla, aqinise ukuzimisela ukuze ubunzima obungase behle bungangeni kimi okanye bungangehleli, egameni lezwe lakithi elithandekayo, iNingizimu ne-Afrika, libe nenhlangano ngempela, ngesimo nangomoya wazo zonke izinhlanga ezikulo."

. kwezinye izinhlangano. 
  ULuthuli wayezalwa uJohn Luthuli owayeyindodana yesibili kaNtaba Luthuli. Unina kwakunguMtonya owake wahlala isikhathi emzini wenkosi uCetshwayo lapho akhulela khona. Engakaganeli kuLuthuli uMtonya waguquka waba umKrestu. 
  Sebeshadile oJohn noMtonya, uJohn wahamba nedlanzana labelungu baya eZimbabwe eyayaziwa ngokuthi iRhodesia. Kwakuyisikhathi sempi enkulu yamaNdebele. UJohn yena wayeqashiwe eyisisebenzi. 
  Kwathi sekupheIile ukulwa uJohn wahlala eZimbabwe wasebenzela ibandla laseSeventh Day Adventist eMishini eyayiseduze nakwaBulawayo engumtoliki nomshumayeli. UMtonya washonelwa indodana yakhe emadodaneni amabili. Wabe esethatha indodana esele u-Alfred walibangisa kumyeni wakhe eZimbabwe. U-A1bert Luthuli wazalelwa kuleli zwe ngo-1898 kwaphela cishe izinyanga eziyisithupha kwashona uyise. 
Uyise wafihlwa eMishini yaseSolusi eduzane naseBulawayo. 
Wasala uMtonya nabantabakhe wabuzwa ubunzima abedlula kubo abanye abafelokazi. Ngonyaka ka-1908 uMtonya namadodana akhe babuyela eNatali ngesicelo sebandla leSeventh Day Adventist elalifuna ukuyosungula iMishini eNatali. Bake bavakashela eGroutville base beya esigodini saseFilidi lapho bahlala khona. epulazini lebandla lama-Adventist. U-A1fred waqala umsebenzi wakhe wobutoIika kwathi umfowabo u-A1bert welusa iminyuzi yaseMishini. lzikole zazingekho. UMtonya wabona ukuthi ukungafundi kuka-A1bert akulungile, wathungatha indlela yokuba afunde. 
  Wamsusa u-A1bert wayomhlalisa kuyise uMartin Luthuli eGroutville. Urnnumzane uMartin wayeyinkosi yesigodi saseGroutville. Walithola ithuba lokuba aye esikoleni sagcwaliseka isifiso sikanina. Ngokuhlala kuyiwe uAlbert wawubona umsebenzi wenkosi ukuthi unjani. Emva kweminyakana uMtonya no-Alfred bashiya eFilidi babuyela e-Groutville. Bafika bangena ebandleni leCongregational bashiya e-Adventist. Bakha umuzi wabo u-A1bert washiya kwayise wazohlala nabo. Unina wayetshala engadini, alime nensimu yakhe ukuze aphilise izingane zakhe. eStanger ehamba ibanga elingamakhilomitha angu-8. Emva kwesikhathi waganwa u-Alfred unina wasala nezinyo elilodwa azolikhulisa. 
  Wathi ukuba aphumelele ebangeni lesine uLuthuli wahamba wayofunda ekholishi lasOhlange elasungulwa uDr }.L. Dube. Kwakungu-1914 kwenzeka lokhu. Siyokhumbula ukuthi lona kwakungunyaka onzima wesikhathi sempi ukudla kutholakala kanzima. Ngakho-ke impilo Ohlange yayilukhuni noma umphathi wesikole ayezama ngazo zonke izindlela ukuba izinto zihambe kahle. Waqeda izifundo zakhe Ohlange okaLuthuli wedlulela e-Edendale ngo-1921 eduze naseMgungundlovu eyofunda esikoleni esaqalwa ibandla lama Weseli. Lapho-ke waqala ukuzwa ukuthi kunjani ukuba umusha esikoleni. Ohlange akatholanga ukunyukwa ngoba eGroutville wayevikelwa amaqoqo akubo uma bethi bafuna ukumnyuka abanye. 
  Into eyaba yintsha kuLuthuli kulesi sikole ukuthi wayeqala ngqa ukufundiswa umlungu. Phela wayemunye kuphela uthisha onsundu lapha. Ngonyaka wokuqala afika ngawo kwabheduka isiteleka kulesi sikole. Sasingasuswa ukudla njengoba kujwayelekile kodwa abafundi babekhononda ngomunye wabafundisi owayejezisa abafundi babafana ngokuba bathwale amatshe besuka nawo emfuleni bawalethe esikoleni. Amatshe ayezigugisa ziphele izingubo zona lezi ezazingatholakali kalula. Kwathi uma isikhalo silethwa kumphathi wesikole wahambisana nesenzo sikathishela. Abafana badikila ukufunda, babizwa ngamunye ehhovisi likathishanhloko. Emva kwalokhu behlukaniswa kabili abatelekayo nabangateleki. Munye kuphela umfana owalimisa lathi ngqo wathi yena akazimisele ukuthwala amatshe. Wakhishwa kwathiwa 10 mfo kaMavuso akahambe ayoqoqa izimpahla zakhe aphume aphele endaweni yesikole. 
  Abafana baba nomhlangano wabo lapho bavumelana khona ngokuthi uma ehamba uMavuso nabo bayahamba. Basuka baqoqa okwabo emile uthishanhloko ebabuka. Wababuka noma sebelandelana bephuma nemithwalo. Babengazange bacabange ukuthi bangase bahlangane nobunzima njengamaphoyisa nomthetho wokuhamba ebusuku urigenapasi. Kwathi uma ubafikela endleleni 10 mcabango bafuna indawo esahlathi balala 
230 
khona ukuze bahambe kahle ngakusasa bengahlushwa umthetho wokuhamba ebusuku. Ngakusasa bavumelana ukuba bahambe bengamadlanzana amancane. 
  Sebesemakhaya kwafika izincwadi ezazithi abafisa ukubuya bangabuya uma beza nabazali babo. V-Albert kwadingeka ukuba alethwe umalume wakhe futhi ashaywe uye phambi kwabanye abazali njengoba kwakumisiwe. Yaphela-ke indaba yesiteleka. Khona lapha e-Edendale u-Albert waqhubeka nokufunda efundela ubuthisha iminyaka emibili. Ngesikhathi efundela ubuthisha kwakugcizelelwa kakhulu ngokuthembeka, ukukhuthala, ubuholi, ukuzwelana nokusizana. Wangenwa umoya wokuthanda ukufundisa ngenxa yesibonelo sothisha bakhe ikakhulukazi indlela ababefundisa ngayo. 
  Ekuqedeni kwakhe e-Edendale wahamba wayofundisa endaweni yaseBlaauwbosch eNatali. Wenziwa uthishanhloko wesikole se-Intermediate. Lapha-ke watholana nomfundisi uMthembu ababehlala bexoxa naye. Lo mfundisi wayekhuluma ngezinye izinto ayengazange azinake uLuthuli. Ngokuhlala kwakhe ernzini wakwaXaba wathola ukusondelana nenkolo ngoba umnurnzane wakhona wayengumvangeli webandla lama-Weseli. Ngokungabi khona kwesonto Ie-American Board uLuthuli waqiniswa kwelaseWeseli kwathi emva kwesikhathi waba urnshumayeli. Kwaphela iminyaka emibili efundisa eBlaauwbosch umnyango wemfundo wamnikeza umfundaze ukuba aye eManzimtoti ekholishi lase-Adams ayofundela isitifiketi esithe xaxa sobuthishela iHigher Teachers Training Diploma. Wajabula kakhulu uLuthuli noma abanlu babengakathandi ahambe. Yena wahamba engazi ukuthi iminyaka elandelayo eyishumi nanhlanu wayeyoyichitha e-Adams.

  Isikole sase-Adams sasinezingxenye ezintathu yiIeyo ngxenye inenhloko yayo. Kwakukhona iHigh School, kube iTraining College yokuqeqesha othisha bese kuba yilndustrial School yokufundisa imisebenzi yezandla. Kwaphela iminyaka emibili efundela ubuthishela.   Ekupheleni kwesikhathi sokufunda e-Adams kwadingeka ukuba uLuthuli akhethe phakathi kwezinto ezimbili ezaba semqoka empilweni yakhe. Umhloli omkhulu waseNatali uDr Loram, wafuna ukunika uLuthuli umfundaze wokuba ayoqhuba izifundo eYunivesithi yaseFort Hare. Okunye kwaba ukuphuma asebenze aqhubeke nesifiso sakhe sokufundisa. Emva kwesikhathi wafundisa isifundo sokuhlelwa nokuphathwa kwesikole (organization). Ngalesi sikhathi eqala ukufundisa e-Adams uLuthuli iNatai yayisesimweni senguquko enkulu ngaphansi komphathi omusha uDr Loram. Engakafiki uDr Loram imfundo yabansundu yayifana neyabamhlophe eyayifana neyase-Europe. Wafika uDr Loram wenza ukuba imfundo imlungise umntwana imlungiselele impilo abathi abarnhlophe kufanele ayiphile.

Abanye bahlaliswa ernhlabeni ongenambuyiselo khona bezoshiya amakhaya bayosebenza kude emadolobheni lapho ukusweleka komsebenzi kuqhubeka ukwanda. Impendulo kaHulurneni kulokhu kusweleka komsebenzi emadolobheni ukuba abantu babuyiselwe ezabelweni abazishiye ngenxa yoburnpofu nokuswela urnsebenzi."

ekuhambeni kwakhe wathokoza ukubona indlela amasonto ayehlangabezana ngayo nentsha. 
  Unyaka ka-1946 wabaluleka kakhulu empilweni kaLuthuli nasebuholini bakhe. Lona unyaka angena ngawo enhlanganweni kazwelonke i-African National Congress. Umsebenzi wakhe waba neqophelo eliphezulu kangangokuthi washesha ukufinyelela esikhundleni sobungameli. 
  Ngawo futhi 10 nyaka uLuthuli wajoyina inhlangano eyasungulwa uHulumeni ukuba ibe umIomo wabamnyama. Le nhlangano yabizwa ngokuthi Natives Representative Council. Kwathi ukuba uLuthuli nabanye babone ukuthi Ie nhlangano ifana nokuneela isithupha ayinalo usizo, baeela ukuba ike ime. A yizange iphinde futhi ivuke Ie nhlangano. 
  Engakangeni kuKhongolose uLuthuli wayekhathazeka kakhulu ngomthetho wokwahlukaniswa kwezizwe. Lokhu kwamenza ukuba angene ezinhlanganweni ezizama ukuba kube khona ukuzwana phakathi kwezizwe ezahlukene. Waba ilungu IeDurban Joint Council of Europeans and Natives, Institute of Race Relations kanye ne-International Club. 
  Wayethemba ukuthi abamhlophe bayoze bayibone ingozi yobandlululo bese beguquka. Emva kwesikhathi kwamkhanyela ukuthi azinalo usizo ernzabalazweni womuntu omnyama ekuqedeni imithetho yobandlululo. Zona lezi zinhlangano zazanelisiwe ukuba kulokhu kuhlanganwa kuxoxwa nedlanzana labamnyama. Naye uLuthuli wazibona eselokhu emenywa ukuba ayokhuluma ezinhlanganweni zabamhlophe njengalezi: 
Durban Workers' Association, Durban Rotary Club ne Y. w.c.A. Wabona ukuthi noma ezama kodwa akayitholi intshisekelo yokuqeda ubandlululo kulezi zinhlangano. 
  Wangena kuKhongolose ngo-1945 ngoba enethemba lokuthi urnzabalazo womuntu onsundu uyophumelela uma kukhona inhlangano kazwelonke eyolwela amalungelo abo bonke abantu abangafundile nabafundile ngoba bonke begqilazwe ngendlela efanayo. Wakhethwa waba sekomidini elikhulu eNatali. UDr J.L. Dube owayengamele uKhongolose eNatali wagula waphuma esikhundleni sobuholi kwangena uA.W.G. Champion owayaziwa ngokuthi uMahlathi. ULuthuli wabona ukuthi kukhona 
238 
ubungeono ngoba uDube wayenza uKhongolose ube owaseNatali ungathelelani kahle amanzi noKhongolose kazwelonke. Ngemisebenzi kaChampion uKhongolose wabumbana futhi kwaba khona ukuzwana nokusebenzelana nenhlangano i-LCU. 
  U-1948 kwaba unyaka womlando ngoba okhethweni kwaphumelela iqembu lamaNashinali wawa uHulumeni wamaNgisi. Kwangena umthetho wobandlululo waba inselelo enkulu kuKhongolose. Inhlangano yentsha kaKhongolose iYouth League yasha amashushu ithi akube khona into eyenziwayo kuyekwe ukukhuluma kuphela. Pho yayiholwa ubani ngoba yayiholwa uqweqwe u-Anton Lembede esebenza namashoshozela 0Mandela, Matthews, Sisulu, Ngubane, Mda, Yengwa, Dr Coneo no-Oliver Tambo. Ngale nkathi uMongameli jikelele kaKhongolose kwakunguDr Xuma. 
  Isifiso sentsha kaKhongolose saphumelela ngoba ngo-1949 uKhongolose waqhamuka nohlelo olusha Iwezinto okwakufanele ukuba zenziwe (Programme of Action). Kwavunyelwana ngokuthi uhlelo olusha luzosebenzisa umbhikisho, iziteleka nokudelela imithetho ebandlululayo. Kwavunyelwana futhi ukuthi ekwenzeni konke lokhu akuyuba khona ubudlova, ukuchitha igazi nokueekela phansi impahla. NamaNdiya ahambisana nalo mqondo neyawo inhlangano yaluvuma lolu hlelo. 
  Ngo-1951 uLuthuli wakhethwa waba uSihlalo kaKhongolose eNatali, unobhala wakhe kwaba uNkonka wefusi urnnurnzane uSelby Msimang. Ohlelweni Iwezinto ezazizokwenziwa kwakhethwa ukuba kuqalwe ngokudelelwa kwemithetho yobandlululo neyehHsa isithunzi somuntu. Kwaqala kwamiswa u-April 6 ka-1952 lwabuye Iwahlehliswa lolu suku kwaba uJune 26. Ayemaningi amavolontiya alo mbhikisho kuzo zonke izindawo zoMzansi Afrika. 
Abanye abazange besalinda uJune 26 baqala ngaye u-April 6. 
Kusukela ngoJune 26 waqala umshikashi"ka amavolontiya engena ezindaweni okwakuthiwa ezabelungu kuphela, amanye ehlala ezihlalweni ezikhethelwe abamhlophe, amanye engena ezitimeleni ahlale ezinqoleni zabamhlophe, njalo, njalo. Amaphoyisa abopha aze akhathala. Ayekade eqale ngabo

abaholi oLuthuli, Dr Naicker noDr Conco. 
  UHulumeni wathukuthela ukuba uLuthuli athi ehola kuye abuye enze izinto angazifuni. UNdabazabantu wathumela incwadi kanqamla-juqu eyathi kuhle ashiye phansi uKhongolose ngaphandle kwalokho akhethe ukulahlekelwa isikhundla sobukhosi. Wala ukushiya uKhongolose uLuthuli wakhipha isitatirnende esathi "Indlela eya enkululekweni indlela yesiphambano." UHulumeni waphendula ngokuba amchithe esikhundleni sobukhosi. Emhlanganweni wonyaka kaKhongolose owawungoDecember ka-1952, uLuthuli wakhethwa waba umongameli kaKhongolose esikhundleni sikaDr James Moroka. U-Moroka wazithela isisila ngoba eealeni lakhe lombhikisho wazama ukuzehlukanisa nabanye ayeboshwe nabo. 
  Ngaye u-1952 walo mbhikisho kwabheduka iziteleka nokucekela phansi izwe lonke. Lokhu kwakungahlangene nohlelo lukaKhongolose yize abaningi abamh10phe babeka uKhongolose kala. Umbhikisho ka-1952 wakhanyisela uLuthuli nabanye abaholi ukuthi kwakukhona okwakusakhalisa mayelana nobumbano Iwabansundu, kwakukhona iqembu le"Bantu National Congress" elaliholwa nguS.5. Bhengu lihambisana kakhulu no-Hulumeni; uKhongolose wayenesitha esikhulu esiyiqembu lenhlangano i"Non-Eurapean Unity Movement" elalikhuluma kabi ngoKhongolose nabaholi bakhe; kwaba khona isitatirnende esakhishwa owayekade ebambele inkosi yakwaZulu esagxeka kakhulu 10 mbhikisho kaKhongolose; namasonto awazange aphume nezwi eWodwa ngoba nawo ayenqikaza. 
  Ekuqaleni kuka-1953 uLuthuli nabanye abaholi bavalwa irnilomo. Kwaba lukhuni kuLuthuli ukuba ahambele abantu bakhe njengomholi. UHulumeni wazama amaningi amaqhinga okukhubaza uKhongolose. Noma wayevaliwe engakwazi nokukhuluma emihlanganweni zonke izinkulumo zakhe wayeziloba afundelwe zona emhlanganweni. Engqungqutheleni enkulu lapho kwakuqoshwa khona izinhlelo zenkululeko (Freedom Charter) uLuthuli waklonyeliswa nge"Sithwalandwe" umklomelo wobuqhawe. Abanye abathola .10 mklomelo kwaba urnfundisi uFather Huddleston nomholi weqembu lamaNdiya uDr Yusuf Dadoo. 
240 


  Ingqungquthela yayimenywe uKhongolose wabansundu nowamaNdiya. Imigomo yezirniselo zenkululeko (Freedom Charter) zazithi: Umphakathi yiwona oyolawula ngokubusa; zonke izinhlanga ziyoba namalungelo afanayo; zonke izinhlanga ziyokwahlulelana umnotho wezwe, izwe liyokwahlukaniselwana nalabo abalisebenzayo; bonke abantu bayolingana emthethweni, amalungelo ayofana kubo bonke; kuyoba khona umsebenzi nokungesabi; izindawo zokufunda ziyovulelwa bonke; wonke umuntu uyoba nayo indawo yokuhlala; kuyoba khona ukuthula nokuzwana. 
  Norna uLuthuli wayevaliwe wabuye wakhethwa futhi ukuba uMongameli kaKhongolose ngo-1955 nango-1958. Kusukela emva kwengqungquthela yabantu (Congress of the peaple) irnithetho yobandlululo yona irnimoya erniningi. Amashoshozela kaKhongolose ikakhulukazi awe Youth League anengwa ukuthi uKhongolose usefaka nezinye izizwe. Bakuhlaba lokhu ngoba bethi kuzodambisa umzabalazo. Iqembu lomoya omusha lathi iAfrika eyarna-Afrika abekwa lapha uMdali; njengoba i-India kungeyamaNdiya. Nebala uqhekeko Iwafufusa lwaze Iwaba yiqiniso ngokuqambeka kweqembu uPan Afriamist Congress. Lagqabuka igoda kumuntu omnyama njengoba kwenzeka mhlazana uZulu eqhekeka phakathi kwehlukana inkosi uDingane nornf9wabo uMpande. Iqembu elisha leP.A.C. laholwa uqweqwe uRobert Mangaliso Sobukwe owayefundisa eYunivesithi yaseWitwatersrand. Uthi uLuthuli ngalolu qhekeko: " ... uqhekeko luyisikhombiso sokuthi ibanga lenjongo yethu liyindlela ende nelukhuni." 
  Wathi elele ngelinye ilanga wavuswa amaphoyisa ambopha wabekwa kala lokuvukela umbuso. Kwakungu-1956. Baningi ababoshwa arnaphoyisa, izifundiswa, abefundisi, odokotela nabanye. Ababoshwa abazange bahlale nje ejele, bafundisana, baqhudelana ngezinkulumo, benza irnidlalo yasendlini, bacula, benza izinhlelo zernikhuleko. Umbhishobhi waseGoli nabanye basungula isikhwama sokuqoqa imali yokuthblela ababoshwa abameli (Treason Trial Defence Fund). uLuthuli nabanye abangu-60 badedelwa. 
  Ngonyaka ka-1960 inhlangano yePAC yakhuthaza abalandeli ukuba badube urnthetho wokuphatha ipasi ngokuwashiya ernakhaya arnapasi bahambe bazinikele ernaphoyiseni ukuba baboshwe. UHulurneni waphendula ngokuba kudutshulwe abaningi ezindaweni ezahlukene. Inhlekelele eyaba buhlungu eyokudutshulwa kwabantu abangu 65, kwalimala abaningi ngoMarch 21 1960. ULuthuli warnernezela usuku March 28 lokuzila nokukhuleka ethi kungayiwa ernisebenzini. ULuthuli nabanye abaholi baboshwa. Wathi enyuka izitebhisi eya lapho ayevalelwe khona wezwa ngenhlanekela iqhurna ebusweni kwawa isigqoko. Wathi uyasithatha kwarnphinda lokho. Akazange azi ukuthi ubani lona owenza lokhu kuye ngoba kwakungabonakali kahle kurnnyama. 
  Kwenzeka into efana nayo lena ngo-1959. Wamenywa ukuba ayokhulurna enhlanganweni yabelungu ePitoli. Kwakukhona izifundiswa lapha oprofesa, abefundisi, izivakashi zakwarnanye amazwe nabanye. Kwangena idlanzana lezinsizwa zabelungu zaqonda lapho uLuthuli ayehleli khona nosihlalo nonobhala wesifazane. Azibuzanga zarnshaya zamthela phansi uLuthuli zarnkhahlela zabuye zaphendukela usihlalo naye zamvivinya zase zigcina ngonobhala. Kwabizwa arnaphoyisa zasuswa lezi zinsizwa waqhubeka uLuthuli wethula inkulurno yakhe yize urnhlathi ornunye wawuvuvukele nornzirnba utubekile. 
  Kukhona futhi akwenza uLuthuli wagcina eseboshiwe. NgoMarch 1960 waya eGoli eyofakaza eealeni lokuvukela urnbuso. Kwathi kubuka abantu abaningi wakhipha ipasi lakhe walishisa warnernezela urnhlakaMarch 28 ukuba kuzilelwe abadutshulwa eSharpeville ngoMarch 21. Nakwezinye izindawo kukhona abawashisa amapasi. Lena eMzinto uDr Ben Zondi waboshwa wahlawuliswa ngalesi senzo. ULuthuli yena kwathiwa uzodonsa izinyanga eziyisithupha ezalengela irninyaka ernithathu eboshelwe ngaphandle ngenxa yesirno sernpilo yakhe. 
  Waqopha urnlando kulo lonke elase-Afrika ngokuba ngowokuqala ukuba aklonyelwe ngornklornelo wornhlaba oyivelakancane i"Nobel Peace Prize" ngo-1960. Kwabamangalisa abelungu baseSouth Africa ikakhulukazi iqernbu elibusayo

ngoba babethi uLuthuli uyiphekula. Lokhu kwabonakala ngokuba irnvurne yokuharnba ayokwarnukela 10 rnklornelo kanye nencwadi yokuhamba ipassport kube urnzukuzuku ukuba akuthole. Phela kwakusadingidwa ukuthi kufanele yini uLuthuli adedelwe ukuya phesheya e-oslo ayokwarnukela 10 rnklornelo.

phakathi kwezizwe eziseMzansi Afrika. 	. 
  Ikomidi lalesi sikhumbuzo laqopha ukwenza izinto ezinhlanu ukugewalisa izinjongo esesizibalile. Okokuqala kwaba ukwembulwa kwetshe lesikhumbuzo ethuneni likaLuthuli kwaDukuza ngoJuly 23, 1972. Okwesibili kwavunyelwana ukuthi kuyoba khona izinkulumo zokumkhumbula (AJ. Luthuli Memorial Lectures). Kwakhethwa izindawo ezintathu zalezi zinkulumo - kuyoba idolobha eMzansi Afrika; idolobha Iwelinye lamazwe akhululekile e-Afrika; idolobha noma yi1iphi elinye izwe ngaphandiekwaseMzansi Afrika. Okwesithathu kwaba injongo yokusungula imithombo yolwazi (libraries) ekhaya e-Mzansi Afrika. Le mithombo izoqoqa ilondoloze izinewadi, amaphepha namapheshana kanye nokungakashicilelwa (manuscripts) mayelana nomlando, inhlalo, ezombusazwe' nezomnotho waseNingizimu Afrika. Okwesine kwaba injongo . yokusungula indawo yokucubungula ulwazi (AJ. Luthuli Reasearch InstitUte) nemininingwane ngomsebenzi kaLuthuli, nangempilo nezifiso zabantu eMzansi Afrika. Kwaqoshwa ukuthi 10 msebenzi uyoqala eNgilandi. Okwesihlanu kwaba injongo yokuqala umshikashika wokukhuthaza imfundo (Educational Programme). INgilandi yenziwa umthombo wokuthuthukisa nokubuza ngemfundo yaseNingizimu Afrika. 
  Ernzansi Afrika 10 mshikashika wathungelwa uBhishobhi A.H. Zulu mhlazane kwembulwa itshe lesikhumbuzo sikaA.J. Luthuli ngoJuly 23 1972. Ngaleli langa kwamenyezelwa ukuthi izikole ezine zarnaSekondari zaphiwa amaqoqo olwazi (encyclopaedias) adume kakhulu emhlabeni ngokuthi encyclopaedia Britannica. zabantu eNingizimu Afrika. Ake sigcine ngemibono kaLuthuli mayelana nezinto ezinhlanu ezaba semqoka ebuholini bakhe: 
Ngokuzwana kwezizwe 
"I-Afrika yonke iyagula ngenxa yalaba abamhlophe abazenza obhuti (senior partners) baphakade. Nathi akufanele sizingcolise ngomqondo wobukhulu wokwengamela ezinye izizwe." 
Ngeqophelo lenkululeko (Freedom Charter) 
"Leli qophelo elikhishwe eKilnerton liwumphumelangqo wezikhathi zamanje ezinzima, ezigqilazayo nezibuhlungu. Leli qophelo lizama ukunikeza impilo, esimweni saseNingizimu Afrika, emagameni afana nokukhululeka, nokuphathwa ngemfanelo (democracy) ... isho ukuphela kokugqilazwa ngomthetho nokususwa kokujivazwa komuntu ... " 
Ngokudutshwa kweSouth Africa kwezomnotho 
"Eqinisweni lokhu kuzoletha ubulukhuni obunzima kubantu abansundu. Lokho asikungabazi. Kodwa uma lokhu kuyindlela emfushane ezogudluza ukuchitheka kwegazi, kungcono sikhokhe ngokuhlupheka. Futhi sivele siyahlupheka, izingane zethu zilambile, sibuye sife ngokubulawa amaphoyisa." 
Ngekusasa 
"Umsebenzi osele phambi kwethu ukwakha izwe elisha, elizoba ikhaya labarnnyama nabamhlophe, esikhundleni sezinhlangano ezinhlakanhlaka ... INingizimu Afrika ayikabi ikhaya lawo wonke amadoda namadodakazi' ayo. Sifisa ukwakha ikhaya elinjena."

Ngo-1931 uMoses waqashwa ukuba asebenze ophikweni Iwezombusazwe kule nhlangano. Washiya urnsebenzi ayewenza wangenela 10 rnsebenzi ornusha. Uyena futhi owasiza ekuhleleni urnshini owawushicilela iphepha "Urnsebenzi" okwakuyilona rnhlobo wenhlangano yarnaKhornanisi. 
  Ngale nkathi inhlangano yarnakhomanisi yayigqugquzela ukuba balwele ingxenye yeNingizirnu Afrika ibe indawo eyiRepublic (uzirnele). Ngokubona ukuthi uMoses ukhaliphile futhi kunguyena owayengasiza ekugqugquzeleni ukuba abantu balwele iRepublic yabo ("Native republic") Ie nhlangano yaharnbisa uMoses yarnyisa eRussia. UMoses wahlala unyaka wonke esikoleni sase Leningrad eMoscow kusukela erninyakeni yokuqala ka-1930. Kwathi ngo-1935 wasuswa esikhundleni sokusebenzela uphiko Iwezornbangazwe. Lokhu kwaba isikhashana wabuye wabuyiselwa futhi esikhundleni. Wasebenza uMoses kwabonakala ukuthi ukuze inhlangano ithuthuke rnakakhushulwe uMoses anikwe isikhundla sobuholi ngoba sekubonakele ukuthi unaso isiphiwo. Ngo-1939 uMoses wakhethwa waba unobhala jikelele wenhlangano. Lesi sikhundla senhlangano yeCommunist Party of South Africa wasiqhoqhobala ngenkathi urnthetho usayivurnela Ie nhlangano, ngenkathi seyivaliwe seyiphila ngornshoshaphansi nangesikhathi esephurnile kuleli edingile. 
  Urna sibukisisa izenzo zikaMoses sizihlanganise nernicabango yakhe kwakulobile nayekukhulurna sithola ukuthi wayekholwa kakhulu urnqondo nezintshurnayelo zikaKarl Marx. Ngaphezu kwalokhu wayezinikele ukuba kufezeke izinjongo zesizwe esinsundu futhi ekholwa ukuthi kudingeka abaholi abaqotho barna-Afrika abazohlahla indlela eya enkululekweni. 
  Wabona ukuthi selifikile ithuba lokuba asize nakuKhongolose, wangena waba ilungu. Ubuholi bakhe ku-ANC naku"Communist Party" badlondlobala. Yize wayencike kakhulu kwinhlangano yarnaKhornanisi wayesebenza ngokuthernbeka futhi nakuKhongolose. Kwakukhona arnalungu kaKhongolose 
252 
ayengayifuni inhlangano yarnaKhornanisi kodwa ayernhlonipha futhi ernkhonzile. 
  Ngonyaka ka-1943 uXurna owayengurnongarneli kaKhongolose warnerna uMoses ukuba abe yilungu lekornidi elabizwa ngelokuthi Atlantic Charter. Urnsebenzi waleli kornidi kwakungukuloba izidingo zase-Afrika ("Africa's Claims"). Ngo1946 uMoses wakhethwa waba yilungu lekornidi enkulu kaKhongolose (National Executive Committee). Lesi sikhundla wasiphatha waze waphoqwa ukuvalwa ukuba asishiye ngo1952. 
  Ernva kwesiteleka sezirnayini ngo-1946 uMoses kanye nabanye abaholi be"Communist Party" bethweswa kala lokuthi bagqugquzela lolu dweshu. Kwaphela irninyaka ernibili lidingidwa leli cala. UHulurneni kaJan Smuts ukwenza lokhu nje ngoba efuna Ukukhornbisa ukuthi ngeke awanike ithuba lokuphurnula arnakhornanisi. UHulurneni akaphurnelelanga kuleli cala. Sekuthi ngo-1950 sekubusa uHulurneni warnaNashinali inhlangano yarnaKhornanisi seyivalwa ngokornthetho. UMoses wasuka eCape Town ngalesi sikhathi waya eGoli wazivulela isitolo sefenisha e-A1exandra. ICape Town yabe iyinhlokohhovisi yeqernbu larnaKhornanisi. 
  Wasebenza isikhashana eGoli kodwa uHulurneni wanele wenza urnthetho wokuqeda arnaKhomanisi (Suppression of Communism Act) uMoses waba ornunye owagadla kubo kuqala 10 rnthetho. Lokhu kuvalwa kwakhe akakunakanga ngo-1952. Wazikhulurnela ernihlanganweni ekhuthaza abantu ukuba bangenele urnbhikisho wokudelela irnithetho yobandlululo (Defiance Campaign). UMoses waboshwa nabokuqala abangenela 10 rnbhikisho. Lesi senzo sikhornbisa obala ukuthi uMoses wayenokuzirnisela entweni asezinikezele kuyo. 
  Wayengenaso isineke ngarnanye arnalungu kaKhongolose ayekhulurna njalo ngokunakekela osekweqile engafuni ukuqunga isibindi. Kwathi-ke ngoDecernber ka-1952 lathethwa kala labalahla, uMoses waboshelwa ngaphandle izinyanga ezingu-9. 
  Ngo-1955 uMoses waya engqungqutheleni yabaholi beThird World endaweni yaseBandung. Le ngqungquthela eyaqopha 
253

Coka, Gilbert 1910 - 1952 
"Uyabona Gilbert ukuthola imfundo yodwa ngaphandle kobuntu akusizi lutho." 
Abazali bakaGilbert babakhe eduze nomfu1a iMfolozi eNataIi. Uyise walwa empini ka-1901 eMtashana lapho kwakubambene uZulu namaBhunu.   Wabe esecela kuyise ukuba kuthi phakathi nonyaka ayohlala nomunye wothisha amsebenzele. Lokhu wakuvumela. phezuIu uyise ngoba wayemazi 10 mfana wakhe futhi ewuhlonipha umbono wakhe. 
  Wahlala kahle kakhuIu nothisha wakhe emphekela elungisa nasendlini abahlala kuyo. Ukukhalipha kwakhe kwamenza waba nesikhathi esiningi asisebenzisa ngokufunda izincwadi namaphepha. Ezincwadini azifunda ezathinta impilo yakhe yilezi: "Up from Slavery", "Her-eward the Wake", "From Log Cabin to White House", 'The Negro World". Wayethanda kakhuIu ukufunda izincwadi zemilando ngempilo nemisebenzi yamaqhawe (biographies). Lezi zincwadi zamfaka umoya wokuzimisela ukuba naye ngelinye i1anga abalwe kumaqhawe omlando eAfrika. 
  Waphothula izifundo zakhe kwase kudingeka ukuba aye ekholiji. Wafikelwa ukujabuIa lapho unyaka uyophela ngoba ezoke ezwe inhlalo nempilo yasekholiji. Nangazo lezi zikhathi abantu abamnyama babeyikhokhela imfundo yabo abamhlophe bengayikhokheli. Uyise wase embiza uGilbert wamtshela ukuthi akanayo imali yokumusa ekholiji nakhu phela kade ekhokha efundisa udadewabo uEunice nomfowabo omdala. Wamcela uyise ukuba ake ahlale ekhaya unyaka emnike ithuba lokuqoqa imali. Kwathi noma kubuhlungu kuGilbert waduduzwa ukuthi naye wayesazi isimo sasekhaya ebona ukuthi uyise ukhuluma iqiniso. Welusa izinkomo zikayise uGilbert engakhohlwa ukuphatha incwadi uma eyokwalusa. Kwathi uma sezibuya ezinye izitshudeni ngamaholide ephasika ezizwa zikhuluma ngemfundo nenhlalo yasekholiji wafikelwa ukuzimisela ukuya ekholiji. 
  Nanguya uGilbert ngelinye i1anga eya kuNsumpa emcela ukuba amfundise. Wala uNsumpa. Akaze alahla ithemba uGilbert waqonda kumhloli wesiyingi saseDundee eyocela usizo. Ukwenza konke lokhu uGilbert akabaxoxeli ekhaya. Isekela lomhloli umnurnzane Fortescue Khumalo watusa ukuzimisela kukaGilbert. Inkulumo yonke yaphetha ngokuthi

uGilbert akaye ekhaya azimisele ukwenza konke okuzoshiwo umhIoli wesiyingi saseDundee. UGilbert wanikezwa imali yokugibela isitimela esebuyela ekhaya. Kwaphela izinyanga ezimbalwa nango esebuyela eDundee ezithela engqungqutheleni yothisha. . 
  Wayeqala ukubona othisha behlangene wathola ukuthi banomoya omuhle yize abanye babengenandaba nazo zonke izinto ezazenziwa emhlanganweni kanti futhi abanye bengekho ezinkuIumweni ezisemqoka. Konke okusemqoka kwakudedelwa emahlombe ekomidi labo. Wasuka lapho eshiya umhIangano wonyaka weNatal Native Teachers Union wayobonana nabahloli ababezomvivinya mayelana nesicelo sakhe semali yokubuyela esikoleni. Wahlala-ke kwamhloli wesiyingi izinsukwana esiza ngomsebenzi wasekhaya njengokuvuka ekuseni abasele isitofu, ageze izitsha asebenze engadini. 
  Zaqhubeka izinsuku kungashiwo lutho ngokuya kwakhe esikoleni. Nokho uGilbert wazilibazisa ngokufunda izincwadi kuIezi zikamhloli ayemsebenzela.

NgoLwesibili uzosuka lapha ekhaya uyofundisa esikoleni eMumbe eMsinga. Ukuya kwakho ekholiji kuyokwenziwa ukuphumelela kwakho emsebenzini eMsinga." Waqeda ukusho lokho wathi akaphume.

  Waphinda wantula umsebenzi wase ebona ukuthi isu elingcono ukuba alobe. Wayengazange wafunda izindlela zokulobela arnaphepha. Kwaya kwaya iphepha iSunday Times lavuma ukukhipha okunye ayekuloba. Kwatholakala ukuthi nalapha kuyincikinciki. 
  Waqhubeka nokufuna umsebenzi wagcina ngokuzirnisela ukuloba. Waqarnba iphepha i"African Libetor" ngo 1935 yokusiza inqubekela phambili yabantu abamnyarna. Leli phepha alihlalanga isikhathi eside. Ngonyaka ka 1946 uCoka nabanye abangu 17 arnalungu kaKhongolose baboshwa bethweswa kala mayelana nesiteleka sabantu abamnyarna ababesebenza ezimayini. 
Izinsuku zokugcina zikaGilbert azicacile kah1e emlandweni. 
Kungalinganiswa ukuthi wawushiya 10 mhIaba eneminyaka engarnashurni arnane nambili cisho nga-1952. 
 
Ngoyi, Lilian Masediba 1911 - 1980 
Kubantu besifazane asebake bangena kwezornbusazwe akekho owaba nedurnela no~uthandwa urnphakathi njengoLilian Ngoyi. WazaJelwa endaweru yaseGarnatlaJa eduze nasePitoli ngonyaka ka-1911. Wayengornunye ezinganeni eziyisithupha zikaMnurnzane uNgoyi owayesebenza ernayini eGoli. 
  Wathi esefike encwadini yesithupha esikoleni, efunda esikoleni okuhlalwa kuso (boarding school), abazali bakhe barnkhipha esikoleni ngoba bengenayo irnali yokurnfundisa. !,!aye ,:"a~ wenza irnizarno kwatholakaJa ukuthi ngaJezo zlkhathi C1she bonke abansundu babernpofu bengenayo irnali. Kwaba buhlungu nakubazali bakhe ngoba babefuna ukuba uLilian afunde agcine lapho inhliziyo yakhe narnandla akhe kwakurnkhornba khona. 
  Waphurna-ke esikoleni iKilnerton Teacher Training College wangena esibhedlela esebenza njengonesi osaqeqeshwa. Washeshe washada ethi wenzela ukuthola ihawu lokukhosela. Kulo mshado wathola ingane kwathi urnyeni wakhe washona ingane yabo inerninyaka ernithathu. Ngo-1945 uLilian wangena efernini yezingubo wasebenza khona. Wathola ukuthi irnithetho abasebenza phansi kwayo abantu yabe ilukhuni' kakhulu. Waqoqa izisebenzi ukuze balwele irnithetho namathuba angcono okusebenza. Ukwenza lokhu nje ungurnuntu okhulele ernaphandleni hhayi edolobheni. 
  Wangena wathi shi emsebenzini wenhlangano eyabe ikhulurnela abasebenzi ernafernini ezingubo (iGarment Workers' Union). avurnelana ngokuseka isiphakarniso sokuthi rnakube khona okwenziwayo erninyakeni yawo-1950 (Programme of Action). 
  Ngo-1952 uKhongolose wanqurna ukuba kudelelwe irnithetho ebandlululayo (Defiance Campaign). WaJungenela lolu hlelo lukaKhongolose walushurnayela yonke iNingizirnu Afrika. Ngaye u-1952 wahola iqernbu labesifazane abahlanu baharnba baya eposini eJeppe eGoli. Bafika bangena lapho kulotshwe khona ukuthi kungena abamhlophe bodwa.   Umsebenzi wakhe wakhula kakhulu kuKhongolose kangangoba ngo-1954 wakhethwa ukuba abe uNgqongqoshe wengxenye yabesifazane kuKhongolose (Womens' League) kwasuswa u-llda Mtwana owayengowesifazane wokuqala ukuphatha lesi sikhundla.   Lezi zikhundla zamsebenzisa kakhulu uLilian ehamba engena ephurna e-Orlando West evakashela abaholi futhi ekhulurna emihlanganweni phezu kwalokhu ebambelele emsebenzini. Abesifazane eNingizirnu Afrika bayizwa intshurnayelo barnlandela njengoba ezinyangeni eziyisikhornbisa kusuka ku-1956 wakwazi ukuqoqa ornama abangu 50,000 ababhikishela amapasi ernadolobheni angu 30 eNingizirnu Afrika. NABANTUKOP: 

Kukho konke akwenza uMseleku wabuya phesheya efunde indlela yokuba abantu bazimele kwezomnotho ngokubambisana (Co-operatives). Wathola phesheya ukuthi ngisho nompofu angathola ukuphefumula uma kuqalwa lolu hlobo kwezomnotho. 
  Wasungula uhele Iwezitolo lapho abantu bezoba namasheya khona bese bekwazi ukuthenga kangcono ezitolo zabo zobambiswano (co-operatives). Umsebenzi kaNABANTUKOP waduma iNatali yonke ngesikhathi esifushane. Wabuye wanyamalala ngokuthi abasebenza naye babengazi ukuthi izitolo zobambiswano zisebenza kanjani. Wawa umsebenzi wesizwe. Ngo-1965 washona uMseleku eshiye induku ebandla eyobuye ithathwe ezinye izinsizwa.

Wasebenza kakhulu yathuthuka indawo yase-Otimati kakhulu emfundweni. Ngokuphumelela kakhulu kwabafundi kwabonakala ukuthi sikhulu isidingo sesikole esizoba iSecondary abafundi bangayi kude njengaseManzimtoti. Esewenza amalungiselelo okusungula iSecondary eOtimati kwathiwa akahambe ayoyiqala eMaphumuio. Nebala wasiqala isikole esabizwa ngokuthi iSabuyaze Secondary School. 
  Esekhona Otimati wasebenzisa isonto ukuba landise ubudlelwane phakathi kwabakholwayo. Kwelakhe isonto kwakungasonti amaLuthela kuphela-noma ubani wayevunyelwa. Waqhubeka ukusebenzela ubumbano esontweni ngokusungula izinhlangano ezinhlobonhlobo zokuthuthukisa isonto nobumbano. Ngo-1959 umfundisi uMsorni wakhethwa ukuba abe ngumongameli (Moderator) webandla lamaLuthela. Kwaba umuntu onsundu wokuqala ukuba aphathe lesi khundla engenalo isekela lomlungu.lsekela lakhe kwaba umfundisi uD.L. Makhathini. Wasiphatha lesi sikhundla ngaphandle kokungabaza. 
  Umoya wobudlelwane phakathi kwamabandla wawulokoza njalo ngangoba waze wawela waya phesheya eGeneva ukuyocobelela ulwazi ngezifundo ezisebenza ubudlelwane (Ecumenical Centres). Uwela nje usevele ufisa ukuba aqale indawo enjena eDlangezwa. Ekubuyeni kwakhe wasungula ikornidi elaqoqa izimali zokuqala iKwaDlangezwa Ecumenical Centre. Ngenxa yezinkinga zezimali nesiza lesi sifiso asiphumelelanga sarna esithubeni. 
  Ngenxa yempilo wacela ukuba anikezwe umhlalaphansi emsebenzini wesonto. Lokhu kwavunywa. Noma esehleli ekhaya akazange ayeke ukusiza emsebenzini wesonto nowomphakathi. Waze wanelwa ukufa ngo-April zingu 20 1979 washiya iqoqo lezinkondlo ezingazange zashicilelwa. Kukhona nencwadi kamnurnzane uMalcolm, umIobi odurnile, eyayi-

mkhuthaza ekulobeni. Umongameli uMsorni washiya eyibekile induku ebandla ngoba washiya amadodana namadodakazi amabili. Eyokuqala indodana umfundisi uLindinkosi Msorni osebenza kwaMaphumuio. 
  Eyesibili uDurnisani Msorni isebenza esibhedlela esikhulu eEdendale ngaseMgungundlovu yafundela ukusiza odokotela (Medical technology). lambada, Anton Francis Mzwakhe 1914-1947 
"Isibopho esiyohlanganisa wonke ama-Afrikil phansi kophiko lobu-Afrikil kuyoba uthando oluqinile nolungapheli lwe-Afrikil, izwe lawokhokho nothando lwenkululeko ye-Afrikil." 
La mazwi awensizwa eyaduma kakhulu kwezemfundo nakwezombusazwe. A yiphilanga isikhathi eside kodwa eminyakeni engamashurni amathathu nantathu ikhona ernhlabeni yaqopha urnlando okungafanele ukhohlakale. Akekho owaphila ngezikhathi zakhe zobulukhuni, owafika kule minyaka ekhulurna kahle izilirni ezingu 8 futhi esephase iziqu zikaM.A. esifundweni sePhilosophy. Owakwenza lokhu u-Anton Mzwakhe Lembede owathi efa ngo-1947 wayesetshale irnbewu kwezombusazwe. Le mbewu yaqhuma kancane esaphila kanti eminyakeni erniningi esafa yayibonakala ngokuba khona koqhekeko kuKhongolose nokuzalwa kweqembu i"Pan Africanist Congress". Nguye phela owagcizelela kakhulu ubuAfrika kubantu esho nokuthi kuhle ukuba urnzabalazo wenkululeko ungangenwa izizwe kodwa kube abomdabu bodwa. 
  UMzwakhe wazalwa zingu 21 July 1914 e-Eston epulazini likamnurnzane uFrank Fell. UMzwakhe wayeyizibulo likaMartin Michael Mbazwana owayeyindodana yesithathu kaDlozi Lembede. UMartin wayesebenza epulazini ehlonishwa omakhelwane nabelungu ngoba wayengurnuntu othanda ukulalela atshelwa khona nomuntu owayenza asekucabangile. UMartin wayedume ngokuthi konke ayekwenza wayekwenza ngokwesaba uNkulunkulu. Lokhu kwaba isifundo esikhulu ezinganeni zakhe.

Umoya Wobuzwe: 
Ngesikhathi eseGoli uMzwakhe wayevamile ukuxoxa nabangani bakhe uMda noNgubane. Umoya wokuzabalaza wase ukhona ukhuthazwa uKhongolose ne-ICU. La bangani babexoxa kabanzi ikakhulukazi ngomgomo womqondo (Philosophy) wokuhola abantu. Mayelana nalo 'mqondo uMzwakhe wakholwa ukuthi kumele abomdabu bazimele bona bazikhulule bona ngokungazinyezi ngebala, ngokuhlangana, nangokuzinikela emzabalazweni. Ngokwakhe ukubona 10 mqondo ubu-Afrika (Afrialnism). Ngokusungulwa kweqembu lentsha (Youth League) kaKhongolose ngo-194410 mbono kaMzwakhe wase utshalekile entsheni embalwa. Waphumela obala waba umkhulumeli wabo bonke abakholwa yilo mgomo womqondo omusha. UMda noNgubane abahleli bamaphephandaba benza amalungiselelo okuba 10 mqondo omusha ungene kalula kubantu. 
  Emhlanganweni wokhetho weYouth League wenziwa usihIalo ethatha isikhundla sikaDr William Nkomo. Ngo-1946 engqungqutheleni kaKhongolose eBioemfontein uMzwakhe wakhethwa waba yilungu lesigungu esengamele uKhongolose (National Executive Committee). 
296 
  Wahlala kulesi sikhundla waze washona. Wayevamile ukuthi uma ekhuluma nge-Afrika athi: "Mina ngiyinto eyodwa neAfrika. Uma ubuka ubuso bami uzobona ukuthi buyefana nomhlabathi wase-Afrika." 
Umgomo Womqondo Wobu-Afrika: 
UMzwakhe wakholwa ukuthi 10 mqondo omusha" iwona owawuyosetshenziswa njengenkolo yabo bonke abomdabu uma sebezabalazela inkululeko. Lo mqondo wakhombisa intshisekelo yokufuna izindlela ezintsha zokulwela inkululeko. Phela intsha yase iqalile ukusola abaholi bakaKhongolose ngokuthi balibele ukuxoxa nezitha kanti futhi bavumelana nezinye izizwe ezingagqilazekile njengabomdabu ukuba zijoyine kuKhongolose bese zidambisa umfutho womzabalazo. Akazange awuthande umqondo wamaMarxist. Wawufanekisa nabelungu benhlangano yamaKhomanisi eNingizimu Afrika. Wayekholwa ukuthi Ie nhIangano ikhubaza umzabalazo ngokuthanda ukwenzela abomdabu okuningi bona bengatholi ithuba lokuzenzela izifiso zabo. 
  Uma kukhona into eyayingamphathi neze kahle kwakuwukubona abomdabu bevumela ukuba ezinye izizwe zibenze izingane bese bebheka kuzo ukuba zibenzele zonke izinto abaz:ifisayo ngisho nezinto abangazenzela ngokwabo. Inhlalo yabomdabu eNtiiasifaii wayibona kahle ngesikhathi eseGoli. Impilo yabantu yamthinta kakhulu ngoba yayibulala impilo yobuntu basemakhaya. Nabantu ababephila Ie mpilo babengaboni ukuthi ibabulala kancane, ikakhulu ebuntwini nasezimiIweni zabo. Wabuka izimfashini nokulandela impilo yabamhlo-phe, kodwa akazange akheke yilokhu. Ngo-1946 waloba ngokuncipha kwezimilo enkulumweni ayenza emhlanganweni wentsha. Wathi: "Ukuphela kwesimilo nokuncipha kobuntu kuqhubeka ngendlela emangalisayo. .. futhi, kuzibonakalisa ngendlela abantu abalahlekelwa ngayo ukuzethemba, bese bekhonza okwabelungu, nokwabaholi bezinye izizwe zaphesheya nemiqondo yazoo Konke lokhu kukhombisa ukugula komqondo."

amaningi. Iphephandaba "InkundIa Yabantu" layikhipha Ie nkulumo zimbili enyangeni kaMay ngo-1946. Enkulumweni yakhe umfokaLembede wakhononda ngokuthi abomdabu badembesele impilo yabo, nobuzwe babo kanye nobudIelwano nezinye izizwe. Ngokw<ikhe ukubona kudingeka ukuba ubuAfrika belaphe ingqondo yabomdabu, babone ukuthi kufanele bangalesabi ibala labo abalinikwa uMdali. Kufanele baziqhenye ngalo; baziqhenye ngornlando .. wokhokho babo njengezinye izizwe. Kufanele balithande izw~abo bazimisele ukulikhulula. Ngakho-ke wanxusa bonke abaholi ukuba bafundise abomdabu ukuba baziqhenye ngebala labo, bangakhohIwa izinkulumo nezenzo zezinye izizwe zokubukela phansi ibala labomdabu. Wagcizelela ukuthi impucuko yaqala e-Afrika ngezikhathi zobukhulu baseGibhithe, futhi akekho ongathi ngeke kuphinde kwenzeke ukuba i-Afrika iqophe urnlando wobuholi emhIabeni. Wakhumbuza abomdabu amazwi kaPewula (Paul Kruger) athi: 
"Wie sich een toekomst scheppen wil, mag het verleden neit uit he oog verleizen. " 
  Okusho ukuthi: Lowo ofuna ukwakha ikusasa angakhohIwa ingemuva lakhe. UMzwakhe waloba ngo-1945 wathi kusadingekile ukuba abomdabu bakhe izikhumbuzo ngemisebenzi emikhulu yabaholi njengoShaka, Moshoeshoe, Hintsa nabanye ngezikhathi zabo nangokuqina kwesimo bazama futhi bazinikela ukusebenzela abakubo. Waqhubeka wathi uMdali ukubekile konke okusemhIabeni ukuba kufeze umsebenzi othile noma ngabe kungamanzi, utshani, iziIwane noma abantu. Wathi uMdali wababeka abantu bomdabu ebabekela ukuba babone, bahlangane, bazikhulule kwezombusazwe. UMzwakhe waba nombono ocacile ngekusasa Ie-Afrika. Wathi ama-Afrika, njengazo zonke ezinye izizwe ezinkulu emhIabeni, ayogcina ehIangene futhi ekhululekile esethathe indawo ebonakalayo phakathi kwezizwe zomhIaba. Ngo-1946 waloba kanje ephepheni "InkundIa Yabantu": " Ama-Afrika awomdabu waseAfrika, ahlala e-Afrika selokhu kwasuka phansi. I-Afrika ngeyabo kanti futhi ayisizwe esisodwa esihIanganiswe ngebala. Kulezi zizwana ezehIukene kuyodaleka isizwe esisodwa." 
Kulo leli phephandaba uMzwakhe wayeseke wawubeka 
298 
umqondo onjena ngo-October ka-1945 lapho athi ukuhIangana kwezizwe zase-Afrika yikhona okuyoletha inkululeko nenqubekela phambili. Waqhubeka wathi uma ama-Afrika engathola uthando olunamandIa lokuhIangana angakha isizwe esisodwa esingaqopha owaso urnlando. Washo futhi ukuthi arna-Afrika ayinto eyodwa ne-Afrika; yikho-ke lokhu okuyoba isisekelo esikhulu sobu-Afrika (Ajricanism). 
  NgokukaLembede umoya wobu-Afrika ugcizelela ukuzithanda, ukuzimela, ukuzihIonipha, nokuzinikela ekuthuthukiseni i-Afrika. Ngakwezenkolo waveza umbono wokuthi kuyadingeka ukuba inkolo yobuKhrestu ibe nesisekelo sobu-Afrika ngokuba isebenzise izingxenye ezithiIe zenkolo yomdabu. 
Ngokuhambisana nezinto zoMdabu: 
Ngesikhathi sikaMzwakhe abantu abaningi bebekhonze kakhulu ubulungu, okomdabu bekubukela phansi. Abafundile babethanda ukukhuluma isiNgisi ikakhulu uma bephakathi kwabantu abangafundile. Arnagama athi "iqaba", "urnhedeni", "ibheshu", "isidwaba", ayesetshenziswa uma kukhulunywa ngalabo abangazange baye esikoleni. 
  Abelungu bakuthokozela lokhu ngoba baze benza umthetho wokuthi abantu abafundile babengabuthenga ubulungu babe ama?emtiti (exempted) bangaphathwa njengabantu. Abanye bomdabu baze baziqamba amagama abelungu babuye baguqula izibongo zabo kwaba ezabelungu. Kwakukhona abanye bomdabu ababekhonze izinhIobo zokhiIimu abenza isikhumba siguquke ibala laso siphaphatheke, kuphele ibala elimnyama. 
  OkaLembede wakhala ezimathonsi ngokudutshwa kwebala lendalo k.uze kuyolandela nokudutshwa kwamaningi amasiko omdabu. OkaLembede wathi ukuze i-Afrika ibe nesisekelo esiqiniIe ngekusasa layo kufanele ukuba ikhethe okuyifanele 
empilweni nasemasikweni ezinye izizwe. 	? 
  Wathi impilo yabomdabu ayifani neyabamhIophe ngoba eyabamhIophe igcizelela ubunye noburnina, nokuzimela wedwa. Impilo yabomdabu yona ibona umhIaba uyinto eyodwa enezinto eziningi ezisizanayo ukwakha ukuthula nobudIelwano. Nakubantu kunjalo. Impilo yobudlelwano, nokuzwana, nokuzwelana, 
299 
,  



nokusizana kusemqoka empilweni yabomdabu. NgokukaLembede impilo yabomdabu iyona eyayizama ukwakha ukuzwana futhi ibeka isisekelo sobumbano okuyogcina kuyinto eyokwenzeka. Esinye isizathu esenza ukuba uLembede.angawathandi amaKhomanisi esokuthi ubuKhomanisi buyinto entsha e-Afrika. Wakhomba iqembu lamaKhomanisi eNingizimu Afrika (iSouth African Communist Party) wathi la maKhomanisi awaqondile ukukhulula abomdabu kodwa ajahe ukuba kwande ivangeli lawo kuphela. Kusobala ukuthi umqondo kaLembede wokungezwani nokulandela impilo yabelungu futhi ethanda ukuvuselela ubuntu namasiko amahle omdabu, kwakufanele kurnxabanise nabamhlophe nabaningi bomdabu ikakhulukazi labo ababebona inkululeko isekulandeleni abamhlophe. Asingakhohlwa ukuthi ngo-1936 abomdabu bephucwa ilungelo lokuvota wabuye wehluleka uHulumeni ukufeza izethembiso azenza kusaqala impi. Lesi senzo sikaHulumeni senza ukuba abanye abantu babuyele enkolweni kaLembede. 
Kanti Okabani uMzansi Afrika? 
Umoya wokuthi uMzansi Afrika owabo bonke asebekuwo ngisho nezizwe okungezona ezomdabu wadlondlobalisa intsha kaKhongolose. Lo moya owase ungena nakuKhongolose kwadingeka ukuba ucishwe ngemibono eqinile yokuthi akunjalo. ULembede nentsha baphika bathi ngemvelo nangendabuko uMzansi Afrika owabomdabu, zonke ezinye izizwe ziyizifiki. Uma izizwe ezazalelwa lapha oyise ababeyizifiki ziseyizo izifiki. Abomdabu kuphela abanelungelo lokuthi:. "Leli zwe deth~". lntsha kaKhongolose yakhipha umgomo-slSekelo (baSIC polIcy) wentsha ngo-1948. Wathi 10 mgomo-sisekelo: 
"I-Afrika yayikade ingeyabomdabu, futhi isengeyabomdab~. 
Abamhlophe abazihIephulela i-Afrika ngendlovuyangena ab~slbona abanikazi be-Afrika ... Kodwa noma ehlulwa ama-Afrika awazinikezanga ekwahlulweni futhi ngeke ayeke ukufuna ukubuyisa izwe lawo. Iqiniso lokuthi ephucwa izwe lawo kanye namalungelo awo, akusho ukuthi izwe akulona elama-Afrika." 
  I"Youth League" yayikhala njalo ngokuthi akube ~ona okwenziwayo ngokubuyiswa kwezwe. ULembede nabathize entsheru 
300 
kaKhongolose babeyihleka usulu inkulumo yo~uthi kukho~a abelungu abalungile. Laba belun~ o~akuthiwa balungile (liberals) bathi yibona kanye abaymgoZl ngokufaka umoya othambisa intshisekelo yenkululeko. Noma umqondo wo: 
Lembede wawunganambitheki kwabanye, wabathoba ngokuthi kuyothi uma inkululeko isitholakele, abelungu abayovuma ukubuswa uHulumeni wabomdabu, bavunyelwe ukuhlala eNingizimu Afrika. Kuyothi labo abangathan~ ba.qoqe imithwalo yabo bahambe. Wabuye wathi uLembede banmgI okhokho abafa belwela izwe abalinikwa uMdali. 
  Uma kuwukuzonda umlungu ukuqhuba impi yokhokho yena uzimisele ukuthi angabizwa noma ngaliphi igama elisho inzondo yomlungu. Kwaba khona abanye e~tsheni abangakuthandisisanga lokhu. ULembede wayengafuni ukuzwa ukukhuthaza ubudlelwano nezinye izizwe eMzansl Afrika abomdabu bengakhululekile. Wayengenandaba nalabo ababezenzela ubuhlobo kwezenkolo noma ubungani nje obungaphathelene nezombusazwe. Ukuthanda ubuzwe nokukhuthaza okomdabu, yilona vangeli okuyothi uma lingene kahle kuvuke ugqozi lokuzikhulula kwabomdabu. 
Akubhikishwe 
Iziteleka ezimbalwa ezaba khona ngaphambi kuka-1946 zabakhombisa oLembede nozakwabo ukuthi uquqaba Iwabomdabu Iwalungaxhumene nabaholi. ULembede. wakhala ~gokuthi uKhongolose akalufundisi uquqaba futhi akalulolongI ukuze lulungele ukunyakaza uma sekufika isikhathi sokubhikisha nokuteleka. Wazama ukulwa nezindlela ezithathela kude, esho ukuthi ukwazi ngezepolitiki kutholakala kahle uma kukhona okwenziwayo. 
  Phezu kwakho konke lokhu abaholi oXuma noChampion bakaKhongolose bakhuza bathi abantu bangaya kanjani embhikishweni bengaphethe lutho lokuzivik~la.
