intsha, bathi akuzanywe ukuba lezi zinhlangano eZ1S1Za uHulurneni ekucindezeleni abomdabu zingaphurneleli. NgoFebruary ka-1947 uLembede watshela ikornidi enkulu kaKhongolose ukuthi abaholi bakaKhongolose abanaso isibindi ngoba abaJ;itu base belungele ukutshelwa ukuthi benzeni. 
Kula! Luphi udosi lwakho? 
Norna uLembede wayeyiphela endlebeni yataholi bakaKhongolose wayenornfutho, nomqondo owawungarnenza ukuba naye agcine esengurnholi kaKhongolose athole ithuba lokwenza konke ayethi akwenziwa nayekucabanga. Pho-ke, akwenzekanga lokhu ngoba uMdali wabona ukuthi kuhle ashiye urnhlaba masishane zingu 27 Julayi 1947. Vma sibuka singathi isikhathi asebenza ngempela kuso kwezombusazwe kwaba irninyaka ernine. Kulesi sikhashana uLembede wayesesebenze urnsebenzi werninyaka ngoba ayenabo oRobert Sobukwe, Jordan Ngubane, nabanye baqhubeka nomoya wobu-Afrika. Washiya arnazwi abangawakhohlwanga ozakwabo oMda, Sobukwe, Ngubane nabanye. Wabayala bonke abomdabu ngokubatshela arnazwi kaJoseph Mazzini waseNtaliyane owayala abakubo wathi: "Thandani izwe lenu ... Yikhaya aninike lona uMdali ukuba nizikhulise kulo, nizilungisele ukuya kuye. Igama lenu, urnbuso wenu, isibonakaliso kwabanye abantu. Linikeni izwe irnicabango yenu, ukubonisana kwenu, negazi lenu. Lithuthukiseni libe lihle kodwa nibe neqiniso lokuthi nilishiya lingangcoliswanga amanga noma ubugqili kanye nokuhleshulwa." 
  Akekho owayesola ukuthi uLembede uzoshiya urnhlaba ngokuzurna ngoba ezinsukwini ezimbili engakafi abaningi babona ibhungu elijabule kakhulu ernkhosini weYouth League kaKhongolose. Kulo mcirnbi walalela urnculo wekwaya "Philharmonic" owaholwa u-Edward Manyosi ephelezelwa umfokaMphahiele ngopiyane. Kwathi lapho urnculi esho la mazwi; " ... and a soft smile came from the stars and a voice from the whisp'ring foam safe, safe at last the danger past, safe in his father's home. "

.- 
urncirnbi wathi: 
"Kuhle lokhu, sengathi umuntu ungenile eParadise". 
Waphinda futhi okaManyoni ekhaya likaLembede kwa-1500 eOriando lapho zadurna kusihlwa, wahlabelela. Kwathi lapho okaManyosi ehlabelela ethi: "But bright was the starry light that shone on the summer sea."

Wayesebenze izinyanga eziyishurni nanye engurnrneli ozirnele. Ihhovisi lakhe wayeliqashe esizwa urnnurnzane ulsaac Dlhomo.

  Nasenhlanganweni kazwelonke yabafundi basema~vesithi eyaziwa ngokuthi National Union of South African Students (NUSAS) uNkomo waba ungqa phambili ezindabeni eziphathelene nabafundi nobandlululo. 
  Ngo-1943 uNkomo nabanye ababefundela ubudokotela baqala ukuhlangana namalunga amasha kaKhongolose. Kule mihlangano babebhunga ngokusungulwa kophiko lwentsha kuKhongolose (ANC Youth League). Kwathi uma selusungulwa ngempela lolu phiko ekuqaleni kuka-1944 uNkomo wakhethwa ukuba usihlalo wekomidi lesikhashana kusahlelwa izinto ezazidinga ukulungiswa kuze kube khona ukhetho oluphelele ngo-September wawo lowo nyaka. Okhethweni kwaphumelela uAnton Lembede owakhethwa ukuba umongameli wokuqala wophiko lwentsha kuKhongolose. 
  Ngesikhathi esafunda uNkomo wangenwa kakhulu izinkulumo nemibono yeKhomanisi uKarl Max. Kwathi ngokuqhubeka kwesikhathi esesebenza lehla leli lukuluku. Umoya wakhe wathoba kangangoba ngo-1953 wangena enhlanganweni iMoral Rearmament (MRA) ayengeke asondela kuyo ngokomqondo ayenawo esafunda. Le nhIangano yamenzela ithuba lokuba ahambele amazwe amaningi ngaphandle kwaseNingizimu Afrika. Uhamba nje ngomsebenzi wale nhIangano useyilo ilunga likaKhongolose. Ngalesi sikhathi wase eqa1ile ukukhononda ngenqubo kaKhongolose. 
  Kwathi evakashele endaweni yaseGaux ezweni laseSwitzerland ngo-1953 wabeka inkulumo eyagxeka kabanzi uKhongolose. Lesi senzo sabangela ukuba uNelson Mandela abize urnhlangano kaKhongolose eGoli. Kulo mhlangano kwabikwa izinto ezashiwo uNkomo egxeka uKhongolose. Khona manjalo uMandela wamemezela ukuthi uNkomo uxoshiwe kuKhongolose. Ngalesi sikhathi uNkomo wase e'yisikhulu esaziwayo ePitoli iningi limthanda. Ukuxoshwa kwakhe kwadida imiqondo yabantu kwavela izinkulumo 
"eziningi ngodokotela owayenosizo. 
306 
  Ngo-1953 uNkomo wakhetha ukuba ilungu lekomidi yenhlangano yobudlelwane phakathi kwezizwe eNingizimu Afrika (South African Institute of Race Relations). Nalapha wazama ukubeka imibono 'yakhe yokuthi ukuzwana nobudlelwano kungathuthukiswa kanjani. Ngo-1969 wakhethwa ukuba yisekela likaMongameli wale nlUangano. Sekuthi ngoDecember ka-1971, izinyanga ezimbalwa engakafi, wakhethwa ukuba uMongameli wale nhIangano. Waqopha umlando ngokuba owokuqala onsundu ukuphatha lesi sikhundla. 
  UNkomo wayezisekela izinhlangano zodokotela ngoba wayewukhonzile umsebenzi wokwelapha. Wayekholwa ukuthi isizwe esinsundu ngeke siyilwele kahle inkululeko ngemizimba entekenteke. Abantu babemkhonze kakhulu ngesineke sakhe nangekhono lakhe. NgoMarch ka-1972 wafa uNkomo sezwakala isikhala asishiya. 
Okufundiwe  

Makhathini, Rev. Douglas Duma laza'rus 1918 - 1978 
"Thumel' abefundisi Benamandla akho, Balshel' abanlu banke, Izindaba zaKho." 
Umfundisi Makhathini wazalelwa Ongoye Mission Station, zingu-4 kuApril ka-1918. Imfundo yokuqala wayithola khona Ongoye. Uyis~ wasuka waya eOscarsberg eyofundela iBhayibheli ngo-l928. UDouglas naye wahamba noytse wayoqhubeka nemfundo yakhe esikoleni sakwaMondi. Wathi uma eseqedile ukufunda kwaMondi waqhubekela eMphumulo eyokwenza izifundo zaseHigh School. Waqeda lapha wayeseyofundela ubuthisha. Waqala ukufundisa khona kwaMondi ngo-1934. 
  Ngezizathu ezithile washiya phansi ukufundisa ngonyaka ka1940 wayosebenza emayini eGoli (iGroolvlei Prop-mines). Ngenxa yokukhalipha kwakhe wenziwa unobhala orrikhulu wesibhedlela sasenkomponi. Ngo-1943 washiya eGoli wabuyela kwaMondi lapho afundisa khona isikhashana wasekhushulwa waba nguthishanhloko wesikole saseMhlathuzana. Seku'".hi ngo1945 wenziwa uthishanhloko woNgoye Higher Primary School. Ngesikhathi efundisa lapha wafikelwa uthando olukhulu lokufundela ubufundisi. Lwaya ngokuqina lolu thando waze wazinikela ngo-1950 wahamba wayofundela ubufundisi. . 
  Eseqedile ukufunda wabuya wazosebenza kwaMondi kusukela ngo-1956 kuya ku-1957. Emva kwalokhu wawela way~ phesheya eMelika lapho afundela khona iziqu zeB.D. Ekubuyem kwakhe wasebenza phakathi kwesizwe sakwaMthethwa eMbabe. 
308 
  Ngonyaka ka-1960 wangena esekethini laseThe~ini wahlala eMilne Street. Waduma kakhulu ngomsebenzl ayewenza kulesekethe ngesikhathi esifushane efikile. Ngo-19?~ wahanjiswa ukuba ayofundisa ekholishi lokuqeqesha abefundlSl eMphumulo (iMphumulo Theological Colleg~). Ngenxa yekhon~ lakhe ngo-1974 wakhushulelwa esikhundlem sokuba umphathi (Reclor) walo leli kholishi. Wasibamba lesi khundla kwaze kwaba unyaka ka-1977. Phela kwakuqala ngqa ukuba leli kholishi lenganyelwe umuntu womdabu. Naye wasibamba les~ sikhundla ngobukhulu ubuciko wenelisa nalabo ababethi umuntu 
omnyama ngeke aphumelele kulesi sikhundla. 	. 
  Wabuye wahamba futhi ngo-1968 kuya ku-1970 waphindela khona futhi eMelika eyoqhuba izifundo zenkolo. Wabuya eseneziqu ze"Masler of Theology". Wenza imis~~enzi etusekay? emenywa ezindaweni eziningi ukuba ethule lzinkulumo neZlntshumayelo. Wayenesiphiwo sokukh~~a nokushuma~ela: 
Umfundisi Makhathini wayesemakormdim esonto amamngi ezama ukwakha ukuzwana nobumbano phakathi kwesonto lamaLuthela nezinye izinhlelo. Ngo-1977 waya eSwazini eyofundisa khona ezenkolo eyunivesithi yakhona. 
  Ngomhla ka-3 ku-June ngo-1978 washona umfundisi Makhathini washiya inkosikazi nabantwana abangu-8 eshonela khona eSwazini. Isidumbu sakhe sabuyiswa. Wangcwatshwa Ongoye zingu-10 kuJune 1978. Ushonanje usebeke induku ebandla kwezokuloba okaMakhathini. Ungomunye wabahlanganyela ekulobeni incwadi ethi "RELEVANT THEOLOGY FOR AFRICA". Le ncwadi yashicilelwa ngo-1973. Yena waloba isihloko esithi "Black Theology" esingathi phecelezi sithi "Inkolo Yabansundu" . 
  Ekupheleni kwesahluko lapho eloba khona ngobuKhrestu nenkululeko, ukhombisa owakhe umbono uma ethi "Njengomuntu omnyama ngokwami ukub.ona ubuKhrestu bungitshela ukuthi ngikhululekile, bufuna n~uv~~ lokhu. Kodwa ngikhululekile ngempela na? Angenzlwa Ylffi ukuba ngikholwe ukuthi ngikhululekile, kanti akunjalo, ngiyimpahla eboshwe kahle yafakwa kahle eshalofini." 
309  


eyunivesithi yaseFort Hare. Amaqoqo ayekhona mhlazana kwenziwa umcimbi wabasha awazange amkhohlwe umusha owayekhethwe ukukhulumela abasha. Uthi uDr M.B. Zondi, "Thina sasisalalele ukuthi 10 musha uzothini ngoba sigcwele thina maqoqo kugcwele ngisho nabafundisayo kanye nenhloko yeyunivesithi. Izwi lakhe a1izange laqhaqhazela ngisho nalapho esezokhuluma amazwi asethusa lapho ethi, 'Laba belungu basuka phesheya kwelakubo behuluba ngezisu benyonyobela izwe lethu leli asebelithathile thina sesiyizinkedama.''' 
  Noma impilo yakhe kwaba impilo ethulile emva kwalokho amazwi kaSobukwe akhumbuleka mhlazana esungula iqembu elisha lezepolitiki. USobukwe waba ngomunye wabokuqala ukungena eqenjini lentsha kaKhongolose (Youth League) eyasungulwa uPilje (ekhuthazwa uMda) eFort Hare. 
  Wafunda eFort Hare waze waphumelela ukuthola iziqu zikaB.A. ngo-1949. Ngesikhathi efunda eFort Hare wangena shi ezindabeni eziphathelene nabafUndi. Wakhethwa waba umholi wenhlangano yabafundi (Stundents' Representative Council) isikhundla esibucayi emayunivesithi. Wasiphatha okaSobukwe ngokuncomekayo lesi sikhundla, kwathi ngo-1949 wakhethwa ukuba unobhalajikelele we"Youth League". Waqeda. izifundo zakhe washiya eFort Hare. Wafundisa endaweni yaseStanderton eNtilasifali waxoshwa ngoba wasekela umzabalazo we"Defiance Campaign" wabuye wabuyiswa ngo-1954 iyunivesithi yaseWitwatersrand eGoli yamcela ukuba azofundisa khona isiXhosa. Nebala waya khona ngo-1951 eyofundisa abamhlophe. Wasebenza kahle kodwa umoya wakhe ungathokozlle ngokuthi 10 rnsebenzi wamkhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi ubandlululo lumkhinyabeza kanjani umuntu omnyama. Wayekholelwa ukuthi ukuduba (boycott) yisona sikhali sokuzikhulula. 
Wangena kuKhongolose ophikweni lwentsha (Youth League). 
Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi akezwananga nenkambiso kaKhongolose ngoba ethi abamhlophe yibona abacashe ngabaholi bebebeyisa uKhongolose lapho befuna aqonde khona. Kwaba khona ukungezwani okushubile noma inkosi uLuthuli uMongameli kaKhongolose echaza ukuthi labo abamhlophe abangenela ukulwa nabamnyama balungile, phinde akwarnkele 
312 
lokho okaSobukwe. Washo nokusho ukuthi yibo abenza ukuba yephuze ukutholakala inkululeko ngoba balwa impi abangayaziabaphathi mapasi ngakho ubuhlungu bokuboshelwa ipasi ababazi; abaphathi zipesheli ngakho ubuhlungu bokuboshelwa izipesheli ababazi. Ngakho-ke ngeke babe nogqozi lokulwa njengabantu abansundu. Akufanele basho ukuthi uKhongolose kufanele enze lokhu nalokhuya. 
  USobukwe wayekholwa ukuthi abantu abansundu kufanele ukuba bazikhulule bona. Wathi kufanele ukuba bakhululeke emqondweni ukuze babone ukuthi uma behlangana inkululeko ingatholakala masishane. Wachuma 10 mqondo kwabaningi abantu sekuthi ngonyaka ka-1958 yena nabanye abalandeli bahlephuka kuKhongolose baqala iqembu elalibizwa ngokuthi iPan Africanist Congress. Yena uSobukwe waba uMongameli wokuqala wale nhlangano. Ngomhlangano omkhulu (Congress) ka-1959 Ie nhlangano yaqala inabalandeli ababalelwa emakhulwini amathathu (300). Akekho owayazi ukuthi izokhula ingafi noma uHulumeni omhlophe eseyivalile. Lana kwakuyinqophamlando wenhlangano eyayizokwaziwa ihlonishwe umhlaba wonke. 
  Ngonyaka ka-1959 uSobukwe wamenywa ukuba ayofundisa eyunivesithi yaseRhodes eKoloni. Nakhona wayefundisa izilimi zabansundu. Watshelwa ukuthi iholo lakhe Iizolingana nelabamhlophe nokuthi isikhundla sakhe sizofana nesozakwabo abamhlophe. Wasibuka lesi silingo esasizomkhuphula abe ngaphezu kwabaningi abamnyama ahole kahle. Futhi bambalwa kabi abamnyama ababengathola lesi sikhundla. Isimemo sachaza ngokusobala ukuthi uma evuma ukuthatha lesi sikhundla kuhle azi ukuthi lokho kusho ukuthi phansi izindaba zombusazwe. Lokhu nje kwamkhombisa ukuthi kunodobo lokuba azithuthukise yena yedwa akhohlwe umphakathi wakubo. Waphendula masishane wasenqaba isikhundla. 
  Umthetho wokuqala a1wa nawo owamapasL Yena wayekhoIwa ukuthi umAfrika kudingeka ahambe phambili ekulweleni inkululeko - ezinye izizwe ezithanda ukungena zingalandela. Wakhipha isimemo kubo bonke abansundu ukuba ngoMarch 21, 1960 bonke bangawaphathi amapasi kodwa bazinikele 
313 




emahhosivini amaphoyisa aseduze nabo khona bezoboshelwa ukungaphathi amapasi. Akuchazwe lapha ukuthi ngalezo zinsuku umuntu omnyama kwakumele ahIa1e njalo ephethe ipasi noma ngabe uwela umgwaqo wasekhaya .uyothenga isinkwa esitolo esingaphesheya. Ngokusa kukaMarch 21 uSobukwe uqobo wahola iqembu labalandeli elaqonda emaphoyiseni esileshini sase-Orlando eGoli. 
  Endaweni yaseSharpeville eGoli amaphoyisa adedela intululwane yezinhlamvu lapho iqembu elalibhikishela amapasi lalihamba khona. Lapha kwafa abantu abangu-67 ngisho nabesifazane imbala. Lesi senzo sashaqisa urnhlaba wonke kangangoba kunezindawo phesheya ezisalukhumbula ngemithandazo lolu suku. Emva kwale nhIekelele kwakhishwa ikhomishani ukuba ihlolisise lolu daba. Ikhomishani yathola ukuthi amaphoyisa adubula ngoba evikela impilo yawo eyayisengozini. 
  Waboshwa uSobukwe wabekwa icala lokuthi wakliuthaza ukuvukela uHulumeni. Wavalelwa iminyaka emithathu kwathi inhIangano yakhe yeP.A.C yavalwa kanye noKhongolose. Idlanzana labeP.A.C elalizibiza ngokuthi uPoqo lasebenza ngezomshoshaphansi. Kwathi sekuzophela isikhathi sakhe sokuboshwa uSobukwe ngoMay 1963 kwakhiwa umthetho esiwuchaze ekuqaleni kwalo m1ando. La mthetho wagunyaza uHulumeni ukuba alokhu esiqhuba isikhathi sokuboshwa kukaSobukwe. 
  USobukwe wasuswa ejele ePiloli waboshelwa esiqhingini saseRobben Island nabanye abadingiselwa khona ngezepolitiki. Wanikezwa indawo engcono ehlukanisiwe neyezinye iziboshwa ngocingo. Wahlala egadiwe imini nobusuku egadwe onogada abahlanu nababili abahamba nezinja. Wavunyelwa uSobukwe ukuba athenge amaphepha afunde kanye nokufunda izincwadi ezithile. KUthe uma sekubalwa kwatholakala ukuthi uHulumeni wakhokha imali enguR75,000 ukugcina uSobukwe eRobben Island kusukela ku-1963 kuya ku-1969. 
  Ngesikhathi evalelwa eRobben Island abantu babengavunyelwe ukumvakashela ngaphandle kwezihlobo ezisondelene naye. Amalungu ePhalamende nawo ayeke amvakashele nabanye abaholi baphesheya. Abesiphambano esibomvu 
314 
sornhlaba (InternatiolUll Red Cross) nabo badedelwa ukuba bayombona. Esiningi isikhathi wasichitha ngokufunda. Kusasele unyaka engakakhishwa eRobben Island wazuza iziqu zeB.Sc. kwezomnotho (Economics) ayezifundela ngasese nenyuvesi yaseLondon. Waphumelela ukuloba incwadi yesiNgisi kanye neqoqo lezinkondlo zesiXhosa. 
  Abaningi abantu bathokoza ukuzwa isimemezelo esakhishwa umholi wezomthetho (Minister of Justice) umnumzane uPelser. Wathi ememezela ngo-April zingu 25, 1969 uSobukwe uzokhululwa kodwa inkululeko yakhe izoba nezihibe zokuvikela uHulumeni kulo muntu. Nebala isihibe sokuqala sathi uzohamba ayohlala endaweni yaseKimberley. Wathi eshaya umhIaka 30 June wabe esehanjisiwe ehlala kude nasekhaya lakhe. Emva kwezinyanga ezintathu umfowabo, umbhishobhi wase-Anglican eGoli, wenqatshelwa ukuba ayobona umfowabo. 
  Enyangeni ka-April ku-1970 wavunyelwa ukuba angenele ukufundela ubumeli asebenze emahhovisini abameli khona eKimberley. Kwaphela izinyanga ezimbalwa eeele imvume yokuba aharnbe okokuphela eNingizimu Afrika ukuze ayofundisa eYunivesithi yaseWisconsin eMelika lapho ayemenywe khona. Impendulo yathi uHulumeni ngeke amdedele ahambe. Yaba yimbi Ie ndaba kangangoba ngoMarch 1971 umnumzane uTheo Gardener uNgqongqoshe wezangaphandle wasivuma isicelo sokuba uSobukwe ahambe okokuphela. Lapho abaningi besathi kwakuhle lokhu uNgqongqoshe wezomthetho umnumzane uPelzer wathi owakhe umnyango usemvalile uSobukwe ukuba angaphumi eKimberley. Lwabhuntsha kanjalo uharnbo lukaSobukwe. USobukwe nonkosazane uNaidoo bafaka isicelo enkantolo yokwelulela (appeal court) ngodaba lokwenqatshelwa ukuba banikwe imvume yokuphumela ngaphandle kwendawo abavalelwe kuyo. kwama-passport. Wahlala izinsuku eziyisishiyagalombili engadli. Emva kwalo mbhikisho wakhe yedwa akuzwakalanga lutho olubalulekile ngoSobukwe kwaze kwaba inyanga kaJune 1974 lapho avunyelwa khona ukuba ahambe usuku aye eGoli ukuyobona inkosikazi yakhe eyayingaphilile. 
  Ekuqaleni kuka-1975 ngenyanga kaJanuary waqeda izifundo zobumeli kwaphela izinyanga ezimbalwa wavunyelwa ukuya enkantolo njengommeli. Asisho lapha ukuthi umthetho wokumvala wawusamile ekutheni akekho ovunyelwe ukusho noma alobe okwaphuma emlonyeni wakhe. Wathokoza uma evunyelwe ukuba aye emngcwabeni kanina owawuseGraaf Reinet ngo-May 1975. Unina washona eneminyaka engamashumi ayisishiyagalolunye engazange ayibone indodana yakhe. Waqala naye uSobukwe ukwethemba ukuthi izinto zizolokhu zixega kanti akabuzanga elangeni. Isicelo asifaka sokuba ahambe njengesimenywa aye emcimbini wokwamukelwa ngokomthetho uWilliam Tolbert ukuba uNdunankulu waseLiberia, sachithwa. 
  Ekuqaleni kuka-1977 wamangalela abashicileli bamabhuku baseNgilandi ngeeala lokunukubeza. Laba bashicileli bashicilela ibhuku elalotshwa ngumnurnzane uLes de Villiers isekela IikaNobhala womnyango wezokusakaza (Infonnation) eNingizimu Afrika. Isihloko saleli bhuku sithi "South Africa a skunk among nations" okusho ukuthi iyiqaqa phakathi kwamanye amazwe. Ingxenye yebhuku ithi uSobukwe wakhuthaza ukubulawa noma ukuhanjiswa ngendluzula eNingizimu Afrika yazo zonke izizwe ezingezona ezomdabu. USobukwe waphumelela ngamalengisi kuleli eala inkantolo enkulu yaseLondon yamnxephezisa ngoR1,500. 
  Kwadaluleka ngoFebruary ka-1977 imfihlo yokuthi eminyakeni emibili edlule uSobukwe wayevakashelwe isikhulu kwabamnyama eMelika umnurnzane uAndrew Young owaba yisikhulu kuHulumeni waseMelika. Umnurnzane uYoung wayemele izwe lakubo iMelika enhlanganweni yezizwe zomhlaba i-United Nations. Ekhuluma ngoSobukwe umnumzane uYoung wathi. "Kukhona abantu abaqopha umlando. URobert Sobukwe ukulelo qembu." UYoung walungisa ukuba izingane zikaSobukwe ziyofunda eMelika. Kwahamba ababili 
316 
bokuqala indodakazi uMiliswa nendodana uDinilisizwe. Sekuthi ekuqaleni kuka-1978 sekulandela owesithathu kubantwana abane bakaSobukwe. Walandela uDalindyebo wayohlala nabakubo ernzini wakwaYoung e-Atlanta eMelika. 
  Ngalesi sikhathi wayengaphilile kahle uSobukwe ngoba phakathi nonyaka ka-1977 wahlatshwa umkhuhlane abangazange bamelaphe wona odokotela baseKimberley .. Ekup~e~eni kukaJuly walelwa imvume yokuba ayobona ompetha (spec:a!lsts) balesi sifo eGoli. Umnurnzane uBenjamin Pogrund wazama izinsuku efuna ukuthintana nomnurnzane uJimmy Kruger owabe engungqongqoshe wezenhlalakahle. Ekugcineni wamthola wavuma ukuba uSobukwe aye eGoli ukuyobona odokotela. Isivumelwano sathi uSobukwe uyofikela kwaProgrund ngoMgqibelo angayi kwenye indawo ngaphandle kochwepheshe bodokotela.

  Kwathi uma kufika izithombe zeX-ray eGoli zlvela eKimberley ochwepheshe bathola ukuthi udokotela owamhlola eKimberley wathola ukuthi unesifo somdlavuza (cancer). Lokhu akuvumelananga nochwepheshe abathola ukuthi uphethwe yisifosokukhathala kwemisipha yenhliziyo.' Kwenziwa amalungiselelo okuba ayiswe esibhedlela saseGroot Schuur eCape Town. Ngosuku olulandelayo kwafika amaphoyisa ezomoya khona eGroote Schuur ukuze angabi nazo izivakashi ngaphandle komndeni wakhe. Odokotela abakulalelanga lokhu ngoba kungahambisani nenqubo yabo. Baningi abantu abeza esibhedlela bezobona uSobukwe abanye babefika bame bambuke nje bese behamba. Wahlinzwa wakhishwa elinye iphaphu. 
  UProfessor uChris Barnard uchwepheshe"odumile waneenga uNgqongqoshe uKruger ukuba ayeke ukumvala uSobukwe ngoba kukhanya ukuthi ugula kabi. Udokotela owayevamile ukuvakashela uSobukwe embhedeni wakhe afike arnxmdse.

327. 

Udokotela uBarnard wathi ngoSobukwe: 'Okungixakayo kakhulu ngoSobukwe ukuthi urnuntu onjengaye owayefanele ukuba abe nenhliziyo ebuhlungu enenzondo kodwa kwaku-. ngekho nokuncane okwakukhombisa inzondo nobuhlungu benhliziyo.' 

  Sekusele izinsuku eziyishumi nanye adedelwe esibhedlela uSobukwe inkosikazi yakhe yafaka isicelo esiphuthurnayo isibhekise emantshini yaseCape Town. Yacela ukuba athole imvurne yokuhlala nesihlobo sakhe umfundisi uPat Matolengwe nomanomngane wakhe othile owayemhlophe. Wakwenza lokhu khona ezoba seduzane nesibhedlela ahlengeke ekukhahlazekeni indlela ebuyela eKimberley. Akazange ayithola impendulo kwathi ngo-October 12 udaba lwathathwa udokotela uAlex Boraine ilungu lePhalamende. Zingu-15 October wakhishwa esibhedlela wabuye wabuyiswa ngosuku lokuqala ku-November. Wadedelwa isikhashana wabuya futhi zingu 6 January 1978 ezoqhubeka nokwelashwa. Wadedelwa zimbili enyangeni kaFebruary akabe esahlala sikhathi washona ngesonto zingu 27 February 1978. 

  Ukufa kwakhe kwakhunjulwa umhlaba wonke ngemithandazo. Wafa esavaliwe sekungunyaka ka17 avalwa. Asigcine ngokusho lapha ukuthi noma wayekholelwa ekutheni ama Afrika kudingeka azimele odwa ernzabalazweni wenkululeko, kodwa ngeke libe khona icala ukungenisa omhlophe ePhalamende eyenganyelwe abamnyama. 

  Wathi kuyothi urna sekuphele ubandlululo wonke urnuntu eMzansi Afrika uyohlonipha isizwe esisodwa soMzansi Afrika ngoba wonke urnuntu uyobe emunye.
